IDEALOOP CORE
Master Reference Document

Last updated: June 22, 2026 (V89 — EXPLORE MODE — "NO RE-EVAL MIRROR" DECIDED (queue language retired) + THE "FROM HERE" SECTION-4 REDESIGN + TAKE-TO HANDOFF ROUTING & UNSAVED-EXPLORATION LEAVE-GUARD + THE EXPLORE QUALITY PASS (deflator label-DERIVATION + token-leak scrub + crowdedness recalibration + Haiku-2a latency) + THE EXPLORE RESULT-VIEW RE-WEIGHT (the card shows the wall + readiness chip · the Our-read flip · a seed card w/ verdict-style modal · terrain density meters · a next-move callout) — **ALL EXPLORE-MODE: engine-prompt / route / two route-side label-and-scrub passes + frontend; this session touches the EXPLORE OUTPUT CONTRACT `ll2_explore_v1` (two NEW per-angle atoms + code-DERIVED labels) and the Explore frontend, NOT a §3.x DEEP surface; NOT a V9.x amendment** (no §3.x DEEP surface, no Deep score formation, no `lookup[archetype][sub_position]`, no MB selection, no `overall_score`, no Deep scorer schema, no MO `display_score` / override-trace, no score-shape guard; the V5.0 DEEP scoring engine is BYTE-UNCHANGED in scoring terms at `bf09382` + the Arc-7→Arc-12 + LL1 + LL2 + V78 + V80 + V82 + V83 + V84 + V85 + V86 + V87 + V88 commits; **NO Supabase-SCHEMA change** — the take-to / save flow rides existing columns, the leave-guard + graduation use existing state). **WHY THIS TOUCHES NO V9 CONTRACT:** V9 governs the DEEP SCORING discipline. This entire session is Explore-mode — a SEPARATE engine with its own output contract (`ll2_explore_v1`), per V11.17/V11.18. The deflator pass changes how Explore LABELS its own output (code-derived from emitted atoms instead of model-self-reported) and adds two per-angle atoms; the crowdedness recalibration changes the route-owned density classification; both are Explore-contract refinements, not Deep §3 surfaces and not a score. **THE LOAD-BEARING DECISIONS (recorded as session doctrine):** **(1) EXPLORE NEEDS NO RE-EVAL MIRROR — the divergence/measurement split (the session's opening verdict, CONVERGENT across two independent Claude passes = structurally correct per P24).** DeepEvolveView is a DELTA-MEASUREMENT INSTRUMENT — the score is its spine (pressure strip · score-ladder lineage · the six parts attributing an edit to a metric · the freecard interpreting an edit into which metric it moves · the result-side `!`-markers narrating V1→V2). Strip the score and NOTHING structural survives — what's left is an editable idea box + a re-run button, BOTH of which Explore already has (`explore_variation` re-runs the fan; `edit_read` returns to the input with the idea). Deeper: the Explore prompt says variance across runs is EXPECTED AND CORRECT — there is no stable baseline to diff, the variance is DESIGNED IN, a "delta between two fans" is noise not signal. Deep MEASURES; Explore WIDENS. Re-eval-as-delta is DEEP's role in the loop; the boundary crossing (Take to Deep) is exactly where measurement begins. → **The V88 "Evolve mirror, NON-VERDICT" framing is RETIRED from the queue; renamed "Explore re-entry, divergence-shaped, no delta."** **(2) SECTION 4 "FROM HERE" — parent-scoped only, the angle-steer KILLED.** The "exhale" concept carried a stowaway — it had drifted from "the section where the founder ACTS" into "the section where the tool helps them COMMIT." Emre's call: he lists the options and gets out of the way; the narrowing is the founder's move, and a surface pointing at one angle breaks the non-ranking lock. KILLED: the recommendation paragraph / angle-steer (both the button AND the `nextMove.recommendation` prose — "take the PM angle to Deep"). LOCKED: Section 4 acts on the WHOLE idea only — three parent tiles **Save · Explore again · Take to Deep** (open-question CONTEXT above — the unresolved thing handed back, not advice — a pointer line below to the per-angle controls). Per-angle decisions live UNDER each angle card — **save · explore · take to Deep** (compare DROPPED — nothing to compare two rough texts against; explore ADDED). Same vocabulary at both scales, zero duplication. Palette: Save grounded pewter · Explore Dawn `#7aa2ff` · Deep violet `#8a82c2` (lifted to `#9a8fd8` at text size); glyphs family-tree / fan-out / converge-flask. "Nothing is lost" moves from a Section-4 COPY promise to the intact saved FAMILY in the lineage (leans on V87, shown not asserted). **(3) TAKE-TO HANDOFF ROUTING + THE UNSAVED-EXPLORATION LEAVE-GUARD.** The take-to actions were auto-running the paid pipeline; now they pre-fill + route to the matching INPUT screen (angle/parent → Deep input, angle/parent "Explore again" → Explore input, empty-fan "as it stands" → Deep input) so the founder REVIEWS before spending a credit — which is what the Deep tile's "edit the seed first" copy already promised. A `LeaveGuardModal` fires ONLY when the exploration is unsaved (`!savedExploreIdeaId && !viewingFromSaved`) — Save & continue (saves the family, then goes) / Leave anyway / Cancel; applied to "Explore again" too (Emre — cheap insurance against a sad accidental loss). The graduation wrinkle handled: the parent take-to-Deep graduates the rough/explored node IN PLACE, now resolved LIVE at the Deep run via a `pendingGraduateParent` flag (so a "Save & continue" that just created the saved idea graduates the right node, not a stale null), cleared on every run + on cold-open Deep. **(4) THE EXPLORE QUALITY PASS — the deflator / label-DERIVATION contract change (the load-bearing one).** Diagnosed via the FOUNDER'S-EYE PROSE-READ (read all 24 ideas / 101 angles TWICE — the metrics can't tell you if it's useful, only a reader can). Finding: Explore's CONTENT is honest (the disconfirmers name real, strong, current incumbents and talk the founder out of bad ideas; Sections 2 + 3 are the engine) but its LABELS oversold UNIFORMLY (fan_state rich 24/24, branchable 24/24, readiness worth_shaping 90% — the four PLANTED thin edge-cases all came back rich/branchable/worth_shaping). The model was grading its own homework → always an A. THE CURE (Emre's doctrine — CODE OWNS THE LABEL, MODEL OWNS THE ATOMS): the synthesis now emits two NEW per-angle atoms — `disconfirmer_kind` (5-value enum: direct_incumbent_holds / free_substitute_floor / demand_unproven / structural_barrier / closeable_gap) + `demand_evidenced` (bool) — and the route's `applyDerivedLabels()` DETERMINISTICALLY derives all three labels (readiness ← opening.trust × disconfirmer_kind × demand_evidenced; fan_state ← the readiness DISTRIBUTION, replacing the old `angles.length` count; branchability ← reconciled), stashing the model's originals as `_readiness_model` / `_state_model`; a missing kind falls back to the model value (safe-to-ship-alone). The model can't inflate a label it no longer holds the pen on — PHYSICAL SEPARATION again (same lever as Stage 2a re-deriving its density class, and the V9.30 MO `display_score`). Frontend needed ZERO new values — readiness / branchability / fan_state enums (incl. the never-fired `partially_branchable`) already existed in `ExploreView.js`; kept simple at three labels. Re-run (live, NOT frozen — see doctrine): fan_state off 100% rich → 75% thin, readiness spread to ~55% probably_thin, leak 0, the planted edge-cases deflated, baseline_codereview stayed rich (4 distinct wedges). A SECOND prose-read confirmed the deflation is HONEST, NOT over-corrected (every thin idea thin because real incumbents hold the lane). Residual was LENIENCY: `demand_unproven → probably_thin ALWAYS` (drop the trust≠strong escape) shipped as a one-line `deriveReadiness` fix, REPLAY-verified over the captured atoms (6→3 rich; license_resale / voice_journal / hotel → thin), NO re-run needed; a second closeable_gap-on-a-strong-incumbent fix proved UNNECESSARY (voice_journal flips via fix #1) and is DEFERRED (it needs a model re-tag = a run). **(5) TWO MORE BACKEND FIXES IN THE SAME ONE-RUN BUNDLE — token-leak scrub + crowdedness recalibration.** Token-ref leak (`signal_N` / `field_N` / `coverage.*` bleeding into user-facing prose, ~17% of ideas): a synthesis prompt rule + a deterministic route `scrubLeaks` BACKSTOP (deliberately LEAVES `lane_N` / `angle_N` — legitimate structural refs the frontend links on); re-run leak count → 0. Crowdedness recalibration: `classifyDensityLane` was excluding famous-but-URL-less incumbents (CodeRabbit / Otter / Fireflies, surfaced from model knowledge = `llm_generated`) from the "strong" count, so a bloodbath (baseline_codereview) read SPARSE; split into `strongAny` (trust strong, ANY source → drives the count + the ≥50% ratio) + `strongVerified` (strong + not llm_generated → a ≥1 ANCHOR only) — new gate `direct≥2 AND strongAny≥2 AND strongVerified≥1` → flips EXACTLY 2 of 84 lanes (baseline's main lane + meeting's notetaker lane → verified_crowded), no false promotions, error direction now the SAFE one (mildly over-call crowded, never under-call a bloodbath). Plus a one-line `demand_question` null-on-`crowded_with_gap` tightening (GATE #3 → 0). **(6) HAIKU-2a LATENCY + THE OUTPUT-TOKEN DIAGNOSIS.** Explore ran ~2:30–4:00 (a 245s sanity run). The diagnosis: NOT call-count — OUTPUT-TOKEN VOLUME across THREE CHAINED Sonnet calls (Stage 1 ~83–95s / ~4.1–4.7k tok · Stage 2a ~42–46s / ~2.9k · synthesis ~88–96s / ~4.8–5.1k ≈ ~12,800 SERIAL output tokens / ~55 tok/s ≈ ~230s; retrieval is ~1% / 1.7s, parallel). Why same-as-Deep-with-fewer-calls: Deep's 8 calls are SMALLER, PARALLEL (MD/MO/OR/TC fan out), and partly HAIKU; Explore's 3 are huge / chained / all-Sonnet. The lever was never "fewer calls" — it's less OUTPUT + cheaper MODELS per call (the chain can't be parallelized). SHIPPED: Stage 2a → Haiku (`claude-haiku-4-5-20251001`) — a temp-0 structured transform (code already owns its numbers + re-derives density), ~42s → ~21s. Stage 1 is the SHARED SPINE (byte-identical to Deep — "both modes read the same evidence") and STAYS Sonnet; trimming it would touch Deep. Realistic spine-intact floor ≈ ~185–192s; Explore is structurally a ~3-minute operation because the shared Stage-1 evidence is the MOAT — a conscious trade, not a bug. **(7) THE EXPLORE RESULT-VIEW RE-WEIGHT (frontend, BROWSER-CONFIRMED LIVE by Emre; the FanSurface branching-diagram / Dawn-node / lineage-canvas / hover-well design PRESERVED untouched per Emre's lock).** The session made the content honest; the layout still oversold. Four inversions fixed in `ExploreView.js`: **(a) the ANGLE CARD re-weighted (`EssenceCard`)** — both faces now ON the card: The opening (Dawn) + The wall (clay, the disconfirmer), a readiness CHIP top-right (Worth shaping blue / Lightly grounded amber / Ready bright), a `disconfirmer_kind` TAG (Incumbent holds / Free substitute / Demand unproven / Structural wall / Closeable gap); the shift-pill + readiness-pill STACKED vertically (nowrap) to kill the wrap-collision; the redundant concept line dropped to hold card height; the full bet+limit still one click into the "look closer" well. **(b) THE "OUR READ" FLIP (`ReadSurface`)** — `reflection` demoted from hero to a confident UN-DIMMED callout (Dawn-blue left bar, 14.5px, no italic — "treatment A"), the "Still open" questions PROMOTED to the 15px hero (the questions are the product, the playback is the caption); orphaned `ReadColumn` / `ReadyG` / `read.clear` removed. **(c) THE SEED CARD (`SeedSurface`)** — "Your idea" in a Dawn-bordered card with a gradient STEM flowing into Our read, truncated to two sentences with a VERDICT-STYLE MODAL ("View full idea →" → blurred-backdrop centered panel + × close, matching the Deep "THE FULL READ" modal — reached after an inline-toggle attempt + a regex-escape bug, fixed to `/[^.!?]+[.!?]+/g`). **(d) TERRAIN OPTION 2 (`TerrainSurface`)** — the hover-to-read was INVISIBLE; each density zone now gets a count badge (REAL distinct competitor count from `reference_items`), a fill density-METER (proportional to the busiest zone), and card-button LANES with a colored pulse dot + sliding arrow + lift/glow (prefers-reduced-motion respected); the hover-to-read is untouched underneath. **(e)** `firms_up_fastest` ELEVATED from a 13px footer to a bordered "Your next move · cheapest test on the board" callout. **DOCTRINE (worth recording):** (i) the DIVERGENCE/MEASUREMENT split — a re-eval-as-delta screen belongs to the mode that MEASURES (Deep); the mode that WIDENS (Explore) re-enters by re-widening, not by diffing — variance is Explore's feature, so there is no delta to instrument; (ii) CODE OWNS THE LABEL, MODEL OWNS THE ATOMS — a model that stamps its own grade always gives itself an A; derive the grade in code from the atoms it emits and inflation is structurally unreachable (the Explore-side rhyme of the V9.30 "code is the DISPLAY authority, not the SCORE authority"); (iii) READ THE PROSE AS THE USER to judge usefulness — the founder's-eye read of all 24/101 found what every distribution table hid (honest prose under dishonest labels) and walked back a metric over-alarm (the 71% orthogonality lint was shared-connective-word noise); (iv) DON'T IMPORT DEEP REFLEXES INTO EXPLORE — freezing exists to hold a SCALAR steady; Explore has no scalar (variance is expected and correct), so freeze nothing, read the bank as a DISTRIBUTION, let the planted edge-cases be the control (Emre caught Claude importing the Deep freeze reflex); (v) HONEST → LEGIBLE → SYNTHETIC — the Explore arc: deflators made it honest, the card re-weight made it legible, the cross-angle reads would make it synthetic; (vi) OUTPUT TOKENS DOMINATE LATENCY, not call count. **STILL OPEN (recorded for the trail, NOT contract issues):** **(a)** the FAN-READ BAND (MOCKED, NOT BUILT) — the synthesis line above the fan reading the fan's SHAPE (shared-wall when N angles share a `disconfirmer_kind`+`rests_on`; open-lane when a thin fan has one surviving worth_shaping angle; open-fan when genuinely distinct; or nothing). It needs the SELECTOR RULE — the exact condition picking shared-wall vs open-lane vs open-fan vs none from the `disconfirmer_kind` / `rests_on` / readiness atoms — the ONE new backend decision, to be written before the band is built; **(b)** the SYNTHESIS-PROMPT BUNDLE (model-side, one run) — crisp `firms_up_fastest` (a short INSTRUCTION, not a paragraph) + no `angle_N` in that prose + the deferred fix #2 (closeable_gap re-tag when the kill names a strong incumbent); **(c)** the LOOP THREAD ("Since last time" on re-explore — the lightest possible thread carrying how the fan MOVED, NOT a Deep-style walkthrough) — touches the still-held re-explore decision, deliberate "later"; **(d)** DEFERRED LATENCY (spine-bound, after quality locks): the Stage-1 FORK (Explore reads a strict SUBSET of Stage 1 — ~12% token cut, modest, needs a frozen-retrieval EQUIVALENCE GATE: full vs forked Stage 1, diff the competitor name-set / types / weaknesses — the competitor array dominates and can't be cut without degrading the fan), the Stage1+2a MERGE (kills the re-emission, ~40–60s, a real rebuild preserving the code-owns-numbers firewall), the synthesis TRIM (~25s), and STREAMING the four surfaces (perceived-latency — the real "eternity" fix, an architecture change); **(e)** the SAVE-ROUTE IDEMPOTENCY check — an angle saved from its row then the family saved via the Section-4 tile must not double-save under idea-x (a save-route concern, not frontend); **(f)** the carried Deep-side items unchanged — `DELETE /api/folders/[id]`, retire the orphaned `/api/ideas/[id]/set-main`, the inert set-as-main checkbox in `EvaluationView.js`, `onAdvance` wiring, the deferred "story of this idea" narrative, the explore/rough → Deep PROVENANCE-handoff routing + the verdict-lead VIEW-side fallback. **DEPLOY STATE:** the Section-4 / angle-row / take-to-routing / leave-guard work was committed + pushed by Emre (git given); the QUALITY BUNDLE (`src/lib/services/prompt-explore.js` + `src/app/api/analyze-explore/route.js` — Haiku-2a + deflators + scrub + crowdedness + demand_q + the fix-#1 deriver tweak) was RUN-VALIDATED on local dev (the 24-bank re-run produced the results above); the result-view re-weight (`ExploreView.js`) is BROWSER-CONFIRMED LIVE by Emre — confirm the bundle + `ExploreView.js` are committed / deployed to prod. **NOT a V9.x amendment** — Explore-mode engine / route / two route-side passes + frontend; the Deep V5.0 engine byte-unchanged at `bf09382`; `ll2_explore_v1` is REFINED here (two new atoms + code-derived labels + recalibrated density), tracked separately, NOT a §3.x DEEP surface; NO Supabase schema change. **Amendments inventory UNCHANGED at 25** (V9.30 newest, V9.28 authoritative); **V9 still OPEN unchanged.** Closure cascade (3 living docs): MasterReference V88 → V89 (this entry); NarrativeContract V11.29 → V11.30; ActionQueue V31 → V32. Launch-critical path: evidence floor (done) → Explore (engine done; **the Explore RESULT/RE-ENTRY UX now done — no re-eval mirror, Section-4 "From Here" redesigned, take-to routing + leave-guard, the quality pass (deflators + leak-scrub + crowdedness + Haiku-2a), the result-view re-weight at V89; remaining = the fan-read band + selector + the synthesis-prompt bundle + the loop thread + the deferred Explore latency + the save-route idempotency**) → workflow subtraction → dashboard (shell live; both modes have input screens; Deep input FINISHED at V82; Deep RESULTS redesigned at V83; Execution-Brief over-writing FIXED at V84; refresh-resilience + usage gate at V85; Deep OUTPUT PROSE tightened at V86; the MY IDEAS HUB + LINEAGE + ROOT/LEAD decoupled at V87; the Deep "EVOLVE" re-eval + Haiku colour pass + result-screen change walkthrough at V88; the EXPLORE re-entry UX + quality pass + result-view re-weight at V89; remaining = the carried Deep-side deletes + provenance-handoff routing + the verdict-lead view fallback) → M4 security → **M5 PAYG/Paddle (first concrete dependency: a real credit balance — free is a hard lifetime-3 against a stubbed "Get credits" button until it ships)** → launch.)

Last updated: June 22, 2026 (V88 — DEEP "EVOLVE" RE-EVAL INPUT SCREEN + HAIKU IDEA-TEXT COLOUR PASS + RESULT-SCREEN CHANGE WALKTHROUGH — FRONTEND / RE-EVAL-ORCHESTRATOR / HAIKU-DISPLAY-PASS / SONNET-WALKTHROUGH layer — **THE DEEP-MODE "EVOLVE" RE-EVALUATION INPUT SCREEN BUILT FROM SCRATCH (`DeepEvolveView` — a pressure strip [verdict · strongest asset · binding constraint] over a three-column work row [lineage · the editable idea canvas · a per-part X-RAY], with manual part-tagging + fit-to-content lineage + "view full" popups), replacing the pre-Explore shared re-eval screen for Deep) + THE HAIKU IDEA-TEXT COLOUR PASS (at evolve-open a clean-context Haiku display call tags the load-bearing clauses of the founder's idea so the canvas loads PRE-COLOURED — six parts target/problem/mechanism/money/moat/scope, VERBATIM-substring-or-DROP, the founder owns + corrects) + THE RESULT-SCREEN CHANGE WALKTHROUGH (a Sonnet `!`-marker pass that narrates what moved between V1 and V2 per metric)** [ALL frontend / re-eval-orchestration / two NON-SCORING display LLM passes — NO engine / prompt-scoring / score / `_internal` / stage-output change; the V5.0 DEEP scoring engine is BYTE-UNCHANGED in scoring terms at `bf09382` + the Arc-7→Arc-12 + LL1 + LL2 + V78 + V80 + V82 + V83 + V84 + V85 + V86 + V87 commits; `ll2_explore_v1` UNCHANGED; **NO Supabase-SCHEMA change this session** (the two new routes are READ-ONLY — they POST text, return tags / narrative, render; the modified branch / save routes carry the re-eval payload through EXISTING columns); **NOT a V9.x amendment**]. **WHY THIS TOUCHES NO V9 CONTRACT:** V9 governs the SCORING discipline — `.score = lookup[archetype][sub_position]` (V9.28 authoritative), the MO `display_score` decoupling (V9.30), the score-shape guard, scorer-schema stability. This session is the Deep RE-EVAL INTAKE + two presentation passes: the colour pass tags EXISTING idea-text spans for the canvas (it forms no scorer prose field — it highlights the founder's own words), and the walkthrough narrates the ALREADY-committed V1→V2 diff (it reads finished analysis, scores nothing). Neither forms, re-encodes, or reports a score, and neither adds or amends a §3 prose surface. **THE LOAD-BEARING ARCHITECTURE DECISIONS (recorded as session doctrine):** **(i) THE COLOUR PASS IS A CLEAN-CONTEXT ISOLATED CALL — physical separation AGAIN.** The tagging Haiku has nothing in its context asking it to judge / score / widen — it only LOCATES which clause carries each part, so it cannot leak a verdict into the frozen engine; this is the same separation lever as the V4S9–V11 TC isolation, the Stage 2a/2b split, the V11.24 verdict-lead compressor, and the V11.25 Execution-Brief kill, here applied to a DISPLAY tagger. **(ii) VERBATIM-SUBSTRING-OR-DROP IS THE PRECISION FLOOR (offsets too fragile).** The contract is a verbatim quote per part, validated by `indexOf` and DROPPED on miss / non-uniqueness — so a recall-biased prompt (see below) can be generous without risk: a wrong tag is structurally unreachable on the canvas, it can only be dropped. **(iii) BIAS TO INCLUDE — the founder prunes in one click, a missing tag is invisible (human-psychology call, Emre's).** The prompt reaches for all six parts (loosened MOAT to count soft durability — switching costs / owning the workflow / lock-in / accumulation / network density / a compounding loop; sharpened SCOPE to catch the stack/pipeline stated as plain facts; spans the COMPLETE clause to its natural boundary, single-sentence-capped, stop at a topic shift) because removal is cheap and addition is work people don't do — precision held by the verbatim guard, recall raised by the prompt. **WHAT SHIPPED (delivered to `/mnt/user-data/outputs/`, validated `node --check` / `esbuild`-clean; committed + pushed by Emre as ONE commit — 5 modified + 9 new):** **(1) `src/app/DeepEvolveView.js` (NEW) — the Deep "Evolve" re-eval input screen**, a React port of the approved `deep-reeval-final.html` (all CSS `dev-`-prefixed + scoped under `.dev-root`, byte-identical to the mockup): a PRESSURE STRIP (verdict headline/lead + strongest-asset + binding-constraint, each metric-coloured, each with a "view full" popup when truncated) over a WORK ROW [lineage 286px · centre idea canvas · X-RAY 380px]; the editable idea is an imperative `contentEditable` island (`ideaRef`, innerHTML set via effect); manual part-tagging (chipPick / tagPick over the six-part vocabulary target/problem/mechanism/money/moat/scope → metric md/md/or/mo/or/tc); the lineage card fit-to-content (`align-self:flex-start`); the X-ray's "how it's won" is the engine `direction` field (NOT Haiku). **(2) `src/lib/services/ideaParts.js` (NEW)** — canonical PARTS (target_user / use_case / mechanism / defensibility / payment_shape / build_profile), ANCHORS, `partOfField`, and the result-screen METRIC_COLOR palette; the Evolve-screen palette is Emre-locked separately (MD blue / MO green / OR purple / TC yellow). **(3) THE HAIKU COLOUR PASS (3 files):** `src/app/api/ideas/[id]/tag-parts/route.js` (NEW — Haiku `claude-haiku-4-5-20251001`, temp 0, max_tokens 1200; validates known-part + verbatim + present-exactly-once-globally + one-per-part; NON-FATAL, always returns `{ok,tags:[]}`, never blocks the screen) + `src/lib/services/prompt-tag-parts.js` (NEW — `TAG_PARTS_SYSTEM_PROMPT`, bias-to-include + the six parts + the precision guards) + `src/lib/services/tagIdeaHtml.js` (NEW — `buildTaggedIdeaHtml(plainText, tags)`: paragraph-splits, wraps each verbatim quote exactly-once-per-paragraph in a `dev-clz {md|mo|or|tc}` span carrying a `data-part` + a `dev-chip` LABEL, escapes the rest, drops overlaps; empty tags → identical-to-plain HTML). **(4) `src/app/DeepEvolveView.js` colour-pass wiring** — an `ideaLoading` prop: the screen opens INSTANTLY with the idea card BLURRED + "Reading your idea…" while Haiku runs, then SHARPENS to coloured when ready; an `injectedRef`-guarded effect injects plain once during loading and swaps to tagged exactly once when ready, and `contentEditable` is locked during load so the one plain→tagged innerHTML swap cannot eat an edit. **(5) `src/app/page.js` colour-pass orchestration** — `runIdeaTagging(analysisObj, rawIdea, ideaId)` builds an `anatomy` hint from the analysis diagnosis fields (`market_demand.diagnosis` / `originality.differentiation_basis_diagnosis` + `defensibility_diagnosis` / `monetization.diagnosis` / `technical_complexity.base_score_explanation` — all DB-verified present), POSTs `tag-parts`, wraps via `buildTaggedIdeaHtml`, falls back to plain on any failure; fired at the end of `startReEvaluation`; render passes `initialIdeaHtml={taggedIdeaHtml || ideaHtml}` + `ideaLoading={ideaTagging}`; plus the `clip()` prose-fit helper (sentence- then word-boundary truncation feeding the fixed pressure-strip / X-ray cells) and the metricKey SHORT-key bugfix (asset/constraint now pass `md/mo/or/tc`, restoring the MD/MO/OR/TC codes + dot colours + popup spine colour). **(6) THE RESULT-SCREEN CHANGE WALKTHROUGH (the `!`-marker re-eval explainer):** `src/app/ChangeWalkthrough.js` (NEW) + `src/lib/services/changeDiff.js` (NEW, exports `diff`) + `src/lib/services/prompt-reeval-walkthrough.js` (NEW) + `src/app/api/ideas/[id]/re-evaluate-walkthrough/route.js` (NEW — Sonnet `claude-sonnet-4-6`, temp 0, NON-FATAL) + the `!`-markers wired into `DeepResultParts.js` + `EvaluationView.js`; it narrates per-metric what moved between V1 and V2, reading the committed diff, forming no score. **(7) THE COLOUR-PASS PROMPT REFINED TWICE FROM REAL-IDEA TESTING** — a first pass tagged only the 4 loud parts (missed soft moat + the plain-facts scope); rewrite #1 added the bias-to-include spine + loosened moat + sharpened scope; rewrite #2 replaced "smallest span" with "the COMPLETE clause to its natural boundary, single-sentence-capped, stop at a topic shift" so MONEY runs the full pricing statement (model + amount + trajectory + discount), not just the first number — which also keeps a founder's edit to the trajectory INSIDE the span so the span-diff anchors. **DOCTRINE (worth recording):** physical separation beats prompt-rule enforcement AGAIN (the colour pass is an isolated tagger that cannot judge); the verbatim-or-drop guard is the structural precision floor that lets recall be generous safely; "code / frontend is the DISPLAY authority, not the SCORE authority" (the V67–V87 line) extends once more — TWO new generative passes downstream of the engine (a Haiku tagging the founder's own idea-text for display, a Sonnet narrating the committed re-eval diff) are still not score authority. **STILL OPEN (recorded for the trail, NOT contract issues):** (a) the EXPLORE "Evolve" re-eval screen — the mode-specific mirror of this one, NON-VERDICT (no score), pending design; This session is the idea-HUB and its genealogy view: which card the hub shows per family, how the lineage renders and branches, a per-node favorite + disposition flag, and a client-state flicker fix. None of it forms, re-encodes, or reports a score, and none of it touches a §3 Deep interpretation surface — it is the LL3 hub MODEL's display + orchestration layer (the V11.19 / V78 family), extended. **THE LOAD-BEARING DECISION (Emre's call, recorded as the session doctrine) — ROOT and LEAD ARE DECOUPLED:** the hub shows each family by its fixed ROOT (the family's origin identity, which never moves), and "Lead" (`is_main_version`) becomes a VISUAL-ONLY badge that lives in the lineage view and changes nothing about the hub. Before this session the hub picked its per-family card as `members.find(is_main) || root`, so any path that set `is_main` (re-eval, branch, an inline "set as main version" button) could RESHUFFLE which card the hub showed — the observed bug: re-evaluating a deep child "k" made the hub show "k" instead of the family root. The decouple fixes the whole class at the SOURCE, not the symptom: with the hub pinned to root, no caller of `is_main` can reshuffle it, so the bug becomes structurally impossible regardless of who sets the flag. **WHAT SHIPPED (delivered to `/mnt/user-data/outputs/`, validated `node --check` / `esbuild`-clean; committed + pushed by Emre — `LineageView.js` · `api/ideas/[id]/route.js` · `page.js` · `lib/services/ideas.js`; the migration is LIVE):** **(1) THE `lineage_favorite_disposition` MIGRATION (LIVE, additive).** Adds `ideas.is_favorite boolean NOT NULL DEFAULT false` + `ideas.disposition text` (CHECK in {null, 'parked', 'killed'}). `disposition` is DELIBERATELY SEPARATE from `status` (the active/archived soft-delete column) so a parked/killed node STAYS VISIBLE in the lineage — disposition is a user-facing lifecycle label, not a delete. Applied + column-verified via `execute_sql` on `nnuixucsgnjvtwpnxnxz`. **(2) `lib/services/ideas.js` — backend wiring + THE DECOUPLE.** `IDEA_LIGHT_SELECT` widened to carry `is_favorite` + `disposition` (on top of the June-20 hub-redesign widening that added `market_demand_score` / `monetization_score` / `originality_score` / `technical_complexity_score`); `shapeNode` surfaces `changed_dimensions` (jsonb), `is_favorite`, `disposition`; `updateIdea` accepts `is_favorite` / `disposition` AND delegates an `is_main:true` patch to `setMain` (so SET LEAD reuses the existing PATCH route — NO new endpoint); **`listHub` now ALWAYS shapes the family ROOT** (`const root = byId[rootId] || members[0]` — was `members.find(is_main) || byId[rootId]`), the one line that decouples Lead from the hub; the two stale "card = its main" doc comments corrected to "card = its ROOT; Lead is visual-only." **(3) `api/ideas/[id]/route.js` (PATCH) — whitelist widened.** Accepts `is_favorite` (coerced bool), `disposition` (validated null/parked/killed), and `is_main` (ONLY `true`, delegated to `updateIdea`→`setMain`) so the lineage's SET LEAD / favorite / status controls all ride the existing PATCH. **(4) `LineageView.js` (~824→~900) — the full mockup feature pass, drop-in (same props + `onAdvance`).** `fmtChanged` (jsonb-safe); filter + query state; a `bestId` memo (highest-scoring deep node, auto-glow); `toggleFavorite` / `setDisposition` / `setLead` handlers (all through `onUpdateIdea`, optimistic); per-node markers (a CLICKABLE LEAD pill = SET LEAD on hover → LEAD, a BEST pill, a favorite STAR, a KILLED/PARKED tag, a glow ring via `@keyframes ilcGlow`); edge score-delta labels (deep→deep `+1.3 ↗` / `-0.1 →`) + a "what changed" chip; status opacity (killed = greyed); an inspector with a LEAD VERSION tag + a 3-chip status control + delta-vs-parent + churn coaching; a tools row (filter chips All/Explore/Deep/Rough + search). Cause: `setLead`→`onUpdateIdea` (page.js `updateIdea`) does an optimistic `setMyIdeas` that flags the new node `is_main:true` WITHOUT clearing the old lead, so `myIdeas` momentarily holds two mains; the reconcile effect's deps were `[targetIdeaId, myIdeas]`, so that churned array re-fired it and re-derived a dirty (two-LEAD) family until the server lineage re-fetch landed. Fix: drop `myIdeas` from the deps → `[targetIdeaId]` (eslint-disabled with a recorded rationale) — after mount this view OWNS its node state and applies every local mutation (lead / rename / favorite / status / delete) optimistically, so a parent hub-list refresh no longer re-derives it. The lead now jumps once and stays. **(6) `page.js` — SET LEAD made the SINGLE lead-setter.** Removed the inline "★ Set as main version" button (the actual promoter of the original hub-flip bug, it set `is_main` on the currently-viewed idea), the `if (branchSetAsMain)` auto-promote in branch-save, and retired `onSetAsMain` to a no-op (the inert `branchSetAsMain` state kept to avoid an EvaluationView crash). With the hub now root-pinned these removals are belt-and-suspenders for clarity rather than the fix, but they collapse the lead-setters to ONE deliberate control. **(7) THE "MY IDEAS HUB" REDESIGN (the June-20 hub work this entry also records).** `HubView.js` ported to React with a custom hover-preview system on the family cards (replacing the older editorial STRONG/OPEN fields), rendering `listHub`'s `{folders, rough, ideas}` with `family_size`; it never touches `is_main`, so the root-pinned `listHub` is the whole story for what the hub shows. **THE CONSEQUENCE (recorded so it is a known design choice, not a surprise):** a family whose ROOT is an explore (or rough) idea shows in the hub as that explore/rough card EVEN WHEN it has deep branches — the deep work lives one click away in the lineage. This is the literal meaning of "the hub always shows the root"; it is intended (the root is the stable family identity; the lineage is where evolution + the Lead badge live). A future additive "has deep versions" hint on such cards is the clean enhancement if it's ever wanted. **DOCTRINE (worth recording):** physical / STRUCTURAL separation again — pinning the hub to root makes a whole bug-class structurally unreachable instead of patching each caller, the same lever as the engine-side TC isolation / 2a-2b split, here in the orchestrator; and the flicker fix is the client analogue — a focused view should own its state post-mount and not re-derive from a churning parent list. This session generalized it so a reload returns the user to wherever they were. **(a)** A NAV-SAVE effect (gated on `didRestoreRef`) writes `sessionStorage["iv_nav"]` = `{screen, dashView, inputMode, ideaId (currentIdeaId||savedIdeaId||savedExploreIdeaId||roughRoomIdea.id||null), evalId, lineageMode, lineageTargetId, compareMode, compareSel}` on every navigation. **(b)** A RESTORE effect (deps `[authLoading,user]`, also `didRestoreRef`-gated) parses it and self-routes: `?hub=new`/`?view=overview` deep-link wins → fresh-result rehydrate → compare → lineage → a generic IDEA-VIEW restore (`loadSavedIdea(ideaId, evalId)` then re-enter the stored sub-screen results2/brief/delta, with `fetchDelta` re-derived for delta) → dashboard/input direct → Overview fallback; idea-views wait for `user` before firing. New shape: a `dev` plan = UNLIMITED, free = 3 LIFETIME (window dropped). **route.js** (`node --check` clean): EVAL_LIMIT=3 lifetime; `getPlan(userId)` reads `profiles.plan_type`; `UNLIMITED={used:0,remaining:9999,limit:9999,lifetime:true,dev:true,next_reset_time:null}`; GET → dev returns UNLIMITED else a lifetime count (NO window filter) `remaining=3-used`, `next_reset_time:null`; POST → dev returns success WITHOUT recording, else lifetime count + insert. **page.js** (esbuild-clean): client `EVAL_LIMIT` 2→3; the anon `getRecentEvals()` localStorage counter drops the window (lifetime); NEW `evalUnlimited` state set from the mount `syncEvalUsage` GET (`setEvalUnlimited(!!data.dev)`); BOTH usage-text display blocks branch `evalUnlimited ? “Developer — unlimited evaluations” : evalsRemaining<=0 ? “…Get credits…” : “N of 3…”`. **DB (LIVE via MCP):** `update profiles set plan_type='dev' where id=(select id from auth.users where email='emrestr154@gmail.com')` applied (id `baf6710f-4d39-4f3a-ba6e-4828ccde6333`) — live regardless of code deploy. **FLAGGED (real launch dependency):** free is now a HARD lifetime-3 with no reset → a real user who burns 3 hits a DEAD “Get credits” button (there is NO PAYG credit balance in the DB — the button is UI-stubbed), so the CREDIT SYSTEM is the next real dependency before opening signups. Clean future design offered (NOT built): a `credits` int on `profiles` seeded by `on_auth_user_created`, decremented per eval by weight (deep heavier than explore), dev skips it. **(3) THE PRERENDER TDZ BUILD-BREAK FIXED.** A Vercel build failed prerendering `/` with `ReferenceError: Cannot access 'bv' before initialization`. - **Previously: V84 (June 19, 2026) —** (EXECUTION-BRIEF SYSTEM-PROMPT layer (`prompt-execution-brief.js`) — **THE EXECUTION BRIEF OVER-WRITING KILL: per-field prose over-writing on the Screen-3 / step-4 Handoff diagnosed and bound at the prompt — a Block-2 OVER-WRITING KILL fence + hard per-field CAPs + a structural, paraphrase-proof TWO-ELEMENT threshold rule** [PROMPT-ONLY, ONE file (the Execution Brief system prompt consumed by `src/app/api/execution-brief/route.js`, rendered by `ExecutionBriefView.js`); NO route / view / schema / scoring change; the V5.0 DEEP scoring engine is BYTE-UNCHANGED in scoring terms at `bf09382` + the Arc-7→Arc-12 + LL1 + LL2 + V78 + V80 + V82 + V83 commits; `ll2_explore_v1` UNCHANGED; NO Supabase-schema / save / get change; **NOT a V9.x amendment**]. **This CLOSES the Execution-Brief over-length item V83/V26 flagged as the next Deep node ("same length lever as the verdict — a constraint, not a redesign").** V83 fixed the Deep verdict over-length by physical separation (the Haiku compressor); the Handoff had the SAME disease one surface downstream, and the Sonnet 4.5 → 4.6 model switch made it live — 4.6 over-writes into a structure tuned for shorter output. **THE DIAGNOSIS (grounded on a real generated brief of Emre's own ILC idea, then five more across three walls):** the over-length is NOT missing-section, NOT structure, NOT count — the brief obeyed every count cap (right number of steps, risks, signals) but each STRUCTURAL FIELD said its one thing two-to-three times. The disease has a fixed grammar: `[core claim] — [em-dash gloss re-saying the core at finer grain] — [tail: "that is the X the wall requires," "so that Y," "the distinction is exactly what Z depends on"]`. The core is the field; the gloss and the tail are noise. Measured: the `bar` field ran ~83 words (preamble + parenthetical + em-dash aside + a whole second significance sentence); step-2 `action` ~59; stacked resource + close-call clauses ~100 on a single step; `stop_if` ~55 — every one carrying the same three-appendage shape. **WHY NOT THE VERDICT'S FIX:** the verdict needed SEPARATION because two surfaces (card + modal) genuinely wanted two lengths → a Haiku compressor made a second short artifact while `summary` stayed rich. The brief has ONE surface and no rich-version worth preserving — the length is pure bloat, not richness that belongs elsewhere. A compressor would be a second Sonnet pass over six FENCED blocks (no-attack-voice, wall-specificity) — high distortion risk against the exact fences that are the brief's whole value, to delete prose that should never have been generated. And progressive disclosure (the V83 DeepResultParts move) is ALSO wrong here: that collapsed REFERENCE detail; the brief's `produces`/`signal` middle is the LOAD-BEARING ARGUMENT (a step without them "is not a step"), so folding it hides the thing that makes the order ours-not-a-to-do-list. The right lever was the PROMPT — and, critically, NOT a bare word cap (the verdict's failed move). **WHY THE PROMPT CAP BINDS HERE WHERE THE VERDICT'S DIDN'T:** the verdict cap failed on FIELD GRAVITY — twelve rules pulling length into `summary` against one brevity rule. The brief's structural fields have NO such gravity — `action`'s job ("stated plainly") and `produces`' job (an artifact noun) both AGREE with brevity; nothing competes. The length was 4.6's default verbosity, which a named-tell ban + a hard ceiling catches — which is why this stays a constraint and never needed separation. **WHAT SHIPPED (prompt-only, one file, validated across SIX walls — Buyer-access ×2, Technical-build ×2, Distribution ×2 — committed by Emre):** **(1) BLOCK 2 — THE OVER-WRITING KILL fence (the conceptual lever).** Names the fixed disease grammar; states the once-and-stop rule (a structural field states its content ONCE, at one grain, and stops — it never re-says itself at finer resolution and never narrates why it matters; the brief's STRUCTURE carries significance, that is what the section headers / the produces-signal split / the gated order are FOR); bakes in a THREE-WAY ILC calibration verbatim so the cut can't drift generic — `bloated` ("a single-pass scoring pipeline from idea text alone, no live search, no payment layer, no tiered auth — that is the build proof the wall requires") / `right` ("a single-pass scoring pipeline from idea text alone") / `too generic` ("build the core" — object dissolved, the cut went too far): cut to the MIDDLE line, never the third; and sets THE LENGTH ANCHOR — the 4a-4f illustrations are LENGTH models, not only shape models (the illustrated bars / steps / decoys / gates run ten-to-fifteen words, fully wall-specific and fully fenced at that length — proof that tight, specific, and fenced coexist; a field at two-to-three times its section's illustration has over-written, not added rigor). Scoped to the STRUCTURAL fields only — evidence, bar, action, produces, signal, won't-count entries, gate thresholds, the two clauses; the bet and handoff serif lines are exempt (their own one-sentence caps in 4a / 4f). **(2) HARD PER-FIELD CAPs (qualitative → hard, each pointing at the anchor):** 4b — evidence / bar each ONE sentence, no gloss or significance tail, "Enough looks like" is the bar itself not a preamble; 4c — per-field length line (action one sentence; signal one sentence; a firing clause is one sentence, never a paragraph; the pileup ceiling is a LENGTH rule as much as a count rule) and `produces` rewritten to "ONE artifact phrase, no why-it-matters clause" with concrete examples ("a signed pilot agreement," "a pre-launch list of 200 organic opt-ins," "a deployed endpoint that accepts cold input" — artifact phrases, NOT pure noun phrases, NOT explanations); 4d — each won't-count entry ONE sentence, citing the block's own illustration ("a waitlist of 500 is not a pilot") as the length target. **(3) 4e — THE TWO-ELEMENT RULE (structural, paraphrase-proof — the session's sharpest fix).** First attempt was a phrasing-LIST ban (naming "the structural cost keeps climbing," "is irrational given the wall's width," etc.); it bound on the lighter wall but the Distribution `stop_if` slipped it by PARAPHRASING ("the cost of continuing compounds" — semantically identical, lexically clear of the named strings). Replaced with the structural rule: each threshold is EXACTLY two elements — a cost (time / money / attempts) and the unmet bar (the specific evidence that has not landed) — and then it STOPS; there is no third element; after the unmet bar the sentence ends; a third clause, WHATEVER it says (rationale, wall-width restatement, cost-trend, precedent gloss), is the significance tail wearing a decision label — count the elements: cost + unmet bar = two, full stop. Counting clauses catches the paraphrase a phrasing-ban cannot. **★ THE NEGATIVE RESULT (recorded because it is the doctrine's other edge): 4a — the see-saw bet-cadence ban was ADDED, tested across walls, and REVERTED.** Observation across six bets: the model gravitates to two shapes — the see-saw ("[strong axis] is real — the open question is whether [the wall], and the first move tests that") and contrastive-negation ("X isn't the risk, Y is"). A 4a FORM addition named and banned the see-saw; the next regenerations stayed on banned cadences anyway (TC see-saw, Dist contrastive-negation). The reason it can't bind: cadence variety ACROSS briefs is structurally UNENFORCEABLE in a stateless single call — each brief is generated independently with no memory of the last brief's bet, so the model picks the locally-natural shape every time, and the bet's narrow cognitive job (name what's settled, name what's open, point at the first move) converges to a few shapes. And it is USER-INVISIBLE: one user evaluates one idea and sees one bet, which reads well; the sameness exists only for a developer regenerating many briefs and comparing. So the rule was STRIPPED, not kept — a rule that cannot enforce what it claims does not belong in the prompt. 4a FORM is back to its original text. **VALIDATION (six walls, measured):** the catastrophic fields are dead everywhere — `bar` 83w → 47w (−43%), step-2 `action` 59w → 27w (−54%), `stop_if` 55w → 36w; structural fields dropped ~30-50% overall; the named tails are gone from bars / produces / actions / won't-count across all walls. The FAILURE MODE NEVER FIRED — zero generic collapse; the three-way calibration held under three different walls (the TC brief kept sparse-outcome-data pipelines / single-metro directories / the Convoy precedent; the Distribution brief kept freight corridors / broker relationships / carrier density; nothing dissolved to "build the core / get users"). The two-element rule's proof: the Distribution `stop_if` that leaked at 52w under the phrasing-ban came back at 38w with the tail gone under the structural rule — same wall, same idea, structural beat lexical. **THE THROUGH-LINE (worth recording as a reusable pattern, not a one-off):** this is the same lever as TC isolation, the Stage 2a/2b split, and the V83 verdict compressor — STRUCTURAL / SEPARATION DISCIPLINE over PHRASING-LEVEL rules. The over-writing kill names the disease structurally; the two-element rule counts elements instead of banning strings; the removed bet-cadence ban is the negative proof — a phrasing rule that couldn't bind, cut rather than kept. The "over-writing kill" is now a REUSABLE pattern: any other Sonnet 4.6 surface that over-writes gets a structural fence + per-field caps, not a phrasing list. **NOT a V9.x amendment** — the Execution Brief is the §3 Deep interpretation surface at the diagnosis→execution boundary (the Handoff); it is bottleneck-relative and FORBIDDEN from re-scoring (it never receives numeric scores), so nothing about score formation, `lookup`, `overall_score`, the scorer schema, MO `display_score` / override-trace, or the score-shape guard is anywhere near it; the V5.0 scoring engine is byte-unchanged at `bf09382`; `ll2_explore_v1` rendered, not redefined; Supabase + route + view untouched. **Amendments inventory UNCHANGED at 25** (V9.30 newest, V9.28 authoritative); **V9 still OPEN unchanged.** (Scope note: even tighter than V83 — V83 touched prompts + route + frontend; V84 is ONE prompt file, a discipline-tightening of an existing §3 surface, adding no output field and changing no wire contract.) Closure cascade (3 living docs): MasterReference V83 → V84 (this entry); NarrativeContract V11.24 → V11.25; ActionQueue V26 → V27. Launch-critical path: evidence floor (done) → Explore (done) → workflow subtraction → **dashboard (shell live; both modes have input screens; Deep input FINISHED at V82; Deep RESULTS view redesigned + shipped at V83 — verdict-first, progressive disclosure, competition tri-split, close-call gate; the Execution-Brief / Handoff over-writing now FIXED at V84; remaining = provenance-handoff routing + the Evolve (step 5) reality-check)** → M4 security → M5 PAYG/Paddle → launch.)

The real cause: the lineage block AND the compare block are physically NESTED inside the orphaned `currentScreen==="myideas"` flat-hub render block, so once the hub became `"hubpreview"` they were UNREACHABLE — clicking Lineage set `lineageMode` but no top-level guard matched, so `page.js` fell through to its terminal `return null` (a blank body). Diagnosed by mapping the full render-guard dispatch top-to-bottom (the reaffirmed lesson: get the ACTUAL dispatch / error, never guess at a white-screen). **Fix (two lines):** the `myideas` guard now ALSO fires on `(lineageMode && lineageTargetId) || (compareMode && compareData)` — its nested compare/lineage checks return the right overlay BEFORE the flat-hub render — and `hubpreview` yields to both modes (`&& !lineageMode && !compareMode`). The same fix cures the LATENT TWIN bug: the Compare button INSIDE the lineage view (`startComparison` sets `compareMode` without touching `currentScreen`) would have white-screened next. **(7) THE LINEAGE FLICKER:** on load the two sibling cards swapped name/icon for one frame. Cause — `LineageView` paints twice (an optimistic paint from `myIdeas`, then the server reconcile) and the two sources ordered siblings differently, while the layout's sibling sort was a no-op (`sort((a,b)=>0)`) so incoming order leaked through. **Fix (`LineageView.js`):** carry `created_at` into the optimistic nodes (already on the rows) + a deterministic sibling sort in `layoutTree` (chronological by `created_at`, `id` tiebreak) so both paints lay out identically — nothing to swap; bonus, siblings now read oldest-left. Delivered + validated (esbuild + the jsdom render harness); rides the next paste. **FILES (committed + deployed by Emre unless noted):** `src/app/page.js` (nav flip + explore threads 1&2 + reopen + the lineage/compare reachability two-liner), `src/app/api/ideas/save/route.js` (the orphan-rule `parent_idea_id` branching), `src/app/ExploreView.js` (`SaveExploredBar` `viewingFromSaved`), `src/app/api/ideas/[id]/route.js` (`explore_json` on the returned analysis — LIVE from the prior arc), `src/app/LineageView.js` (the sibling-sort flicker fix — delivered + validated this session, paste pending). **THE CUTOVER STILL REMAINS (DEFERRED #2, parts ii–v):** move-to-folder via a `[id]` PATCH; retire the flat `/api/ideas/list` + the flat hub; DROP `status_label`; wire eval writes through the service so new evals get `mode` set. **★ NEW DEFERRED — THE HOIST-BEFORE-DELETE HAZARD:** the lineage + compare overlays are STILL physically nested inside the orphaned `myideas` block; when the cutover deletes that block (DEFERRED #2 iii), they MUST be hoisted to top-level guards FIRST, or this session's exact white screen reproduces. Logged in the ActionQueue. **★ NEW DEFERRED — PRE-LAUNCH PERFORMANCE HARDENING:** the hub loads in ~2–3s in PROD, root-caused to a cross-region network waterfall, NOT a slow query (`listHub` is a single parallel round-trip). Verified facts: Supabase DB = `eu-west-1` (Ireland, confirmed live); Vercel functions default to `iad1` (US-East), so every per-request `getUser` auth round-trip + every DB query crosses the Atlantic, stacked sequentially. Four deferred items, one pre-launch pass: (1) Vercel Function Region colocation → Dublin/Frankfurt (the big FREE lever — and it's FOR the US/EU/CA customer mix, not for Istanbul: a DB-chatty function belongs next to the DATA, so a US customer is *faster* with a Dublin function); (2) local JWT verification replacing the per-request `supabaseAdmin.auth.getUser(token)` round-trip (helps in any region; security-sensitive → cross-review); (3) drop the redundant `/api/ideas/list` fetch on hub open (folds into the cutover); (4) a HubView skeleton (perceived-perf). The honest CEILING: code can't escape the function↔DB distance for the query itself; the region change is the structural fix, and upgrading the Vercel plan does NOT fix it. Logged in the ActionQueue. **NOT a V9.x amendment** — no §3.x DEEP surface / score / scoring schema / Deep stage-output; `ll2_explore_v1` is rendered/persisted, not redefined; the Supabase schema is untouched this session (the V78 additive migration already landed). **Amendments inventory UNCHANGED at 25** (V9.30 newest, V9.28 authoritative); **V9 still OPEN unchanged.** Closure cascade (3 living docs): MasterReference V78 → V79 (this entry); NarrativeContract V11.19 → V11.20; ActionQueue V21 → V22. Launch-critical path: evidence floor (done) → Explore (now COMPLETE — built + integrated + the model finished + the read-back closed) → workflow subtraction → **dashboard (the hub is now LIVE as the default; the cutover tail + the pre-launch perf pass remain)** → M4 security → M5 PAYG/Paddle → launch.)

- **Previously: V76 (June 13, 2026) —** (LL2 — EXPLORE MODE BUILT + VALIDATED ON A 29-IDEA BROAD BANK + THE `branch_idea_text` NEUTRALITY LEAK CURED [NEW MODE — a SEPARATE Explore engine on its own route; the V5.0 DEEP scoring engine is BYTE-UNCHANGED in scoring terms at `bf09382` + the Arc-7→Arc-12 display/reliability/Execution-Brief commits + the LL1 retrieval/display commits; NOT a V9.x amendment — Explore is its own mode with its own output contract, not a §3.x DEEP surface]. **This is launch-list item (2) — the second cognitive mode, the only remaining half of the two-mode split; Deep was already done.** Explore widens a rough idea instead of judging it; it is built ON the LL1 evidence floor and shares the SAME neutral Stage 1 read as Deep (the spine). **ARCHITECTURE (locked):** `keywords (+ gate) → four-source search → buildCompetitorContext → Stage 1 (REUSED, clamped temp0/top_k1/top_p0.1) → Stage 2a-Explore SORTER (NEW, clamped) → Explore synthesis (open) → SSE` — THREE model calls (Stage 1 + sorter + synthesis), far under Deep's eight. **THE STAGE 2a-EXPLORE SORTER IS THE ARCHITECTURAL HEART:** Explore was the lone RAW-EATER of Stage 1 (it consumed verdict-shaped evidence directly, with no shaping layer — Deep has Stage 2a, Explore had nothing), which is the structural root of the run-3 \"non-outwardness\" disease. The sorter is the middle-man Deep had and Explore was missing. It is SORTER-NOT-ANALYST (\"transforms, never generates\" — it RE-SHAPES existing Stage 1 facts and never holds a verdict to corrupt, which is exactly what keeps it spine-safe; it does NOT widen coverage, because coverage-widening would owe Deep re-verification). The intellectual core is the DUAL-FACE insight: Deep needs only a fact's cap-face; Explore needs BOTH the opening-face AND the limiting-face of each fact (a competitor's weakness is an opening AND, if direct+strong, a wall). **FILES (3, built + validated + committed + pushed by Emre this session; SHA not recorded here; run-proven on the local dev pipeline, NOT yet prod-verified):** NEW `src/lib/services/prompt-stage2a-explore.js` (the sorter — `outward_signals[]` {opening/adjacency/unmet_job/barrier, full provenance, `opening_face` + nullable-to-emit `limiting_face`, trust}, `density_reads[]` {lanes, members ≤5, categorical `classification` verified_crowded/emerging_unverified/mixed/sparse — NO number}, `coverage` {`evidence_limit`}); NEW `src/app/api/analyze-explore/route.js` (wire-up; inlined helpers `computeExploreEvidenceCounts` + `classifyDensityLane` — the route OWNS the classification THRESHOLD, not just counts: sparse if <2 members; verified_crowded/mixed only with a real core ≥2 direct AND ≥2 strong-real; else emerging_unverified — and it DETERMINISTICALLY OVERWRITES each `density_read.classification`, so a soft model majority can't bury a real core and can't manufacture \"crowded\" from thin/llm evidence); `src/lib/services/prompt-explore.js` (synthesis — reads the SORTED object, with the load-bearing instruction that trust-weighting + crowd-vs-unverified are ALREADY DONE upstream, do not re-derive). Runner / case bank / run artifacts deliberately LOCAL-ONLY / gitignored per convention. **FOUR FIXED SURFACES (the facet band was KILLED twice on real data — do NOT reintroduce facet_tags):** Read (idea reflection + branchability) · Angles (0–5 directions: opening + bet + disconfirmer + readiness + branch_idea_text) · Terrain (lanes) · Next Move (dominant_uncertainty + recommendation). **THE RUN THAT EARNED THE ARCHITECTURE — broad-bank probe, 29 live ideas, recomputed from raw, split by the sorter's OWN classification:** the run-3 non-outwardness disease (dominant_uncertainty = `differentiation` 68% even on empty niches) is CURED. The thesis test (`classification × dominant_uncertainty`): `verified_crowded` 16/19 → differentiation (correct + expected — a proven-crowded field's open question IS how you differ); `emerging_unverified` only 1/10 → differentiation (9/10 ESCAPED to demand/buyer/etc.). The lone \"exception\" (foodtruck-spot) is the RUNNER's lane-counting metric being cruder than the engine — its core lane is genuinely verified_crowded and the synthesis read it right. Cleanest proof = `couples-habits`: names direct competitors in EVERY disconfirmer yet headlines DEMAND, because the sorter read those competitors as UNVERIFIED — the old flatten (\"competitors exist → differentiate\") would have gotten it wrong; the new chain (\"competitors exist but unproven → does anyone want this?\") got it right. **`differentiation` is now CONCENTRATED where it belongs and ABSENT where it was the disease.** Open-space prose reads as an honest two-sided FORK (\"open because underserved, or open because unwanted?\"), not a shrug; vague input refuses cleanly (`life-easier` → not_branchable). **THE FIX SHIPPED THIS SESSION — the `branch_idea_text` neutrality leak (spine-critical):** the broad run surfaced ONE spine-critical leak (`farm-to-neighbor`'s `branch_idea_text` carried \"underserved geographic regions\" — the text Deep ingests COLD, pre-loaded with a demand verdict) plus 3 user-facing-prose tone-creep instances (DU text + recommendation). The DURABLE fix is STRUCTURAL, not a word-ban (geography is only the first costume — demographic / vertical / platform expansion all smuggle the same verdict): `prompt-explore.js` tightened so an expansion-shaped `branch_idea_text` NAMES its target (region / group / vertical / platform) as a fact and NEVER characterizes that target's openness, coverage, or demand — \"the shift is WHERE or WHO, never WHY it is open\" — plus a cheap word-guard (underserved/untapped/unmet/uncovered/overlooked/neglected). The leak PROBE was WIDENED (`route-explore.js` `buildValidation`): `branch_idea_text` stays a spine-critical `leak_candidate`; `dominant_uncertainty.text` + `recommendation` are now scanned into `warnings` (the tone surfaces the old probe was blind to), with confirm-by-eye fork-vs-assertion guidance. A 3-idea confirm re-run came back GATE-#1-clean (farm-to-neighbor's `branch_idea_text` no longer leaks) and the SAME-SHAPED geographic-expansion angle (`ballot-plainlang`) SURVIVED with its verdict-framing replaced by a factual target descriptor — evidence the structural rule, not luck, did the work. **WATCH-ITEMS CARRIED (NOT pre-emptively patched, per P7 / calibration-first):** `mechanism_shift` angle-SHAPE monotony (42% of angles overall, 47% in crowded ideas — the \"incumbent has limit Y → remove Y\" skeleton; the one templating surface that survived the band's death, now measured for the first time → the NAMED read-for target on the next prose pass, NOT a footnote); readiness middle-collapse (69% `worth_shaping`); `retrieval_condition` is a dead signal (adequate 100% — drop it or move the threshold to the per-lane classification where the real signal lives); fan `thin` 55% is honest conservatism on a crowded-heavy bank, NOT starvation (a UI-expectations point for the frontend — Explore returns a MODEST fan, not the wide-bloom the mockups implied). **DOCTRINE:** physical separation beats prompt rules, AGAIN (the sorter is structural, the calibration-only fix was correctly rejected); "Close to determinism" is an OVER-CLAIM to retire — determinism is structurally unavailable to anyone judging ideas; success lives in execution. · **The number is the reality-anchor, NOT the thing to soften.** V5.0 computes `score = lookup[archetype][sub_position]` from predicate commitments, each carrying `evidence_cited` + a `not_higher` reason. Keep all numbers at full resolution; the only failure mode is the NAKED NUMBER (a score with no handle beside it). The antidote already exists in `_internal` — the `not_higher` chain IS the handle ("here's exactly what would move it") — it is merely unsurfaced. · **EXECUTION BRIEF is Deep-ONLY by structural necessity** (it is the consequence of a settled verdict; Explore has no verdict to be the consequence of). Explore's counterpart is NOT a brief and NOT empty — it is the LOOP-BACK / "next move" surface (save / explore / take-to-Deep), which also carries Explore's emotional-landing duty since no brief comes later to do it. · **Explore = reverse-engineer Deep as NEGATIVE SPACE, not a template:** Deep narrows / Explore widens; Deep prosecutes the idea / Explore thinks with the user; Deep treats uncertainty as risk / Explore as possibility. Explore surfaces (interpret / expand / orient, NEVER judge): The Read · Angles (light evidence folded in) · The Open Lane · Next Move. Selection pressure expressed as ONE coarse readiness signal per branch — NEVER a 5-axis rubric (that rebuilds Deep's verdict instrument inside Explore). Object model: **Idea → Angle → Branch → Evaluation → Decision**; the branch object is the API between the two engines and is owned by the frozen Deep side. **LAUNCH LIST (locked this session — four items; everything else explicitly NOT priority):** (1) **evidence-layer upgrade**, (2) **Explore mode** (the only remaining half of the two-mode split — Deep is done), (3) **workflow features upgraded for the new ILC** (mostly SUBTRACTION — open features to all, retire the 3-state subscriber gating), (4) **build the dashboard**.
