- **Previously: V69 (June 05, 2026) —** (ARC 9 — V5.12 F4 RELIABILITY LAYER SHIPPED [retry-once on transient stage failures + honest Stage 2c degrade; FAILURE-HANDLING + DISPLAY only — no engine/prompt/score/_internal/stage-output change; NOT a V9.x amendment]. This is the F4 + F13 portion of ActionQueue item L16 (Bundle 5); the two gate sub-items (`G_FREE_THIN_DIMENSIONS`, `S_OR_ACTIONABILITY_HOOK`) were DROPPED per Emre's no-gate-work decision (S_OR_ACTIONABILITY_HOOK was already gate-suite-delegated per V5.4; G_FREE_THIN_DIMENSIONS is Free-scoped / FPIR-deferred), and item M10 (pre-launch B10a gate-config audit checklist) was DROPPED for the same reason (gate work; also low-relevance since no launch-gating B10a is planned). **The reframe:** F4's original pre-V5.0 3-tier Partial-State taxonomy (`partial`/`degraded`/`failed`) is over-built for V5.0 — the MD/MO/OR scores are load-bearing, so there is no meaningful PARTIAL state; it collapses to TWO real states — DEGRADED (Stage 2c synthesis missing, scores intact) and FAILED (everything else, which already worked as a hard error + stream close). Net-new = **(A)** mark the degrade honestly + **(B)** transient-retry resilience. **Files (3, committed + pushed by Emre):** `src/app/api/analyze-pro/route.js` + `src/app/EvaluationView.js` + `src/app/page.js`. **B — retry:** a `callWithRetry(callConfig, label)` wrapper around ALL EIGHT model calls (Stage 1, 2a, TC, MD, MO, OR, 2c, 3); on a transient throw it emits a calm NON-ERROR `retry` SSE event, waits a 1.2s backoff (`RETRY_BACKOFF_MS`), and makes ONE second attempt; a second throw propagates UNCHANGED to the existing per-stage / outer error path, so genuine double-failures surface exactly as before. It wraps the model CALL only — it does NOT retry JSON-parse failures (at temp 0 a re-call reproduces the same malformed output; parse handling untouched). Before this, ANY transient blip (timeout / 5xx / rate-limit / reset) on any of the 8 calls discarded the whole ~80s / paid evaluation with a single generic \"Analysis failed.\" **B+ — the notice:** `page.js` gains a `retry` branch in the SSE consumer (`analyzeWithStream`, the SINGLE shared reader used by both first-eval and re-eval, confirmed by source-read) that renders the notice as a calm in-progress line in the live pipeline panel — kept DISTINCT from `error` (which throws and aborts the run), since routing it through the error branch would kill the very run it is reassuring about; it resolves to a checkmark in the final completion sweep. **A — honest degrade:** the Stage 2c degrade is tracked in a LOCAL `synthesisDegraded` through the 2c try/catch and applied to `ev.synthesis_degraded` ONLY at final assembly (beside `overall_score` / `display_score` / `_internal` restore) — so Stage 3's input is BYTE-IDENTICAL to the pre-F4 pipeline (summary + failure_risks legitimately stay on `ev` where Stage 3 reads them; only the presentational flag is held back from Stage 3's input, mirroring the `_internal` / `thin_dimensions` strip-then-restore discipline). `EvaluationView.js` renders an honest \"we couldn't generate the summary; your scores are complete\" note instead of a blank Summary box, triggered on the flag OR an empty summary, `typeof === \"string\"` guarded so it degrades gracefully on saved analyses from before the flag and never calls `.trim()` on a non-string. **Test scaffolding (LOCAL-ONLY, gitignored — `/run-f4-*.js`, `/verify-*.mjs`, `/mock-*.mjs`, `/analyze-*.mjs` added root-anchored to .gitignore):** a NODE_ENV-gated `_test_fault` request directive (STRUCTURALLY INERT in production — `NODE_ENV === \"production\"` ⟹ `testFault` null ⟹ all four `TEST_*` flags false ⟹ every injection point dead, same safety model as fixture mode) drives the harness without a real outage or a server restart; `verify-retry-logic.mjs` (zero-dependency unit test of the exact injection logic) + `run-f4-failure-harness-http.js` (drives baseline / retry_recover / retry_fatal / degrade_2c against the live dev pipeline). **VERIFIED by Emre on the live dev pipeline: verify-retry-logic ALL-PASS + harness 4/4** — baseline ran the full real pipeline clean (0 retries, not degraded → hooks inert when untriggered); retry_recover showed the retry line after `stage1_start` then recovered and completed; retry_fatal hit `retry → error` with no complete (double-fail path unchanged); degrade_2c completed with `synthesis_degraded === true` + empty summary. **The one honest limit:** forcing a synthetic throw proves the RECOVERY logic; it does NOT prove a real Anthropic 5xx throws in the exact caught shape — the SDK does reject on those (so the `catch` catches), but that final 5% certainty arrives only the first time production logs a real retry-and-recover. **Operational notes (not code):** the retry adds up to ~1.2s + one extra call per stumble (~10s + 8 extra calls in the pathological all-fail case) — confirm Vercel `maxDuration` has headroom over the already-long ~80-110s pipeline; and the retry catches errors/rejections, NOT an indefinite HANG (a hang still rides the platform timeout as today). **Doctrine extended:** the failure-handling layer is SEPARATE from the engine — reliability work touches orchestration (retry) + display (the honest note), never score / prompt / `_internal` / stage-output. This carries V67's \"code is the DISPLAY authority, not the SCORE authority\" and V68's \"the frontend is the presentation authority, not the score authority\" one step further: orchestration reliability is ALSO not score authority. **Production engine UNCHANGED in scoring terms** (still `bf09382` + the Arc-7 `scoring.js`/`route.js` display/12b commits + the Arc-8 frontend commit); this F4 commit adds failure-handling + display only. **V9 STILL OPEN, amendments inventory UNCHANGED at 25** (V9.30 newest, V9.28 authoritative) — F4 is failure-handling + display, not a contract change. **Closure cascade (3 living docs):** MasterReference V68 → V69 (this entry); NarrativeContract V11.9 → V11.10 (F4 recorded; explicitly NOT a V9.x amendment); ActionQueue V11 → V12 (Arc 9 + L16 F4/F13 DONE + gate sub-items & M10 DROPPED). Launch-critical path unchanged: M4 security → M5 Paddle.)

- **Previously: V68 (June 04, 2026) —** (V68, ARC 8 — V5.11 EVALUATION-VIEW PERCEPTION LAYER SHIPPED [pure DISPLAY; no engine/prompt/score change; NOT a V9.x amendment]. This is the V5.11 frontend item Arc 7 flagged as "the next build" — the three-metric perception layer that makes the honest scores read well. It renders only what the engine already commits; doctrine = V67's "code is the DISPLAY authority, not the SCORE authority" carried one layer up to the presentation surface. **Files (3, committed + pushed by Emre, Vercel auto-deploy):** NEW `src/app/MetricProseDetail.js` (~200 lines, self-contained) + edited `src/app/EvaluationView.js` + edited `src/app/components.js`. (NOTE: these UI files live under `src/app/`, not `src/components/`.) **What `MetricProseDetail.js` does:** splits each metric's prose into labelled question/answer pairs, every answer a committed raw prose field mapped **1:1** — nothing invented, the component never generates or paraphrases, it only routes which committed field sits under which question label (the question labels are the only added text). `QUESTION_SETS`: MD/MO three questions `[diagnosis, binding_*_explanation, direction]`, OR four `[differentiation_basis_diagnosis, defensibility_diagnosis, binding_constraint_explanation, direction]`. A `canSplit` gate renders the split ONLY when all raw fields are present, else falls back to the single joined `.explanation` verbatim — so it shows the real per-field prose or the real joined prose, never a fabricated fill. **Per-metric header features (each a pure render of a committed field):** MD demand-type ladder (`_internal.demand_archetype` → 7-tier label, always on); MO capture-case name (`_internal.monetization_archetype` → label, always on) PLUS a conditional movement box folding into the same bordered box only when `display_score` is a number AND ≠ `score` (surfaces the V9.30 MO fine `display_score ?? score`); OR primary-exposure line (`_internal.binding_constraint.primary_subtype` → phrase) + inline neutral SVG shield (the app uses emoji section icons / no icon lib, so the line-shield is hand-drawn SVG; the earlier "generic-ai" variant tail removed per Emre). **Colour discipline LOCKED (the load-bearing fix):** the band colour from `getScoreColor` reaches ONLY the score pill — labels (`t.text` 600), answers (`t.sec`), arrows (`t.mut`), the MD ladder, the MO numbers, and the OR exposure phrase are all neutral. A live OR 1.9 (red band) had turned the entire metric section red and read as a rejection; confining colour to the pill restores Emre's original "blue/yellow reflect only the scores" rule. **`EvaluationView.js`:** the single shared prose Card became ONE card per metric (MD, MO, OR each its own) + a separate TC card carrying the "EXECUTION CONTEXT · NOT IN THE OVERALL" divider (TC keeps its existing `renderProseSection` + `getTcColor`, gated branch preserved). **`components.js` tokens:** page `bg: "#0a0d13"` (the "Seamless" navy Emre picked from three mocked options), cards `surface: "#0e1117"`; `getScoreColor`/`getTcColor` unchanged. **Free vs Pro:** the rich design is a PRO feature — Pro `route.js` retains the raw prose fields after `joinProse`, restores `_internal` at final assembly, and sets MO `display_score` at final assembly, so the Pro payload carries everything the component reads; the Free single-call pipeline emits none of it, so the component degrades cleanly to one joined paragraph with no header features. **Resolves the V9.28-deferred OR four-field UX caveat** (the multi-field renderer is now built — for OR and also MD/MO). **Cross-review:** second-Claude (pasted by Emre) endorsed the always-on MO "Capture case · [label]" from `monetization_archetype` (the missing NAME half MD/OR already had; spine intact since it's a name not a second ladder; the fine number stays conditional on movement); Claude diverged on ONE label, rejecting "Proven willingness to pay" for `direct_precedent_grounded` as overstating the rung → "Comparable priced precedent." **Open / deferred:** the question LABELS are Claude's framing of each field (content untouched — a labelling concern to eyeball, not invented prose); `MO_ARCHETYPES` + MD-label microcopy is PROVISIONAL pending a native-English pass; Free-pipeline parity (emit raw fields / `_internal` / `display_score`) is separate later work; carrying the header-feature treatment to hub/compare is FROZEN this session; `surfAlt`/`headerBg` may need navy alignment; confirm the save path persists `display_score` + raw fields on saved analyses. **Doctrine reaffirmed:** pure display — no score/prompt/pipeline touch; reads committed fields and degrades where absent; honest-equivalence stays visibly equal (no manufactured distinction). **Production engine unchanged** from V67 (`bf09382` + the display/12b commits); the three frontend files are the only new ship. **V9 STILL OPEN, amendments inventory UNCHANGED at 25** — V5.11 is perception-layer, not a contract change. **Closure cascade (3 living docs):** MasterReference V67 → V68 (this entry); NarrativeContract V11.8 → V11.9 (perception layer recorded; explicitly NOT a V9.x amendment); ActionQueue V10 → V11 (Arc 8 + item 12d V5.11 marked DONE). The explain-feature (M2) + its preconditions (12b done, 12a parked) remain deferred; launch-critical path unchanged: M4 security → M5 Paddle.)

- **Previously: V67 (June 04, 2026) — ARC 7 — CODE-SIDE SCORING EXECUTED: MO fine DISPLAY score SHIPPED + 12b SHIPPED; full code-canonical migration RED; MD/OR display DECLINED; 12a PARKED. This session built the V5.10 code-side path V66/Arc 6 only identified, and let the run data settle every open per-metric question. **MO fine DISPLAY score → SHIPPED** (`src/lib/services/scoring.js` `computeMoDisplayScore`/`computeMoScoreDiagnostic` + one assembly-line injection in `src/app/api/analyze-pro/route.js`; both committed + pushed by Emre). Decoupled exactly as V66 specified: `.score` stays the robust 3-anchor coarse value — confirmed by source-read that Stage 2c band gates key only off `overall_score` (5.0/6.5) and Stage 3 keys off TC bands + a per-metric `MD/MO<5.0` modifier, ALL reading `.score` — while `display_score` is a code-computed finer value rendered `display_score ?? score`, entirely out of the feedback loops. A CONSISTENCY GUARD falls back to coarse whenever code's recomputed bucket disagrees with the model's declared `sub_position`. Empirics on the clean june328 baseline (26 MO cases): fallback 38.5% (all guard_mismatch), max delta 0.6, crosses_5 = 0, distinct scores 9→13 (+4 — the 6.0 and 5.4 piles genuinely spread). **Full code-CANONICAL migration (code owns the canonical `.score`) → investigated → structural RED, do not pursue.** Two independent reasons: (1) the model's declared bucket and its committed SP-sum genuinely disagree on ~27% of cases, and the disagreement is NOT rule-shaped — identical committed (SP-B, mechanism, strength) signatures land in different buckets, because the model applies a binding-constraint pull toward lower beyond the strict PRIORITY_PULL trigger; making code canonical would override that judgment by fiat and INFLATE the exact anti-inflation cases that are the product's moat; (2) a rerun-stability test (rfull, 15 multi-run cases) showed 13/15 reruns MOVED the MO bucket with the packet VARYING 15/15 — MO's run-to-run variance is dominated by **upstream Stage 2a packet divergence**, which code cannot touch (code computes from SP values, which track the packet), so migration buys ZERO stability. That movement is the accepted explain-the-difference evidence-tracking, not scorer noise — proven on CON-MO-B (5.4→5.4→6.0 because run-3's packet surfaced broader competitor corroboration → SP-C narrow→broad → sum 1→4 → middle). **Verdict LOCKED: the model keeps scoring authority; code is the DISPLAY authority only, adding fine resolution solely where evidence + arithmetic agree.** So "move scoring to code" resolves to "add fine DISPLAY where evidence + arithmetic agree," NOT "make code the score authority" — because bucket placement contains judgment, not just arithmetic. **MD + OR code-side display → evaluated → DECLINED (not built).** A within-cluster sum-spread check across all three metrics (rfull) showed the trick delivers only where the compressed cluster's `sub_position_sum` VARIES: MO's A4-middle (10 cases) varies [3,4,3,4…] → the +4 win; MD's A4 wall (18 cases) is ALL sum=2 → interpolation inert exactly where the compression is (resolution is multi-dimensional → PROSE, already locked V66); OR's dominant cluster (16 cases `no_defensibility_component`/lower) is ALL sum=−1 honest-equivalence → spreading would manufacture false distinction. The mechanism self-protects (constant-sum cluster → all map to one fine value → cannot fake precision), so it is safe-but-pointless on MD/OR — confirming the per-metric asymmetry one final way: each metric's resolution lives somewhere different (MO sum / MD multi-dimensional shape→prose / OR honestly flat). **The per-metric display answer is NOT a template to copy — it is the specific answer for the one metric (MO) whose resolution is sum-shaped.** **12b (V5.9) → SHIPPED:** the two MO bucket overrides (PRIORITY_PULL + GLOBAL_SP_CAP) factored into a single-source `computeMoOverrideTrace(mo)` in `scoring.js` (consumed by both the display score and the trace, so they cannot drift); `route.js` writes explicit `_internal.override_applied {rule, arithmetic_bucket, final_bucket, trigger}` (or `null`) at assembly; computed from committed SP values only — it does NOT read or rewrite the model's declared `sub_position` (no silent relabeling, since the explain-feature must see the mechanism); downstream reads `effective_bucket = override_applied?.final_bucket ?? sub_position`. Verified 17/17 display regression + 8/8 trace tests. **Finding:** GLOBAL_SP_CAP is arithmetically UNREACHABLE (spA≤1 ⟹ max sum 1+1+2=4=middle, never upper), so PRIORITY_PULL is the only override that ever fires; it fired 0× across the 26+49-case runs (rare; the 2/204 defect cells were the larger June 2 audit) = a low-incidence traceability guarantee (`null` on almost every case; live-verify a real override case when one occurs). Unblocks the V5.3(b) follow-up (replace the `G_ARITH_LOOKUP` REVIEW carve-out with a mechanical read of `_internal.override_applied`). **12a (V5.8) → PARKED (explicit decision):** the real fix (MD always emits a complete `_internal`) can only live in the model/prompt — the fragile prompt-nudge class V66/Arc 6 built and reverted; code CANNOT reconstruct the missing substance (SP `level`/`value`s + `binding_friction` are committed judgment, not derivable from the score; and three MD anchor values — 4.5, 5.0, 7.5 — collide across archetypes, so even the skeleton inverse is ambiguous). The most code can honestly do is a graceful-guarantee (structural `_internal` always present, `predicate_commitments` flagged `unavailable` where unrecoverable) so `G_INTERNAL_PRESENCE` passes and no consumer crashes — explicitly NOT "the explain-feature now works on those cases." It pays off only once the explain-difference feature (M2) is built, which is deferred. **Open question banked for that session:** why MD's miss-rate is ~4% while MO/OR were 0 here (should be 0); working hypothesis UNCONFIRMED (MD's `_internal` is the heaviest of the three → truncated under output pressure; alternative: a specific MD branch emits a score without the full struct) — diagnose the root cause WHEN the receipt is actually needed. **THE DOCTRINE (P29-in-practice):** the model commits the monetization judgment (archetype + SP levels) and the prose; CODE computes the user-facing FINE score only where the evidence and the arithmetic agree, and otherwise falls back to the model's coarse score; the stable pipeline keeps using the coarse `.score`. This is the realized fine+traceable corner of the design triangle — but BOUNDED: code is the display authority, not the score authority, because the score itself (bucket placement) carries judgment the arithmetic doesn't capture. **Engine code SHIPPED this session — the first deliberate prompt→code scoring move** (`scoring.js` + `route.js` display + 12b commits). No prompt changed; `.score` and all downstream behavior provably unchanged. **Production engine = `bf09382` + the two display/12b commits.** **Closure cascade (3 living docs):** MasterReference V66 → V67 (this entry); NarrativeContract V11.7 → V11.8 (record the per-metric resolution doctrine + 12b shipped + the bounded "code = display authority, not score authority" line); ActionQueue V9 → V10 (done — Arc 7 + 12b DONE + 12c PARTIALLY DONE + 12a PARKED + new frontend item V5.11). The next build is the V5.11 three-metric frontend perception layer; the explain-feature (M2) + its now-half-met preconditions (12b done, 12a parked) remain deferred. Launch-critical path unchanged: M4 security → M5 Paddle.)

- **Previously: V66 (June 04, 2026) —** (MD/MO SCORING-RESOLUTION INVESTIGATION — within-band fine scoring; BUILT → REVERTED; **production byte-for-byte unchanged**. This session re-opened the finer-scoring question (M1 decimal-decompression KILLED + V5.5 more-buckets DEFERRED) and resolved it definitively. **Per-metric orderability diagnosis (two corpora — 56-run + two 28-runs; dominance vs incomparable pairs within same-score clusters):** **MD ~73% INCOMPARABLE** — genuinely multi-axis (Pull = pain_intensity + current_behavior + trigger; Capture = target_specificity + capturable_density + friction_survival); a single finer scalar would manufacture false rankings. **MO 62% orderable** — single-axis gradient the `sub_position_sum` already captures (sum-resolution is the right fix in principle). **OR 94% orderable + a 153-pair honest-equivalence floor at 1.0** (`no_defensibility_component`) — no hidden structure; OR is DONE. Evidence-locked side-finding: `current_behavior` should be FLAT-TIER (top three behaviors one tier) — the only ordering under which the MD grouping holds. **BUILT then REVERTED:** (a) MO sum-resolution fine table in `prompt-stage-mo.js` (per-archetype table keyed on `sub_position_sum`, replacing the 3-anchor `DECIMAL LOOKUP`; anchors preserved; overrides composed; `v50-gates.js` given an `MO_SCORE_TABLE` branch; replay-verified 9→13 distinct scores, shift mean 0.12 / max 0.40, blend impact ≤0.10); (b) MD `demand_shape` internal marker in `prompt-stage-md.js` (Section 4B: pull/capture/shape_type from the 6 demand predicates, flat-tier `current_behavior`; conditional `diagnosis` clause firing ONLY on strong/thin corners; banned-pattern fenced; scalar/archetype/sub_position/lookup byte-untouched). **The decisive live 28-run (fixture mode, local, NO deploy):** the MO fine-table FAILED in execution — **12/26 cases (~46%) emitted `score` ≠ `table[archetype][declared sub_position_sum]`, 11 off by ≥0.2** (e.g. CON-OR-A declared sum 3 → table 6.1, emitted 5.7). Root cause: the model can't reliably index a dense 9-cell grid, AND its pre-existing `sub_position_sum` arithmetic errors (`G_ARITH_SUM`, declared ≠ SP-A+SP-B+SP-C) now translate directly into wrong scores. The old 3-anchor system was ROBUST to small sum errors (three buckets absorbed them); the fine table is FRAGILE (every sum maps to a distinct score). MD `demand_shape`: computed on 100% of cases with `_internal`, sensible distribution, NO label leak (the 2 flagged were substring false-positives like "pull request"), but the conditional clause fired on ~0 cases (near-inert) and one shape_type miscomputed — safe, no regression, no visible effect. Pre-existing-not-this-session: `G_ARITH_SUM` 16, `G_INTERNAL_PRESENCE` 8 (= Defect 1 / V5.8), Stage 2a contamination (upstream evidence variation = the V5.0-Freeze "why-it-changed" territory), `G_OR_A6_STRUCTURAL` 1. **REVERTED `prompt-stage-md.js`, `prompt-stage-mo.js`, and the `v50-gates.js` MO branch to known-good originals** (`node --check` clean; original `DECIMAL LOOKUP` + `Archetype 4 (5.4-6.5): lower=5.4, middle=6.0, upper=6.5` confirmed restored; 0 `demand_shape`/`MO_SCORE_TABLE` mentions). `route.js` never edited. **Production unchanged — nothing half-applied.** **THE DISCOVERY — the design triangle (P29):** you can have any two of {fine-grained scores, evidence-traceable justification, LLM-only execution}. Fine + LLM-only = vibes evaluator; traceable + LLM-only = coarse robust evaluator (= IdeaLoop today); **fine + traceable = code-side deterministic scoring from model commitments.** IdeaLoop was reaching for all three. The model HAS the cognitive resolution (commits sum=3 vs sum=2 reliably) but FAILS the clerical execution (exact arithmetic + table-cell lookup); the failure is the model-as-calculator, not the architecture or the high-trust design choice. **Per-metric verdict LOCKED:** OR done (honest-equivalence floor; forcing spread = fake distinction); MD scalar-stable + genuinely multi-dimensional (surface shape in PROSE conditionally, never the scalar, on current evidence — and the orderability numbers came from corpora-WITH-reruns, so the MD two-axis case needs ~80–150 DISTINCT ideas run once before the Capture axis firms up); MO fine resolution real and single-axis but in-prompt execution dead → achievable only code-side. **THE FORWARD PATH (NOT built — next chat):** move per-metric score derivation into `scoring.js` (which already computes the overall score mechanically from MD/MO/OR — precedent: V4S28 B8 removed TC from the composite code-side). The model commits SP-A/B/C LEVELS (reliable judgment; already in each scorer's `_internal.sub_position_predicates.{spA,spB,spC}` with both `level` and numeric `value` — verified present); CODE computes sum-from-components (also cures `G_ARITH_SUM`) + overrides + the fine table → authoritative score. **The one real risk is the Stage-2c seam** (corrected fine scores differ from current; Stage 2c has band-dependent logic, so a corrected score could cross a 2c band-trigger and shift synthesis prose). **Clean fix — decouple:** `scoring.js` derives BOTH a coarse score (feeds Stage 2c/3, provably-unchanged behavior) AND a fine score (display only, out of feedback loops) = fine + traceable + risk-free. Insertion point confirmed: `src/app/api/analyze-pro/route.js` after `const mo = stageMoResult.monetization || {}` (line 561), before the score-shape guard (564–591); best shape = the prompt reverts to robust 3-anchor as a coarse fallback and code computes the authoritative fine value (so a malformed `_internal` degrades to a sane coarse score, never a garbled fine one). Deliberately reverses the "all deterministic logic in the prompt" convention (justified: the model can't execute fine arithmetic). Pre-req before wiring: confirm exactly what Stage 2c + Stage 3 each read (per-metric `.score`, band, or overall). ChatGPT converged with Claude: ship coarse + precise prose now; revisit code-side scoring only if real users feel compression. **P29 — the scoring design triangle / model-judgment-vs-deterministic-execution boundary** (generalizes P25 one level deeper to the arithmetic-execution layer: keep deterministic arithmetic in CODE not the LLM; coarse-prompt-scoring robust, fine-prompt-scoring fragile, fine-code-side-scoring possible). **No engine code shipped this session** (diagnostic + reverted-experiment; production unchanged). The V5.5 "more sub_position buckets 3→4-5" deferral is SUPERSEDED — more in-prompt buckets is the wrong, fragile mechanism; code-side derivation (ActionQueue V5.10) is the right one. The felt compression problem keeps its V5.5/M2 answer: prose carries shape (`direction`-surfacing) + the explain-the-difference feature; coarse scalar + precise prose is the shipped position. **Closure cascade (3 living docs):** MasterReference V65 → V66 (this entry); NarrativeContract V11.6 → V11.7 (forward-note recording the investigation + the resolution of the V11.6 "more buckets" deferral as code-side-only — NOT a V9.x amendment, nothing shipped); ActionQueue V8 → V9 (Arc 6 + P29 + locked decisions + new item V5.10 + reframe #10). The next engine-change candidates are V5.10 (code-side fine scoring) and the V5.5 `direction`-surfacing build; neither is launch-blocking. **Dead-as-live audit pass (same session):** added an authoritative-current-state banner under §1 (it was frozen V4S28-era scaffolding still reading "Narrative Contract V6 active"); the one genuine cross-doc inconsistency — NarrativeContract §3.9/§3.9a naming the deleted Stage 2b as the live `evidence_strength` producer — was corrected in NarrativeContract V11.7 (producer is Stage 2a under V5.0). No history deleted; all prosecutor/Stage-2b/QC references in the "Previously" chain are correctly-labeled architectural history and left intact.)

- **Previously: V65 (June 3, 2026) —** (V5.0 LIVE IN PRODUCTION + repo cleanup / fixture-hardening / V5.3 code-side gates / V5.4 MatchTable audit / V5.5 within-band design investigation + MD/MO why_this_level internal-symmetry patch, June 3 session. **DEPLOY-STATE CORRECTION:** V64 + NarrativeContract V9.28 documented V5.0 as "shipped to outputs/, git commit pending, NOT YET tested end-to-end." Contract record: NarrativeContract V9.29.

**V5.3 — code-side validators (`v50-gates.js`, LOCAL-ONLY per convention, NOT committed to repo):** Four fixes, `node --check` + synthetic-smoke verified. (a) G_ARITH_SUM rewritten to read an explicit per-metric `THRESHOLDS.SP_KEYS` map transcribed verbatim from the scorers (MD/MO use prefixed `spA_/spB_/spC_` keys; **OR keys are UNPREFIXED** — `archetype_fit_strength` / `component_operational_depth` / `binding_exposure_resolution`), replacing a buggy regex/position matcher that had been binding OR correctly only by luck. (b) G_ARITH_LOOKUP routes the MO `category_grounded` override mismatch to REVIEW not FAIL — INTERIM; **CARRY-FORWARD:** when V5.9 (ActionQueue row 12b) ships an explicit `_internal` override field, replace this hardcoded REVIEW carve-out with a mechanical check of that field. (c) NEW HARD gate G_INTERNAL_PRESENCE: numeric `score` ⟹ `_internal` present (catches the MD-emits-score-with-no-`_internal` defect, 9/204 cells observed). (d) SEP_FROZEN_DETERMINISM + SEP_CONTAMINATION_HOLD reclassified into a new `diagnostic` tier (severity NA, surfaced as read-only `varianceDiagnostics`); `overallVerdict` / `separationVerdict` rewired to key only off the traceability + arithmetic HARD gates (G_INTERNAL_PRESENCE, G_ARITH_LOOKUP, G_ARITH_SUM). **HEADLINE VERDICT SEMANTICS CHANGED — justified variance no longer fails ship; pre-V5.3 run logs are not comparable.** This codifies the locked philosophy: structured judgment under uncertainty, not determinism; 1-2pt justified rerun variance is a FEATURE; the only defect is untraceable output.

**V5.4 — Stage2a→Stage2b MatchTable v2.3 gap audit (SUBSTANTIALLY RESOLVED; doc archived to Mac):** the MatchTable's contract function (Stage 2a → the deleted Stage 2b mappings) is OBSOLETE under V5.0; only 8 carry-forward concerns held value. Disposition — **#3 five domain flags** (`is_devtool` / `is_consumer_subscription` / `is_regulated_finance` / `is_regulated_education` / `is_regulated_govtech`) CONFIRMED COVERED in `prompt-stage2a.js` (schema 549-554, firing criteria 78-96, multi-flag 102, scoped sorter-not-judgment 76/106); **#1 forbidden anchors / #2 OR actionability hook / #7 per-archetype validation-move** DELEGATED to the gate suite (S_FORBIDDEN_ANCHORS, S_OR_ACTIONABILITY_HOOK @0.80, S_TEMPLATING); **#4 regulated sub-bands / #5 marketplace 3-phase / #6 decisive-uncertainty modifier / #8 MD precedence ladder** DEFERRED post-launch (need real-vertical evals).

**V5.5 — cross-metric MD floor + band-overlap + within-band score-compression investigation (FLOOR LOCKED; surfacing DESIGNED-NOT-BUILT; buckets DEFERRED):** this is the ActionQueue row-10 cluster. Three separable findings. **(1) MD floor 3.0 — LOCKED-as-intentional** (resolves the FLOOR sub-question of V9.28 Finding 2; see NarrativeContract V11.6). Falsifiability-asymmetry basis (per P27, reconstruction from artifact content, not a recovered comparative-decision record): you cannot positively *evidence* zero demand from a described product — absence-of-demand-evidence ≠ evidence-of-demand-absence; the honest low read is "speculative, no behavioral grounding" = A1 `speculative_need` = the 3.0 floor. MO/OR floor 1.0 because no-payment-capture and no-defensibility CAN be positively evidenced as absent; the 1-2 tail (MO `insufficient_evidence` / OR `no_defensibility_component`) is geometrically symmetric to the rare 7-8 top. Pushing MD to 1-2 was considered and rejected (can't evidence total absence; a truly dead idea already dies through MO+OR's 1.0 floors in the composite). The **band-overlap** sub-question (MD's overlapping bands let a strong lower-archetype's upper sub-position outscore a weak higher-archetype's lower sub-position; MO/OR touch cleanly) **stays OPEN.** **(2) Compression is upstream of the decimal (analysis only, no change):** full 56-run data — 26/53 runs at exactly 6.0 (49%), 40/53 in the 5.4-6.0 band (75%); two funnels — archetype clusters at A4 `specific_buyer_unresolved_adoption_friction` (28/53) and sub_position clusters at "middle" (33/45 traced), A4+middle = 6.0 (21 runs). Each archetype offers only 3 reachable decimals (lower/middle/upper, ~0.4-0.5 apart) — the decimal is fully determined by (archetype, sub_position), i.e. the old half-point ladder in decimal clothing. **Post-lookup interpolation offset REJECTED** (Emre's own reasoning): can't justify a 0.1 in prose, cosmetic/hollow, and it breaks the `score = lookup[archetype][sub_position]` contract just hardened in G_ARITH_LOOKUP — do not do this on MD/MO/OR. **More sub_position buckets (3→4-5) DEFERRED** until surfacing proves whether within-band reasoning is articulable — don't manufacture precision before proving existing precision is communicated. The May 18 "compression is design, not bug; most ideas SHOULD land at the cap" reframe is load-bearing and adjacent — any within-band discrimination change must consciously re-open it, not slip past. **(3) The real gap is SURFACING, not reasoning (DESIGNED-NOT-BUILT):** within-band reasoning already exists in every scorer's `_internal.sub_position_predicates[].why_this_level` (uniform across MD/MO/OR after this session's V9.29 symmetry patch). User-facing prose (MD/MO 3 fields, OR 4 fields) justifies the ARCHETYPE + binding constraint + direction-to-next-archetype, but does NOT surface why-this-position WITHIN the band. **Locked design (build next chat, NOT this session):** fold the within-band reasoning into the existing `direction` field (the natural host — it already answers "what would move higher") as a TWO-CLAUSE field — (1) current-position clause translating lower/middle/upper via a plain-language band-position phrase ("lower/middle/upper part of this band"; never "sub-position", never internal enum names), (2) next-evidence clause. Use skeleton-FAMILIES for openers (not an ordered illustrative list — the tcIncrementalNote whack-a-mole failure pattern). Per-metric: OR must NOT re-explain its binding_constraint (it has a separate field); MO must give evidence-threshold language only (no prescription / no "charge more"). Risks: enum-leakage (translate, don't transport the internal vocabulary), templating, Stage 2c overlap. **Verification when built: end-to-end run is MANDATORY** (direction feeds Stage 2c via `.explanation`), plus gate-suite re-run + templating check + length watch (two-clause vs the 1-2 sentence cap). ChatGPT adversarial round = DONE (converged and sharpened the two-clause structure, the band-position phrase, the skeleton-families, and the OR-no-overlap + MO-no-prescription guards). - **Previously: V64 (May 29, 2026) — V5.0 PIPELINE MECHANISM-CLASS SHIFT SHIPPED [architectural-level — end-to-end testing pending], May 22-29 arc. This is the next move in the V4S29 → V4S30 → V4S31 → V4S32 mechanism-class progression (per P22 — mechanism change > careful generation when on diminishing-returns curve), and structurally larger than any single step in that arc: V4S32's prosecutor + repair *detected and corrected* the residual anchor-fixing/co-decision disease at ~10% catch rate; V5.0 *structurally prevents* it by replacing model-judgment scoring with mechanical lookup. The old Stage 2b (two-call Adj + Score + clamp + prosecutor + repair + re-prosecution machinery) is deleted in its entirety and replaced with three isolated metric scorers (Stage MD / Stage MO / Stage OR) that emit `score` mechanically as `lookup[archetype][sub_position]` from predicate commitments, with prose generated *after* the score token via JSON output ordering. Score-and-prose co-decision (the disease class V9.x amendments + the V4S32 prosecutor layer were both built to fight per V63 P19) is no longer reachable. **Architecture (locked):** Stage 2a V5.0 (`src/lib/services/prompt-stage2a.js`, 667 lines, assembled from three slot-ins via Node-based VERBATIM-import assembler — never structural memory after the prior fabrication failure) emits per-metric packets (MD/MO/OR) each carrying `admissible_facts` + `strongest_positive` + `strongest_negative` + `unresolved_uncertainty` + `anchor_status` plus the metric's binding emission (`md_binding_friction_named` / `mo_binding_payment_constraint_named` / `or_components_evidenced` + `or_binding_constraint_named`); legacy OR fields `or_safeguard_satisfied` + `or_replication_barrier_type` REMOVED. Top-level `evidence_strength` emitted by Stage 2a directly (Option A LOCKED — the orphan-fix: old producer Stage 2b-Adj is deleted, and Stage 2c + Stage 3 hard-depend on this field; shape `{level: HIGH/MEDIUM/LOW, reason, thin_dimensions: [target_user/use_case/mechanism]}` matching frontend B8 contract exactly). **Three new isolated scorer files in `src/lib/services/`:** `prompt-stage-md.js` (857 lines, 7 archetypes A1-A7 band 3.0-8.5, 6 demand predicates, 9 friction subtypes FP-1..9 matching Stage 2a `md_binding_friction_named` enum exactly, SP-A/SP-B/SP-C arithmetic range −2..+6, bucket mapping [−2,+1]/[+2,+4]/[+5,+6], 21-cell lookup monotonic-within-bucket overlapping-across-buckets — intentional overlap zone A2-A5 lets strong lower-archetype edge weak higher-archetype); `prompt-stage-mo.js` (1159 lines, 6 archetypes A1-A6 band 1.0-8.5, 5 payment-capture predicates, 8+1 binding mechanism subtypes BM-1..9 matching Stage 2a `mo_binding_payment_constraint_named` enum exactly, same SP arithmetic range as MD, 18-cell lookup monotonic touching-clean-tiers); `prompt-stage-or.js` (1431 lines, 6 archetypes A1-A6 band 1.0-8.5, 7 binding-constraint subtypes + 6 components + 13 variants matching Stage 2a `or_components_evidenced` + `or_binding_constraint_named` enums exactly, SP-A 0..+3 / SP-B archetype-specific 0..+2 / SP-C −1..+2, range −1..+7, buckets [−1,+1]/[+2,+4]/[+5,+7], 18-cell lookup identical decimal pattern to MO). Each scorer's `_internal` block records: predicate commitments with `evidence_cited` per predicate, the computed archetype, the sub_position_sum arithmetic, the bucket, the binding constraint with primary/secondary, and the `schema_version` (normalized to `_v5` family across all three this session). **`src/app/api/analyze-pro/route.js` rewritten 1092 → 953 lines (−139 net):** deleted 4 imports (`STAGE2B_ADJ_SYSTEM_PROMPT` + `STAGE2B_SCORE_SYSTEM_PROMPT` + `runStage2bQualityControl` + `logQcEvents`); deleted helpers `deriveExpectedScoreRange` (score-basis clamping, ~30 lines) and `callSonnetForQc` (prosecutor caller, ~22 lines); deleted Stage 2b two-call block (Adj + Score + merge + clamp loop, ~130 lines) and entire QC block (orchestrator call + catastrophic-error fallback + logQcEvents, ~75 lines); deleted score_adjudication + quality_control strip/restore blocks (~80 lines net) and sanity-check block (~26 lines net per V63's P19 architectural insight — score-prose contradiction the heuristic guarded against is now structurally prevented); deleted `quality_control_summary` payload field. Added 3 scorer imports + comment (~8 lines), three parallel scorer calls (~170 lines, `Promise.all` each fed `idea + own packet + domain_flags + sparse_input_triggered`; verified per scorer that cross-metric quarantine holds — MD reads `domain_flags` 17× / `sparse_input_triggered` 3× and nothing from monetization or originality packets, MO 22×/1× same isolation, OR 14×/1× same isolation), same sampler config as all scoring calls (temp 0 / top_k 1 / top_p 0.1 / max_tokens 4096). Added `.explanation` synthesis per metric (`joinProse` helper concatenating each metric's prose fields — MD `[diagnosis, binding_friction_explanation, direction]`, MO `[diagnosis, binding_payment_constraint_explanation, direction]`, OR `[differentiation_basis_diagnosis, defensibility_diagnosis, binding_constraint_explanation, direction]` — into the single `.explanation` string the frontend renders via `renderProseSection`; raw prose fields retained on each metric object for a future multi-field UI without pipeline change). Added `_internal` strip/restore mirroring V4S28 B8 thin_dimensions pattern (strip before Stage 2c/3 for lean context, restore at final assembly for logging/runner/debugging — frontend grep-verified 0 reads). Added score-shape guard (~29 lines, post-parse `typeof score === 'number' || Number.isNaN(score)` check per metric; on violation fails cleanly via SSE error mirroring existing parse-failure handler rather than letting non-numeric `.score` crash frontend `score.toFixed(1)`). `evidence_strength` repointed to `stage2aResult.evidence_strength`. Stage 3 input message repointed from deleted `stage2bResult` to `{ evaluation: ev }` wrapper (Stage 3 prompt reads `evaluation.failure_risks` — wrapper preserved). **LLM-call topology:** new pipeline 8 calls flat (Stage 1 + Stage 2a + Stage TC parallel + Stage MD + Stage MO + Stage OR parallel + Stage 2c + Stage 3) vs old 8 calls + variable QC tail (up to ~6 prosecutor + repair + re-prosecution calls inside the external `stage2b-qc-orchestrator` not visible in route.js's own `client.messages.create` grep). Scoring middle latency: one parallel wall-clock round (max of three scorer call times) vs old two sequential rounds (Adj → Score) + QC tail. Cost flat per evaluation regardless of case shape; QC-mode-dependent variable cost dissolved. **Frontend: zero changes required — VERIFIED field-by-field across `src/lib/services/scoring.js` + `src/components/components.js` + `src/components/EvaluationView.js` + `src/app/page.js`:** the deleted machinery is grep-confirmed 0 references in frontend (`quality_control` 0, `score_adjudication` 0, `quality_control_summary` 0, `prosecutor` 0, `stage2b` 0 — nothing to remove). Every metric-field read resolves cleanly via emission (scorers emit `.score` numeric), synthesis (route.js builds `.explanation` from prose fields), null-safe fallback (`ev.monetization.label || "Monetization Potential"`), `.filter(Boolean)` defensive (`ev.market_demand.geographic_note` / `trajectory_note` undefined-safe), or conditional render (`marketplace_note: null` doesn't render). `evidence_strength` shape is exact Option A match (frontend reads `es.level` HIGH/MEDIUM/LOW + `es.reason` for MEDIUM callout + `es.thin_dimensions` array of `target_user`/`use_case`/`mechanism` with defensive fallback if missing — Stage 2a emits precisely this). `failure_risks` from Stage 2c unchanged. `scoring.js` byte-untouched: `calculateOverallScore` reads `market_demand.score × 0.375 + monetization.score × 0.3125 + originality.score × 0.3125` rounded to 1 decimal exactly as before (V4S28 B8 weights, TC still excluded). Same formula, weights, fields, rounding — only the *source* of the metric scores changed (mechanical lookup vs old Adj→Score→clamp→QC); individual metric scores for a given idea may differ from V4S32 baseline by design. **One UX caveat acknowledged + accepted (Emre: "adjust later it's alright"):** OR's four-prose-field structure (differentiation_basis_diagnosis + defensibility_diagnosis + binding_constraint_explanation + direction) collapses into one paragraph in the current single-block UI — functionally seamless, visually flattened; raw fields preserved on each metric object so a future multi-field renderer is a pure-frontend change with no pipeline touch. **Three-metric internal audit COMPLETE — mechanical chain verified per scorer (this was the 'one final check' Emre asked for):** 17/17 worked examples compute correctly against the locked lookups (5 MD examples across archetypes A1/A2/A4/A6/A7 + 6 MO examples across A1-A6 every archetype + 6 OR examples across A1-A6 every archetype; for each example the stated `(archetype, sub_position arithmetic, bucket, decimal)` triple was extracted and verified to equal `lookup[archetype][bucket]` exactly). All three lookup tables complete with no missing cells (MD 7×3 = 21 cells, MO 6×3 = 18 cells, OR 6×3 = 18 cells); all monotonic increasing within each bucket position (lower/middle/upper each strictly increase with archetype index). All sub-position arithmetic ranges coherent and fully covered by bucket boundaries with no gaps or overlaps (MD/MO range −2..+6 covered by [−2,+1]/[+2,+4]/[+5,+6]; OR range −1..+7 covered by [−1,+1]/[+2,+4]/[+5,+7]). All predicate level enums (target_specificity / pain_intensity / current_behavior / trigger / friction_survival / capturable_density for MD; target_specificity / payment_target / current_payment_behavior / pricing_anchor / capturable_density for MO; ORIGINALITY_BASIS / COMPONENT_EVIDENCE_STATE / REPLICATION_DIFFICULTY / JOB_SUBSTITUTABILITY / ADVANTAGE_COMPOUNDING for OR) defined in Section 1 of each scorer and consistent with archetype entry criteria in Section 2. Binding-subtype enums match Stage 2a EXACTLY across the seam — verified by bidirectional grep: MD 9 friction subtypes (`workflow_switching` / `trust_displacement` / `regulatory_acceptance` / `procurement_cycle` / `liquidity_bootstrap` / `retention_or_habit` / `build_or_free_substitute` / `integration_or_data_access` / `none_or_minimal`) present in scorer + Stage 2a; MO 8+1 mechanisms (`free_substitute_pressure` / `marketplace_cold_start` / `payment_authority_split` / `regulated_payment_friction` / `low_frequency_payment_mismatch` / `conversion_economics_unproven` / `incumbent_capture_pressure` / `price_defensibility_gap` / `none_or_minimal`) present both sides; OR 7 binding-constraint subtypes + 6 components + all 13 variants present both sides. **Three real findings closed in audit + fix pass (this session, no new prompt logic; surgical):** (i) `schema_version` was inconsistent across scorers (MD `stage_md_v5`, MO `stage_mo_v1`, OR `stage_or_v1`) — normalized to `_v5` family aligning with V5.0 pipeline generation (MO `v1`→`v5` 1 occurrence; OR `v1`→`v5` 7 occurrences across examples + schema def; MD already at `_v5`). Cosmetic but matters for future code-side validators that key off schema_version. (ii) **Stage 2a → scorer seam representational gap surfaced.** Scorer worked examples present the packet as a flat list of source-tagged facts (`- [idea_description] Target: ...`, `- [competitor: X] ...`) but route.js actually feeds each scorer `{ domain_flags, sparse_input_triggered, evidence_packet: { admissible_facts: [...], strongest_positive, strongest_negative, unresolved_uncertainty, anchor_status, <binding emission> } }` — facts nested inside `evidence_packet`, not at top level. The model would still read the JSON correctly in normal operation, but a scorer pattern-matching the flat-list examples could look for `admissible_facts` at the wrong level and under-use the structured fields (especially `strongest_negative` which Stage 2a uses to derive the binding emission). Added one-line `INPUT SHAPE:` clarification to each scorer's opening immediately after the first sentence, naming the exact JSON shape, listing what `evidence_packet` contains, and pointing the scorer to read facts primarily from `evidence_packet.admissible_facts` while treating `evidence_packet.strongest_negative` as Stage 2a's flagged most-limiting fact. Metric-specific binding emission named correctly in each (MD `md_binding_friction_named`, MO `mo_binding_payment_constraint_named`, OR both `or_components_evidenced` + `or_binding_constraint_named`); zero cross-contamination grep-verified. Closes the seam representational gap deterministically before any Phase 13 stress test, rather than discovering it empirically. (iii) **OR `secondary_subtypes` schema-example mismatch fixed.** The OR scorer's REQUIRED OUTPUT SCHEMA (line 1331) declares `secondary_subtypes` as an array of objects `{subtype, variant, evidence_cited}` with the rule "each must differ from primary in subtype OR variant" (the object form is necessary because OR subtypes carry variants — a secondary that shares the primary's subtype but differs by variant can only be expressed as an object). But three worked examples (Example 1 line 1028, Example 2 line 1081, Example 5 line 1242) emitted arrays of bare strings (`["fast_follower_replication"]`, `["job_substitution_pressure"]`). Examples contradicted the schema. Because models learn output shape heavily from examples, this would likely produce string arrays at runtime and break the distinctness rule. Converted all three to object form, with each secondary's `variant` and `evidence_cited` sourced VERBATIM from that example's own stated predicate basis — Example 1 secondary `fast_follower_replication` / variant `null` (no-variant subtype) / evidence cited from its narrative_field prompt-design fact; Example 2 secondary `job_substitution_pressure` / variant `manual_workaround` / evidence cited from its `job_substitutability = substitutable_with_friction (manual call review by sales managers is the status-quo substitute)` predicate basis; Example 5 secondary `job_substitution_pressure` / variant `adjacent_tool` / evidence cited from its `manual research + LinkedIn Sales Navigator` substitute basis. No fabrication — all evidence drawn from each example's own already-stated facts. Variant validity verified against `job_substitution_pressure` variant set {`generic_ai`, `oss`, `adjacent_tool`, `manual_workaround`} (both new variants valid) and `fast_follower_replication` no-variants property (correctly carries `null`); distinctness-from-primary verified per example (all three secondaries differ from their primary in subtype, satisfying the rule). The three empty `secondary_subtypes: []` examples were left untouched as shape-neutral. Schema definition line untouched (still declares object form); all 6 scores untouched (every example still computes correctly post-fix). **One cross-metric design observation LOGGED for explicit confirm or reconciliation (Finding 2 from the audit — open question, not a bug under either reading):** MD has floor 3.0 + overlapping bands (A1-A7 packed into 3.0-8.5; A2-A5 middle zone overlaps such that a strong lower-archetype's upper sub-position can outscore a weak higher-archetype's lower sub-position — A2-upper 5.5 > A3-middle 5.4 > A3-lower 5.0). MO and OR have floor 1.0 + touching bands (A1-A6 in 1.0-8.5; archetype rank strictly dominates — A_n upper = A_n+1 lower at shared boundary, never exceeds). Each metric is internally consistent on its own terms; the cross-metric asymmetry is real. Discussed with Emre as the design-question follow-up. The semantic basis (per P27 below, marked as reconstruction from documented artifacts rather than recovered comparative-decision record): MD's `speculative_need` A1 encodes "possible need without behavioral grounding — founder-conceived rather than market-evidenced" — the absence-of-evidence case. You cannot positively *evidence* zero demand from a described product (the packet has no signal because no behavioral evidence exists, not because demand is metaphysically nonzero); a packet flagged anti-demand (explicit rejection by named segment) is itself demand engagement and routes to A1-lower or higher-archetype-with-friction rather than sub-3.0. MO and OR floor 1.0 because payment capture and defensibility components *can* be positively evidenced as absent (no payment evidence at all, no moat at all). Reconciliation alternative considered with Emre: pushing MD floor to 1-2 was discussed and concluded absurd under either reading (you can't evidence its total absence; and it would re-introduce the correlation disease the original March 30 "approach Market Demand from its core" session deliberately killed — a truly dead idea already dies on MO + OR's 1.0 floors through the composite, MD doesn't need to go low to land the verdict low). Open: whether MD's overlap behavior (sub-position can overcome archetype) is desired in itself, or should be reconciled to MO/OR's clean-tier behavior (archetype rank dominates) for cross-metric consistency. **Confirmed-as-intentional pending explicit lock OR reconciliation decision** — held for a ChatGPT adversarial round before any structural change per Emre's discipline. Documented for the record so future-Emre doesn't lose the design history if it surfaces again. **End-to-end test status: NOT YET RUN.** Syntax verified (`node --check` passes on all three scorer files + route.js + assembled Stage 2a); shape contracts cross-checked statically; bidirectional Stage 2a ↔ scorer enum grep verified. One real Sonnet round-trip per scorer would confirm runtime output shape matches documented schema (top-level keys `market_demand` / `monetization` / `originality` with numeric `.score`) and exercise the score-shape guard — the cheapest highest-value de-risk and the next gate before Phase 13 stress testing. Phase 13 watch-items carry forward from V63: synthetic catalog SYN-DEV-OSS-1 (conversion_economics_unproven), SYN-CSUB-V-1 (free_substitute_pressure), MAT2-BEG (price_defensibility / adjacent segment transfer), MAT3-TNA (payment_authority_split), AUDIT-A3 (regulated_payment_friction), OPTZ-MED, sparse packets, plus the locked OR fact-density pressure (6+ evidence dimensions against the 3-4 `admissible_facts` cap — verify the scorer extracts facts from all packet fields including `strongest_negative` and `unresolved_uncertainty`, not just admissible_facts). **Methodology principles surfaced this arc (proposed P25-P27 for cascade lock, in addition to P21-P24 carried from V63):** **P25 — Mechanical lookup beats careful generation when on a diminishing-returns curve at the *judgment* layer.** P22 (V63) established that when three architectural moves all hit the same residual, the answer is a different mechanism class. V5.0 makes this concrete one level deeper: when *careful generation* itself is the residual (V4S32 prosecutor caught the disease at ~10% even after V4S31 physical separation closed override frequency from 40% → 3%), the next mechanism class is *remove the judgment* — replace model score-choice with a deterministic function of predicate commitments. The model still judges *predicates* with `evidence_cited` (where it's good — reading evidence shape from a packet); the *system* computes score (where the model rationalizes — anchor-fixing + co-decision). The disease class moves from "model picks score then rationalizes prose" to structurally impossible. Pattern: when an adversarial-audit mechanism has working catch-rate (signal that the underlying decision is still wobbling, not noise), the next move is to mechanize the decision, not to make the audit smarter. Recurring methodology gap; should be treated as standing discipline at session entry rather than a per-session correction. Locked-as-pattern May 29, 2026 (provisional — track whether self-correction frequency improves session-over-session; currently the gap is closing within-session but not session-entry). **P27 — Design history reconstruction discipline.** When asked "why did we design X like that" and the explicit comparative decision record cannot be located in project knowledge + past chats, name the semantic basis as RECONSTRUCTION from the design artifact's own content (e.g., archetype A1 `speculative_need`'s definition grounds MD floor 3.0), NEVER confabulate the comparative rationale ("we decided MD floor 3.0 vs MO/OR floor 1.0 *because* Y" when no record of that decision exists). Cite what is documented (the floor, the archetype semantic content, the structural choices) vs what is inferred (the comparative *why*). The MD-vs-MO/OR band asymmetry investigation this session was the canonical test of this discipline — semantic basis present in A1 definitions + 7-vs-6 archetype packing consequence, comparative decision record not found, framing presented as reconstruction with explicit caveat. V9.28 ABSORBS V9.25 (V4S30 Stage 2b schema externalization) + V9.26 (V4S31 two-call physical separation) + V9.27 (V4S32 Prosecutor + Repair) as fully-superseded mechanism classes — the architectural-history record preserves them as the path-through V4S29 → V5.0; the production prompt + orchestration no longer contains any of them. **V9 STILL OPEN.** Lock condition updated: V9 transitions OPEN → LOCKED when V5.0 production data confirms (a) score-shape guard never fires across first 100+ production evaluations, (b) scorer output schema stable at runtime, (c) Phase 13 watch zones (OR fact-density + high-band cases) close with documented calibration, OR auto-lock at July 15, 2026. **Closure cascade for this session (3 docs updated):** (i) MasterReference V63 → V64 (this entry); (ii) NarrativeContract V11.4 → V11.5 (V9.28 amendment integrated; V9.25 + V9.26 + V9.27 marked superseded-but-preserved as architectural-history record); (iii) execution-plan v5.10 → v5.11 (V5.0 session record added — Stage 2a assembly + three-scorer + route.js + frontend audit + three-metric internal audit + secondary_subtypes fix + INPUT SHAPE addition + schema_version normalization; methodology principles P25-P27 added; action queue refreshed; locked execution order rewritten as: end-to-end run → Phase 13 → validators → cross-metric MD floor decision → deploy + commit → Paddle → landing page → launch). **The 17% floor was no longer a floor at V4S32; at V5.0 it's no longer a *thing*.** It was a class of failure with a defined detection mechanism (prosecutor) and a defined correction mechanism (repair) at V4S32 — at V5.0 the entire failure class is structurally unreachable. The next floors will be different in kind: lookup-table calibration accuracy (mechanical), evidence-packet quality (upstream), and predicate-commitment honesty (the one remaining model-judgment layer). Each has its own diagnostic and cure path; none of them are the score-prose co-decision disease.

V4S30 schema externalization 17%. V4S31 physical separation 17%. Each move hit its target but the floor stayed. **Three architectural moves all hitting the same number wasn't whack-a-mole — it was structural.** The 17% is the irreducible stochasticity of single semantic judgment on borderline cases. Each layer of architectural constraint adds less than the previous. The engine work was on a diminishing-returns curve. **The emotional collapse moment (locked verbatim):** Emre: "Look man, I'm not chasing the perfect here, but we did two fucking structural architecture changes. User-wise nothing changed. What's the angle here? We are drawing circles. We are at the same place we started. What's the point of all this?" Claude owned the overpromising. Mapped trajectory honestly: V4S29 fixed unstructured prose; V4S30 fixed prose-without-structural-commitment; V4S31 fixed structural-commitment-with-anchoring-pressure. Each layer hit its target. The disease moved each time. The rate floored. Engine work has diminishing returns; the real product wins are real but invisible; the bottleneck for the 30-idea junior freelancer persona is NOT Stage 2b — it's popup feature + MD templating + landing page + Paddle. **The big reframe — Justifiability, not consistency (Emre, locked verbatim):** "the point is not to make every score consistent or reduce spikes, the biggest priority should be the justification. If the prose is sound I don't care about 7.5 spikes 1/5 — as long as our prose is not templating and well-justifiable, I'm okay." Tested all 6 V4S31 spikes against the bar — NONE passed. Not three founders disagreeing — one founder reading the case correctly 4 times and selectively half the time. The spike rate WAS a real problem under Emre's own bar. **The convergent idea — Prosecutor + Repair (V4S32):** Claude proposed stopping trying to make Stage 2b's generation more careful and adding a separate downstream audit step asking "does this prose's reasoning survive careful reading by a domain-knowledgeable founder?" ChatGPT independently arrived at the same idea — called it "prosecutor" — but sharper: conditional triggering (only on risky outputs: score ≥ 7.0, resolution=overridden, applicable_rules=[] with high score); three verdicts not two (PASS / FAIL / BORDERLINE — BORDERLINE = MB popup pattern applied here); adversarial framing ("find the flaw") not balanced; three-stage separation (Stage 2b generates, Prosecutor audits, Repair fixes). Emre added the product-genius angle: surface the prosecutor in the SSE. "Internal Quality Check..." — a user watching the engine police itself is a brand position no marketing copy can buy. Real, not theater — because the audit genuinely happens. **Convergent independent solutions are strong signal** — methodology principle from this arc. **V4S32 architecture LOCKED:** Sequential layer between Stage 2b-Score and Stage 2c (not parallel — Stage 2c reads scores + explanations and must reflect post-repair values). Per-metric parallelization within the layer (MD/MO/OR independent — Promise.all for prosecutor calls, repair calls, re-prosecution calls; wall latency = max(metric) not sum). Repair regenerates `score_adjudication` (not just score + explanation — otherwise downstream reads stale adjudication). Strip `quality_control` before Stage 2c, restore at final assembly (mirrors V4S31 adjudication strip pattern). **V4S32 trigger logic (active at launch):** `high_score` (score ≥ 7.0 — spike territory); `overridden` (resolution === "overridden" — A3-class disease); `empty_rules_with_high_score` (applicable_rules.length === 0 AND score ≥ 6.5 — walk-all-skip risk MAT3-tna senior, MAT2-beg disease). **Trigger log-only at launch:** `mid_band_anchor_risk` (regex/substring on positive_basis — boolean flag, no prosecution; oﬄine sample-prosecute later if catch rate meaningful). **Skip cases (always PASS without calling prosecutor):** score < 6.0 (no overconfidence to catch); applicable_rules non-empty AND resolution === "binds" AND score === cap_floor_value (textbook clean cap landing). **V4S32 verdict enum (6 values, per ChatGPT review correction):** SKIPPED_NO_TRIGGER (triggers evaluated, none fired — not logged); QC_UNAVAILABLE (technical failure timeout/parse/5xx — logged for operational visibility); PASS (clean); BORDERLINE (close call, candidate for popup feature); FAIL_REPAIRED (caught flaw, repair landed clean, re-prosecution PASS, score replaced); DOUBLE_FAIL (caught flaw, repair attempted, re-prosecution also FAIL — original score preserved). **Per-metric quality_control field added to ev:** prosecutor_verdict, triggers_fired, flaw_category, repair_attempted, repair_succeeded, original_score (preserved on FAIL_REPAIRED), close_call_framing (only when BORDERLINE), prosecutor_latency_ms, repair_latency_ms. **Payload-level quality_control_summary added:** qc_mode, checked_metrics, repaired_metrics, borderline_metrics, double_fail_metrics, qc_unavailable_metrics, total_qc_latency_ms, qc_layer_version 'v1.0', quality_failure (true when 2+ metrics DOUBLE_FAIL). **Feature flag STAGE2B_QC_MODE = off | log_only | repair, default 'repair'** per launch decision (Emre solo-testing — log_only doesn't earn its place when no real users exist;
