The lens reordered priorities: Summary templating moved from "minor OBSERVE" to EXISTENTIAL; alpha variance moved to SEVERE; Stage 1 blindness moved from "big win" to LOW within-profile impact; TC profile-awareness moved to LOW. **Three problem classes locked from the reframe:** Prose templating (fixable with anti-imitation method) / Selection bias (needs decision-policy discipline) / Scoring distribution (needs rubric calibration / score-discipline). **Prose templating chapter SHIPPED (May 18, 2026)** — `src/lib/services/prompt-stage2c.js` shipped β1 cure (Summary "The tension between proven X" 49%→0%, +5 lines via E6 disease additions + β1 anti-imitation NOTE; ChatGPT's broader [X] wording incorporated) + β2 preemptive cure ("the unresolved variable" 11%→8.9%, "that determines this case's trajectory" 8%→0%, same E6+anti-imitation NOTE method, ~6 lines net add). `src/lib/services/prompt-stage-tc.js` shipped tcIncrementalNote cure (100% literal template "A simpler starting point would be" → 0% on targeted phrase, replaced literal format mandate at line 263-264 with cognitive-operation framing + forbidden opener + 5 illustrative forms; semantic guardrails preserved verbatim — phasing/timeline/outcome prediction BAD examples kept) + tcBase cure (44% "Matches the X" combined → 0% on targeted prefix, rule 3 split into 3/3a/3b with anchor-name requirement preserved + anti-dominance + 5 illustrative forms including "Matches the X because Y" as still-valid form per ChatGPT's anti-dominance-not-hard-ban note). Stage TC +19 lines net. Both files contain ChatGPT's "These are illustrative forms, not options to rotate through mechanically" wording. **Mid-band templating verification** (29 cases × 2 passes, fresh templating runner): **Class 1 (cured patterns must disappear) 7/7 PASS** — every targeted disease pattern from May 18 was 0-1.8% post-cure. **Class 2 (whack-a-mole guard) 2/4 FAIL** — both TC fixes cured the targeted pattern AND created a near-identical-concentration NEW pattern at the FIRST alternative in the illustrative list (tcIncrementalNote "A leaner first version is..." → 85.7%; tcBase "This sits at the..." → 89.3%). **Class 3 (γ canary) PASS** — β fixes didn't displace into γ. **Class 4 (alpha stability) PASS** (0.30 vs threshold 0.45). **The whack-a-mole meta-finding (locked as design-method learning):** Pure-ban approach with provided alternatives has a STRUCTURAL CEILING — when given an ordered list of "illustrative" alternatives, the model picks the first available and treats it as canonical. The "not options to rotate through mechanically" wording does nothing. Model isn't rotating — it picks one and stops. Stage 3's skeleton-family pattern (multiple cognitive operations with avoid-when conditions, no ordered canonical list) is the structurally different approach that resists this; that's the design pattern for any future structural redesign of TC sub-surfaces. **TC residuals ACCEPTED via UX-prominence reframe (Emre's product judgment):** tcBase sits in main TC paragraph as 1 sentence among prose (anchor name and reason both vary — modest UX harm); tcIncrementalNote is italicized friendly hint at end of section (visually de-emphasized, X/Y content varies — low UX harm). Different UX weight than Summary opener (first thing read on page, was 49% templating, now cured). **Prose-templating chapter effectively closed.** Could spend a structural session applying Stage 3's skeleton-family pattern to both TC sub-surfaces; user-perceived improvement marginal because surfaces are inherently low-prominence; move to bigger problems instead. **Stage 2c Risk 3 archetype A bias C7 structural patch SHIPPED (May 18, 2026, prompt-stage2c.js +25 lines net, Stage 2c now 1208 lines total).** **Diagnosis** — C7 was missing the discipline that makes Stage 3 MB selection work (no walk-all-before-selecting, no "first-listed doesn't get priority," only soft "compare against C5 evidence patterns" tiebreaker, DISTRIBUTION DISCIPLINE clause at line 952 operationally meaningless per-case). Additionally: structural imbalance — C4 splits archetype A into three internal subtypes (A1/A2/A3) competing for the same JSON output "A" while B/C/D/E each have one subtype (3:1:1:1:1 imbalance baked into candidate space before any selection bias). Two-stage root-cause: initial diagnosis caught the proximate cause (concreteness vs leverage); deeper diagnosis after Emre's pushback ("Stage 2c has a structure. Now I want you to internalize that structure...") forced discovery of missing CONTEXT-DRIVEN NARROWING step that BOTH working selection procedures (Summary A4 + Stage 3 MB) use before judgment. Original C7 patch went straight to walk-all-7 with no narrowing; without narrowing, binding-leverage test has to do all the work alone against 7 candidates with no contextual prior. **Path A "structurally complete" patch shipped — 6 numbered steps matching A4 + Stage 3 MB selection pattern:** STEP 1 DEFAULT CANDIDATE SUBSET (context-driven narrowing using C3 classification INSIDER/PARTIAL-INSIDER/OUTSIDER + idea binding-resource dimension: PARTIAL-INSIDER → {B, C}; OUTSIDER + software-build → {A1, A2, A3}; OUTSIDER + relationship-locked-buyer → {B}; OUTSIDER + credentialed-buyer → {C}; OUTSIDER + capital-heavy → {D}; OUTSIDER + sales-motion-heavy → {E}); STEP 2 WALK within subset with structural note on A's 3:1 imbalance contextualized to subset; STEP 3 SINGLE FIRE → select; STEP 4 MULTIPLE FIRES → BINDING-LEVERAGE TEST with ChatGPT's softened wording "B may be the higher-leverage binding gap despite A's visibility" (not "is the higher-leverage gap regardless of A's visibility" — softened wording prevents over-correction into B), two worked contrasts A-vs-B and A-vs-C; STEP 5 OVERRIDE CHECK for non-subset candidates requires substantively stronger evidence (RARE); STEP 6 VERIFICATION requires articulating leverage justification when A selected over co-firing non-A. **Confidence ~80% A archetype drops from 61% toward 35-45% on next test run.** Risks: over-correction toward B (softened "may be" mitigates), narrowing-classification load-bearing accuracy (new judgment layer), verification step creating over-justification. **Verification status: PENDING.** Will run via targeted Risk 3 runner OR full B10a. ChatGPT's verification methodology improvements incorporated: A-displacement quality manual review (was A genuinely wrong on cases that shifted, or did patch push it away from valid execution-capacity risk?), per-C3-class distribution segmentation (PARTIAL-INSIDER vs OUTSIDER buckets tested separately), B-vs-C distinguishability metric. **Two product framings established as V4+ design intent (Emre, mid-session):** **(1) Justifiable variance is feature territory, not bug territory** — variance between justified alternative readings on ambiguous cases is signal, not noise. "If you let 3 different ex-founders judge the idea, they probably select different bottlenecks for the same idea. We can't be deterministic too much because it damages output quality." Conditions: each variant must be individually correct + well-justified (not "model defaulted under ambiguity"); variants must be bounded (categorically different diagnoses still bug, e.g. competitive substitution vs market doesn't exist); UI must surface honestly. Covers: MB variance (10 violations on May 18 — parked as design-accepted, no engine work), Risk 3 firing-rate inconsistency (14 silent-firings — re-examine through this lens), alpha variance on band-boundary cases (partial coverage). Does NOT cover: Risk 3 archetype A bias 61% (cross-case dominance, different problem class — still gets C7 patch), prose templating (identical phrases across different ideas, not "different valid readings"). **(2) Ambiguity-surfacing popup pattern (V4+ feature)** — for surfaces with multiple valid options (MB, Risk 3 archetype, score-band boundaries), pipeline output includes ambiguity flag + alternate-reading payload. UI renders unambiguous cases normally; ambiguous cases get subtle "click for model's reasoning" indicator. Same UX shape as existing "what does this score mean?" popups. Popup reveals: "This case sat between two valid framings"; model's reasoning chain for each; why ultimately picked the one shown; what signals would have tipped it the other way. Engine work: schema addition (boolean ambiguity flag + alternate-reading payload), NOT logic change — capture-the-discarded-reasoning that already lives inside selection procedures like Stage 3 MB's walk-all step. Two related V4+ concepts: ambiguity popups (primary, inline per-case) + multi-run unified read mode (secondary, power-user). **Stage 2b Stream A score-discipline patches SHIPPED (May 19, 2026, prompt-stage2b.js 452→514 lines, +62 lines net, +1287 words).** **Three problem classes targeted scoring distribution next:** MD 59% at 6.0 (4 distinct values across 37 cases), OR 46% at 4.5, alpha variance >0.3pt on 13 cases. **Two-stream framing locked (Emre's reframe — both audiences co-equal, neither subordinated):** Score = book cover (Type 1 user — sees score, doesn't read prose if score feels off); Prose = first pages (Type 2 user — reads prose, gives credit if reasoning strong). Stream A = score discipline (Type 1). Stream B = prose templating with cognitive families (Type 2, deferred). **Stream A patches:** (1) **A1 OVERRIDE-EXPLICIT CLAUSE (MD/MO/OR)** — when scoring above what an anti-inflation rule / INVALID BASES / BINDING CAP / HEDGE DISCIPLINE would permit, prose MUST name the cap rule by identifier and state the specific packet fact that overrides it. (2) **A1 TRIGGER-BUYER MATCH amendment (MD)** — forces buyer named must match cap-rule's specified actor; catches A3-style leak where regulatory trigger affects prescribers but cap asks about patients. (3) **A1 RULE PRECEDENCE amendment (OR)** — when multiple anti-inflation rules apply, most restrictive (lowest cap value) governs: COMBINATION (4.0-5.0) < FEATURE VS PRODUCT (5.0) < VERTICAL POSITIONING (5.5) < WORKFLOW IS NOT WEDGE (6.0). (4) **A2 CAP-LANDING PRECISION (MD narrow-use + MO)** — when NAMED cap fires AND no counter-anchor argues past it, score lands at cap floor (6.0) not rubric ceiling (6.5); NOT applied to OR (tiered cap landings already working calibration). (5) **A1 SCOPE clarifier** — "This clause applies when a specific cap rule actually fires on this case... A cap does not fire merely because the case has friction." Added after first verification cycle revealed M2 rule-citation creep (model invoked "caps demand at the middle band" on cases where no cap was being argued past); SCOPE clarifier cured this. **Verification (8-case × 5 reruns × 2 cycles):** First cycle (A1 alone): hard leaks eliminated (A3 MD 7.5 → max 6.5, MAT2-senior OR 7.0 → max 6.5) but M2 rule-citation creep (6.5 → 6.0 across all 5 runs). Second cycle (A1+A2 + SCOPE applied): **7/7 cases pass + both FP guards pass for first time**, M2 rule-citation creep cured, M2 MD held at 6.0 across 5/5 (interpretation per pre-lock: 6.0 is correct baseline per outcome 2(a)). **Residual diagnosed: "soft engagement without binding" pattern at A3** (drifted UP from 6.0 with A1 alone to 6.5 with A1+A2 in 4/5 runs) — model describes cap-relevant friction in natural language ("relationship displacement friction") without committing to bind OR override, lands at 6.5 between cap floor 6.0 and rubric ceiling 7.0; satisfies neither A1's enforcement (not going above 7.0) nor A2's enforcement (not formally "naming cap rule by identifier" as triggered); model found third option both reviewers warned about. **Deeper structural diagnosis (token-order root cause)** — when JSON schema emits `{"scores":{"md":X}, "explanations":{"md":"..."}}`, the score token emits BEFORE the explanation prose. Model forms holistic gestalt over packet+rubric+cap rules, emits score, then generates prose to rationalize. Score+prose co-decided in one act, not sequenced as evidence→comparison→score→justification. Prompt clauses can shape prose but not the underlying decision sequence — score was already chosen at gestalt time, "middle ground" at 6.5 exists because both readings of the case feel valid and model picks most defensible coherent (score, prose) pair under ambiguity. **Real structural fix would be Stage 2b output schema decomposition** (force diagnosis tokens BEFORE score token): `md_analysis: { cap_mechanisms_in_packet: [...], cap_resolutions: [...], score: X, explanation: "..." }`. Token order = reasoning order. Score becomes mechanically derived from prior tokens. Soft-engagement loophole closes structurally, not via prose discipline. This is session-sized work (parser changes + Stage 2c/Stage 3 input shape updates + schema validation + backward compatibility), not surgical patch — DEFERRED to B10a data first. **Decision criteria for Stream A next move LOCKED (no more iteration this session):** Soft-engagement frequency on B10a 37-case bank determines action: ≤7/37 (≤20%) → calibration noise, move to Stream B prose templating; 8-15/37 (20-40%) → apply ChatGPT's narrow A3 binding-requirement patch + re-verify + ship; >15/37 (>40%) → defer to Stage 2b structural decomposition session (schema change). **NEW V4S29 methodology lessons logged this arc (5 lessons, proposed Principles 17-20 below):** (i) **Targeted Stage tests cannot catch population-level cross-case templating** — Stage 2c verification reported F17 "Your N years..." opener 0/39 cured (correct for that surface) but couldn't see β1 templating which required 20+ different ideas at same band to detect. Methodology gap, not engine miss. Solution: cross-case templating probe (top opening 5-gram across 20+ cases) at structural session verification time. (ii) **Pure-ban approach with provided alternatives has structural ceiling (whack-a-mole at design-method level)** — when given ordered list of "illustrative" alternatives, model picks first available and treats it as canonical regardless of "not options to rotate through mechanically" wording. Stage 3's skeleton-family pattern (multiple cognitive operations with avoid-when conditions, no ordered canonical list) is structurally different and works. (iii) **Within-profile lens as primary UX verification target** — cross-profile testing answers QA questions about structural consistency; within-profile testing (one user + one profile + many ideas) answers product questions about whether engine feels like it's seeing each idea fresh. Within-profile primary for narrative-prose surfaces. (iv) **Score+prose co-decided at token-emission time** — JSON schema order = reasoning order in LLM token streams; prompt clauses shape prose but not underlying decision sequence; for full structural control, output schema must force diagnosis tokens before score token. (v) **Justifiable variance is feature territory, not bug territory** — run-to-run variance on ambiguous cases between valid alternative readings is signal not noise; engine fix surfaces ambiguity, UI fix names it for user; different from cross-case dominance which is real problem. **Proposed Principles 17-20 for cascade lock:** P17 (Within-profile lens as primary UX verification target), P18 (Cross-case templating probe at structural session verification time), P19 (Score+prose co-decided at token-emission time), P20 (Justifiable variance is feature territory not bug territory). **NarrativeContract V11.2 → V11.3 amendment locked this session (V9.21 NEW + V9.22 NEW + V9.23 NEW + V9.24 NEW):** V9.21 Stage 2c Summary β1+β2 anti-imitation discipline (E6 disease additions + per-archetype anti-imitation NOTEs); V9.22 Stage TC tcIncrementalNote + tcBase anti-template surface variation discipline (literal format mandate retracted, anchor-name requirement preserved while sentence-form varies, with documented whack-a-mole residual at first alternative); V9.23 Stage 2c C7 archetype selection structural patch (6-step procedure with context-driven narrowing + binding-leverage test + verification, matching A4 + Stage 3 MB selection pattern); V9.24 Stage 2b Stream A score-discipline (A1 OVERRIDE-EXPLICIT + A2 CAP-LANDING PRECISION + A1 SCOPE clarifier + TRIGGER-BUYER MATCH + RULE PRECEDENCE amendments). **V9 still OPEN.** Lock condition unchanged: V9 transitions OPEN → LOCKED when next major surface clears (post-Stream-A B10a verification confirms scoring discipline cure landed, OR auto-lock at June 10, 2026). **Files modified in production this arc (3 files):** `src/lib/services/prompt-stage2c.js` (β1 + β2 + C7 patches, +49 lines net, file now 1208 lines, May 18 ship); `src/lib/services/prompt-stage-tc.js` (tcIncrementalNote + tcBase patches, +19 lines net, May 18 ship); `src/lib/services/prompt-stage2b.js` (Stream A1+A2+SCOPE patches, 452→514 lines, +62 lines net, +1287 words, May 19 ship). Local dev shipped; commit status varies. **Closure cascade for this session (3 living docs updated + 1 new tracking doc):** (i) NarrativeContract V11.2 → V11.3 (V9.21 + V9.22 + V9.23 + V9.24 amendments integrated); (ii) MasterReference V61 → V62 (this entry); (iii) NEW `18-may-b10a-findings.md` tracking document created as append-only handoff doc covering full arc from May 18 B10a to Stream A ship + methodology learnings + decision criteria + V4+ product framings (active reference for next chat). **Locked execution order (May 19, 2026) — updated post-Stream-A ship:** (1) ~~Stage 3 route + frontend cleanup~~ ✅ CLOSED; (2) ~~Stage TC structural session~~ ✅ CLOSED (V9.20); (3) ~~Stage 1 structural session~~ ✅ CLOSED (per Emre's V61 confirmation; documentation gap retroactively noted); (4) ~~May 18 B10a comprehensive verification~~ ✅ CLOSED; (5) ~~Stage 2c β1+β2 prose templating cures~~ ✅ CLOSED (May 18); (6) ~~Stage TC tcIncrementalNote+tcBase prose templating cures~~ ✅ CLOSED (May 18); (7) ~~Stage 2c Risk 3 C7 structural patch~~ ✅ SHIPPED (May 18) — VERIFICATION PENDING; (8) ~~Stage 2b Stream A score-discipline patches~~ ✅ SHIPPED (May 19) — B10a VERIFICATION PENDING; (9) **Stream A B10a verification** — NEXT immediate work, decision criteria locked at §3.10 of 18-may-b10a-findings.md; (10) **Conditional next** based on Stream A B10a outcome: Stream B prose templating session (cognitive families), OR narrow A3 binding-requirement patch + re-verify, OR Stage 2b structural decomposition session (schema change); (11) **Stage 2a calibration revisit** for MD compression — bigger work, structurally separate, deferred to dedicated session; (12) **Execution Plan feature planning session**; (13) **Execution Plan feature build.** Pre-launch infrastructure work still deferred to dedicated sessions: F4 + F13 Bundle 5; F6 Specificity Gate recalibration; pre-Paddle security session. (ii) **Documentation voice vs operational voice drift** — Claude consistently drafted in documentation voice across 8 structural batches (explaining intent, narrating reasoning); ChatGPT consistently compressed to operational voice (instructions only, examples without prose); pattern emerged Stage 2b → Stage 2a → Stage 2c → Stage 3 → Stage TC across all 5 structural sessions but Stage TC was the first session where Claude self-corrected mid-stream after the pattern was named; remains a recurring failure mode for future prompt work. (iii) **Variation is not always a virtue** — adjustment_explanation field needs variation (anti-templating for same-profile-many-ideas users) while incremental_note field needs containment (predictability of shape); right discipline per field, not blanket "more variety better"; design choice locked per-field rather than universal. Zero findings inside redesigned Pro stage prompts (Stage 2a/2b/2c/3) genuinely unaddressed. **3 NEW methodology principles locked this session (Principles 14-16):** **Principle 14 — Pre-cure structure check.** Before proposing new cure structure, read existing structure exhaustively. F23 first-draft proposed C6a/b/c/d expansion; pre-cure structure check revealed C5 already had rich evidence anchors with 24 examples; cure became C7→C5 reroute (no new rows). 4-question check before any cure: (a) what existing structure already addresses adjacent problems? (b) does the existing structure have richer machinery at adjacent layer? (c) can the cure connect existing structure rather than add new structure? (d) does the proposed cure duplicate, extend, or replace existing? Locked May 16, 2026. **Principle 15 — Asymmetric danger of positive vs banned examples.** Banned phrases (F2 "Building X requires Y") get cured by removing them. Positive worked examples become sticky templates within the archetype/category they exemplify (Principle 10 in production). Asymmetry: prompt designers reach for examples to clarify intent, but examples within a category compress into templates. F23 cure deliberately avoided adding any positive examples to C7 — the cure references existing C5 examples rather than adding new ones. Pattern: when curing variance, prefer reference-to-existing-discipline over add-new-positive-examples. Locked May 16, 2026. **Principle 16 — Surgical over architectural-expansion discipline.** When existing structure has rich machinery solving an adjacent problem, the cure connects existing structure rather than building parallel structure. F23 surgical cure (1 line rewritten, 0 new rows, 0 new examples) outperformed C6a/b/c/d expansion would have (4 new rows, parallel to C6's existing pairwise logic). Architectural expansion creates verification burden (each new row needs its own test cases); surgical reroute inherits existing verification (C5's discipline already tested at synthesis stage). Pattern: cure scope should match disease scope; pairwise disease → pairwise cure; system-wide disease → system-wide cure. Locked May 16, 2026. **B10b cross-section narrative coherence verification (still future work) consumes NarrativeContract V11 as ground truth across 9 interpretation surfaces; F23 patch added to V11 → V11.1 amendment (§3.4 Risk 3, V9.19) provides additional B10b verification anchor.** **NarrativeContract V11 → V11.1 amendment locked this session (V9.19 NEW — §3.4 Stage 2c C7 archetype selection discipline).** C7 archetype selection routes ambiguous cases through (a) C5 per-archetype evidence patterns + (b) Section 1.1 case-truth fallback. Soft "earliest meaningful validation step" tiebreaker DEPRECATED. Pairwise archetype confusion (2-way) resolved deterministically; tri-archetype confusion (3+ way) tracked as F23 known residual. **V9 still OPEN.** Lock condition unchanged: V9 transitions OPEN → LOCKED when Stage 1 structural session ships, or auto-lock at June 10, 2026. **Locked execution order (May 16, 2026) — updated post-F23 cure:** (1) **Stage 3 route + frontend cleanup** — IMMEDIATE NEXT SESSION (still pending; nothing in F23 work changes this priority). pattern proved twice this session at Row 5 MO competitor-default + Row 6 INPUT-SIDE-mandatory both caught by ChatGPT pushback. - **Bundle 2 closure record (May 8, 2026, deployed):** Bundle 2 (F1 partial cure) shipped sampler hardening (`top_k=1, top_p=0.1` alongside `temperature=0`) on three Anthropic SDK calls in `src/app/api/analyze-pro/route.js`: Stage 2a (`messages.create` for STAGE2A_SYSTEM_PROMPT), Stage TC (parallel to Stage 2a, scoring TC isolated), Stage 2b (`messages.create` for STAGE2B_SYSTEM_PROMPT). Stage 1 already had this from V4S28 P0.5; Stage 2c and Stage 3 deliberately NOT hardened (narrative synthesis stages, out of F1 scope). Six lines of config across three calls. No prompt edits, no schema changes, no architectural changes. **Cure scope: PARTIAL F1 cure** — cleanly addresses Layer A (sampler-driven near-tie collapse) of the four-layer phenomenology surfaced by the F1 investigation. Diagnostic evidence: ARC-D2 σ(MO) 0.63→0, M3 σ(MO) 0.21→0. Layer C residuals (L2 frame-selection on cross-cutting evidence, MAT2-beginner cross-metric budget swap) persist by design — scoped for future Stage 2a packeting bundle. **Architectural cures NOT shipped:** F1's original lock specified 1A (OR sidecar) or 1B (full split); investigation produced no evidence either was necessary. Investigation also tested and rejected: asymmetric MO band tightening (introduced cross-metric coupling — L2 MD downshift artifact, the canonical Layer D demonstration); symmetric dominant-signal selection instruction (regressed previously-cured ARC-D2 from σ=0 to σ=0.73). Both rejected via locked decision criteria. **Investigation infrastructure shipped (`runners/` directory):** 4 diagnostic shared modules (`f1-diagnostic-shared.js`, `f1-investigation-shared.js`, `f1-diagnostic-thresholds.js`, `extension-resolver.mjs`); 9 investigation runners covering Phase A, Phase B, Phase 1 (deep capture), Phase 2C (sampler), Phase 2A (MO tightening), Phase 2B (MD loosening), Test 3 (combined), Test 4 (MAT2-focused), Test 5 (dominant-signal); 3 prompt counterfactual files in `runners/prompts/` (`stage2b-mo-tightened.js`, `stage2b-md-loosened.js`, `stage2b-dominant-signal.js`); 1 end-to-end verification runner (`run-bundle2-verification.js`) exercising full Pro pipeline against live `/api/analyze-pro`; auto-generated diagnostic outputs (`f1-*-report.md` files commit selectively as evidence; `f1-*-checkpoint.json` and `f1-*-results.json` regenerable runtime state typically gitignored; `.f1-fixtures/` Stage 1 + Stage 2a fixture cache typically gitignored). The `runners/` directory is **investigation infrastructure, not throwaway scripts** — future bundles addressing model-output behavior problems should extend it rather than rebuild from scratch. The pinned-anchor prompt counterfactual pattern (substitution strings hard-fail if production prompt drifts), the checkpoint/resume pattern, the locked-decision-criteria-before-run pattern, and the `runStage2bWithOptions()` wrapper for custom prompt + custom sampler injection are all reusable across investigations. **Verification:** full-pipeline `run-bundle2-verification.js` runner — 4 cases × 3 reruns = 12 evaluations through the live Pro pipeline. Zero pipeline errors. Schema integrity confirmed across all 12 runs. End-to-end variance observed (cumulative across Stage 1 retrieval + Stage 1 synthesis + Stage 2a packet construction + Stage 2b scoring + Stage 2c synthesis + Stage 3 bottleneck classification) substantially exceeds diagnostic variance. **Verification thresholds were miscalibrated** (set against diagnostic numbers from frozen-fixture environment, applied to full-pipeline runs where four upstream stages regenerate per run) — the verification did NOT fail Bundle 2; it surfaced a previously-unmeasured property of the product (end-to-end variance has more sources than Stage 2 sampler hardening addresses). This is documented as a methodology lesson for future bundle verification design: **verification thresholds must distinguish controlled (diagnostic) vs end-to-end (full-pipeline) measurement** explicitly. **Methodology output: Methodology Principle 7 (counterfactual prompt tests precede architectural change)** locked from F1 investigation. Documented in MasterReference V53 Methodology Principles section + `F1-investigation-case-study.md` (canonical worked example). Applies to all future investigations of model-output behavior problems (variance, templating, framing instability, judgment drift) — NOT to information-flow / validation / state-management problems, which legitimately require architectural reasoning first. **Productive tension with V4S11 lesson** ("physical separation beats prompt rules"): both remain valid. V4S11 says cross-metric contamination genuinely cannot be solved by prompt-level rules. Principle 7 says don't *assume* physical separation is the cure for variance problems without testing prompt fixes first. Counterfactual tests reveal which lesson applies in any given case. **F1's layered phenomenology locked (taxonomy for future variance investigations):** Layer A — Sampler-driven near-tie collapse → CURED by sampler hardening; Layer B — Band-boundary fuzziness → curable by enumerable rubric anchors (NOT shipped — asymmetric tightening rejected, symmetric untested); Layer C — Interpretive frame-selection on cross-cutting evidence → cure surface is Stage 2a packeting discipline (future bundle); Layer D — Cross-metric prompt-reading coupling → operational rule (symmetric edits only); not a separate cure. **Bundle 2 lessons that carry forward:** (1) Methodology Principle 7 itself is the most durable output — future investigations consume the F1 case study as worked precedent. (2) Verification thresholds must distinguish controlled vs end-to-end measurement — diagnostic measurements (Stage 2b against frozen fixtures) and end-to-end measurements (full pipeline regenerating) produce different numbers; thresholds set against one cannot be applied to the other. (3) Asymmetric prompt edits trigger cross-metric coupling — L2 MD downshift artifact is canonical demonstration; operational rule: never ship asymmetric prompt edits without verifying cross-metric stability on cases that hit unchanged metrics; symmetric edits are default safe direction. (4) Sampler hardening is a stability floor, not a complete cure — real value, partial coverage; layered phenomenology requires layered cures. (5) Probabilistic-judgment products have an irreducible variance floor — some variance reflects genuine ambiguity in evidence (two coherent reads of the same fact pattern); product identity ("honest stress-testing") is compatible with this; user-facing framing should reflect it; per-evaluation confidence labels remain forbidden (V4S26-era pipeline-comparison confusion). (6) The reframe question that broke the architectural anchor mid-investigation ("Why is MD steady? What is MD's packeting doing differently than MO or OR?") is the canonical example of how user-domain insight breaks Claude's prior assumptions — flagged as the type of intervention worth seeking explicitly. **NarrativeContract V8 still LOCKED** — Bundle 2's cure is sampler config (not contract-governed); V9.9 (§3.9 EvStr home) and V9.11 (Stage 2 isolation) verdict-conditional amendments RESOLVED as no-amendment-needed; V9.14 NEW added for Methodology Principle 7 (drafting deferred per V9 lock policy). Surfaced finding for next-session work: Haiku gate calibration revisit needed (see "Pending follow-ups & known issues" section below).** **Bundle B9 Stage TC parse hardening (V4S28 surface added during smoke testing — reproducible Pro pipeline parse failure on structured input) DEPLOYED, VERIFIED, and CLOSED (May 4, 2026, single commit on main: 'B9 Stage TC parse hardening — defensive cleanJsonResponse for prose preamble').** One file modified: `src/app/api/analyze-pro/route.js` — the `cleanJsonResponse` helper function upgraded from startsWith-based fence-stripping (which only handled markdown fences at start/end of response) to substring-extraction approach (locates first `{` and last `}`, slices between them, handles bare JSON / markdown-fenced JSON / prose-preamble + fenced JSON / prose-preamble + bare JSON / JSON with trailing prose all in one path; defensive null/empty/non-string handling at function entry; returns trimmed input if no JSON object found so existing JSON.parse error path fires unchanged). Bug discovery: while running Sherpa-input (450-word developer experience monitoring product pitch with formal IDE-plugin / tutorial-vs-real-engineering framing) on Pro pipeline as a G1-LONG follow-up smoke test, two consecutive runs both produced "Stage TC parse failed: ..." errors in Vercel logs with identical failure shape — Sonnet leaked Stage TC's internal reasoning headers (HARDEST TECHNICAL PROBLEM / SIMPLEST WORKING VERSION / BEYOND-TUTORIAL GAP) as visible prose preamble before the markdown-fenced JSON output, breaking the existing parser's `startsWith("```json")` detection. Diagnosis confirmed: same input on Standard pipeline (unified prompt.js single Sonnet call) succeeded with clean TC=7.0 evaluation, ruling out content-cursed input or model bad-day; the bug was specifically in Stage TC's isolated-call path where the prompt's reasoning structure had unusually high attention budget on Sherpa-class structured input (Sherpa's content directly maps onto the TC framing, causing the model to mirror the prompt's internal headers as visible output). Helper is shared across all six chained-pipeline parses (Stage 1, Stage 2a, Stage 2b, Stage 2c, Stage 3, Stage TC) — Stage TC was first to surface the bug because its isolated-call attention budget makes it more prone to preamble leak; one helper change covers all six call sites with no stage-specific work needed. Verified across 7 test shapes: bare JSON, markdown-fenced JSON, Sherpa-shape preamble + fenced JSON, empty, null, non-JSON garbage, embedded-brace strings — 7/7 PASS. Pure additive upgrade — every input the old parser handled correctly still parses identically; only previously-failing inputs (prose preamble) now succeed. Live verification post-deploy: Sherpa input on Pro pipeline now produces clean TC score with no Vercel parse error; user's IdeaLoop self-eval (4k characters) remains clean as regression check. **TC scoring logic + reasoning structure NOT changed by this fix — locked off-limits per active TC monitoring directive (anchor-fixing bug from B6 surfaced; TC scoring math + reasoning structure stay locked until dedicated TC fix session).** Output format hardening at prompt level (e.g., explicit "do not echo reasoning steps" instruction in `prompt-stage-tc.js`) deferred to that future session — current parser fix is sufficient to make any future leak user-invisible. Original "G1-LONG silent failure" deferred item from B9 v2 closure is hereby reclassified: it was not a Stage 2b silent truncation (the max_tokens 4096→8192 bump from B9 v2 deployment did not fix it because that wasn't the actual root cause); it was Stage TC parse fragility on prose-preamble-leak failure mode. The "G1-LONG silent failure" name is closed; Sherpa input added to deferred B10a regression bank as G1-LONG-1500W stress case for future regression coverage.** **B9 closure summary (V4S28 B9 fully closed May 4, 2026):** Three sub-bundles shipped this session — archetype coverage authoring + thin_dimensions hygiene + B6 catch-up commit + Stage TC parse hardening. What V2 Does (Deployed)

- Haiku keyword extraction (claude-haiku-4-5-20251001) before main analysis
- GitHub API + Serper.dev API for real competitor data (4 parallel searches)
- Real competitor data injected into Sonnet prompt
- Frontend shows source badges (GitHub/Google/AI) on competitor cards
- Clickable URLs on real competitors
- Green "Verified Sources" badge when real data found, yellow AI warning when not
- Classification tag on analysis screen (e.g., Commercial Product, Social Impact)
- Screen restructure: Competition + Evaluation on Screen 3, Build Plan on Screen 4
- Single Sonnet call produces all sections at once (competition, phases, tools, scores)
- Evaluation limits: legacy — being replaced by credit system (see Section 6)

What V3 Adds (Deployed)

- Supabase backend: PostgreSQL database with Row Level Security
- User authentication: email/password signup and login via Supabase Auth
- Auth modal on page.js, session listener, login/logout controls on all screen headers
- Profile dual-write: localStorage + Supabase profiles table
- localStorage profile auto-migrates to database on first login
- Profile saves go through /api/profile server route (RLS fix)
- Save evaluations: logged-in users see 'Save to My Ideas' button on Build Plan screen
- Saving creates idea row + evaluation row in database as full JSON snapshot
- Unauthenticated users see 'Sign up to save your evaluations' prompt
- Free tier cap: being replaced by credit system (see Section 6)
- My Ideas Hub: lists saved ideas with score circle, title, date, classification tag, verified badge, mini score bars, summary preview
- Click any card in My Ideas to reopen full evaluation from database
- Soft-delete (archive) instead of hard delete
- Progress tracking: roadmap checkboxes and notes per saved idea (uses progress table)
- Checkboxes and notes only appear when viewing saved ideas from My Ideas, NOT during first-time evaluation
- Progress summary bar with completion count on Build Plan screen
- Mini progress indicators on My Ideas hub cards (completed/total phases)
- Evaluation limits migrated from localStorage to database for logged-in users (uses eval_usage table)
- Context-aware language for saved vs new evaluations
- My Ideas link appears in header on ALL screens for logged-in users
- 'IDEALOOP CORE' title is clickable on all screens (navigates home)
- Dev reset endpoint at /api/dev/reset-evals
- Unique constraint on progress table for upserts
- Idea naming on save with pre-filled first sentence and Cancel button

What V4 Session 9 Adds (Deployed)

The Stage 2a/2b split: Stage 2 split into Stage 2a (metric-bounded evidence extraction) + Stage 2b (scoring from packets only). Physically prevents cross-metric contamination by delivering only admissible evidence per metric to the scoring step.

What V4 Session 10 Adds (DEPLOYED — March 31, 2026)

TC ISOLATION: TC pulled completely out of Stage 2a/2b into its own dedicated Sonnet call. TC never sees Stage 1 output, evidence packets, competition data, or domain flags.

Pipeline: Stage 1 → [Stage 2a + Stage TC in parallel] → Stage 2b → Assembly → Stage 3
- Stage TC: idea + profile only. Battle-tested TC rubric. max_tokens: 1000. Parallel with Stage 2a.
- Stage 2a: extracts 3 packets (MD, MO, OR) — no TC packet.
- Stage 2b: scores MD, MO, OR from packets — does not score TC.
- Assembly: merges TC score from Stage TC into evaluation before Stage 3.

V4S10-TC test results (3 independent runs):
- OR-TC: 0.342, 0.414, 0.338 (average 0.365). Down from 0.759 baseline and 0.499-0.579 pre-isolation range. CONFIRMED FIXED.
- Double-counting: 0/34 across all three runs. STABLE.
- Health Companion OR: 6.0, 6.5, 6.0 (PRO). Never returned to old 7.5 inflation. STABLE.
- TC distribution: 6 unique values, spread from 6.5 to 9.0. No clustering. HEALTHY.
- Pipeline speed: PRO averaging ~134s. ACCEPTABLE.
- MD-MO average: 0.533 across 3 runs. Higher than the single-run 0.031 outlier but within natural overlap range. The "almost perfect" V4S10 numbers were partly noise at n=17.
- MD-OR average: 0.542 across 3 runs. Same pattern — single-run outliers do not represent steady state.

CALIBRATION VERDICT: Pipeline is at "acceptably calibrated product baseline" status. Remaining correlations are in the "natural conceptual overlap + small-sample variance" zone. Further offline prompt calibration has reached diminishing returns. Next improvements come from real user feedback, not more test suite runs.

Pro pipeline is 5 Sonnet calls total. Stage TC runs parallel with Stage 2a, so wall time ~120-160s.

What V4 Session 11 Adds (DEPLOYED — April 2, 2026)

SIDE-BY-SIDE COMPARISON: First core workflow feature. Lets users compare two saved evaluations from My Ideas hub.

Architecture:
- ComparisonView.js: separate component file (~530 lines). Contains prepareComparisonData(), 6 screen components. Competitors/Risks/Scores/Tools use CSS Grid; Roadmap uses independent flex columns.
- page.js: thin comparison mode toggle. States: compareSelected, compareSelecting, compareMode, compareData, compareLoading.
- Entry point: "Compare Ideas" button in My Ideas Hub → selection mode with checkboxes → user taps 2 ideas → Compare button → loads both via GET /api/ideas/[id] in parallel.
- No new API routes needed — uses existing GET endpoint.

Comparison screens (6 total, navigated sequentially):
1. Competitors — grid-row aligned, shared competitor detection with blue border + "Shared" badge
2. Scores — grid-row aligned (same metric at same vertical position), green up/red down arrows
3. Key Risks — grid-row aligned, failure_risks side by side
4. Roadmap — independent flex columns with minHeight-matched cards, expandable phase details expand independently per column
5. Tools & Estimates — grid-row aligned per tool card within categories, category headers aligned, duration/difficulty pinned at bottom
6. Key Tradeoffs — synthesis screen showing winner + loser per metric with first-sentence extractions, overall decision summary. NOTED: needs redesign to be more decision-useful (currently just restates score differences). Will be rebuilt in V4S17.

Desktop: two-column side-by-side. Mobile: tab toggle (Idea A / Idea B).

Data pipeline bugs found and fixed:
- failure_risks and confidence_level were never persisted to scoring_json in save route or re-evaluate route (added to both)
- GET /api/ideas/[id] was not extracting failure_risks or confidence_level from scoring_json when reconstructing analysis object (added to reconstruction)
- Codex reverted the GET route fix mid-session — had to be re-applied in V4S12
- NOTE: Ideas saved BEFORE this fix do not have failure_risks in the database. Must re-evaluate to populate.

What V4 Session 12 Adds (COMPLETE — April 2, 2026)

COMPARISON VISUAL POLISH: All 6 comparison screens refined for consistent row-aligned equal-height layouts.

Changes:
- Competitors: switched from TwoCol (flex) to CSS Grid with display:contents. Each competitor pair sits in its own grid row with equal-height cards.
- Key Risks: switched from TwoCol to CSS Grid. Each risk pair row-aligned with equal height.
- Roadmap: switched from CSS Grid to two independent flex columns. Cards use minHeight:120 so all collapsed cards appear identical height. Columns are fully independent — expanding a phase on one side does NOT affect the other side.
- Tools & Estimates: completely restructured. Each individual tool card now gets its own grid row (not all tools per category in one cell). Category headers get their own grid rows. Duration/Difficulty pinned as final grid row.
- GET /api/ideas/[id]/route.js: re-applied failure_risks and confidence_level extraction that Codex had reverted.
- TwoCol component is now dead code (defined but unused by any screen). Can be cleaned up later.

Layout pattern per screen:
- Competitors, Key Risks, Scores, Tools: CSS Grid with display:contents, display:flex on cells, height:100% on cards. No horizontal grid lines, only vertical center divider.
- Roadmap: Two independent flex columns (not grid). Cards use minHeight:120 for visual alignment. Fully independent expand/collapse.


2. Scoring Formula

**V4S28 B8 (May 1, 2026) — TC removed from Overall composite. New weights re-normalized to sum to 1.0:**

Overall = MD × 0.375 + MO × 0.3125 + OR × 0.3125

- Market Demand (MD): 37.5% — is the demand real, capturable, and recurring for a new entrant?
- Monetization (MO): 31.25% — can revenue be extracted from that demand?
- Originality (OR): 31.25% — can the position be defended against incumbents?
- Technical Complexity (TC): NOT IN OVERALL — framed as "execution context · build difficulty"; remains a first-class metric with its own rubric and isolated Stage TC scoring call. UI displays TC alongside the Overall but visually separated by an "EXECUTION CONTEXT · NOT IN THE OVERALL" divider.

**Rationale for α change:** TC measures something different in kind (build difficulty against the founder's profile) from MD/MO/OR (idea quality against the market). Bundling TC into the Overall produced silent score compression — most ideas score TC 6-8 (audit data), creating a constant 1.2-1.6 point drag on Overall — without adding explanatory power. TC's value is now communicated through its own framed surface rather than being silently weighted into the composite.

**Pre-B8 historical formula (preserved for context):** `Overall = MD × 0.30 + MO × 0.25 + OR × 0.25 + (10 - TC) × 0.20`

Calculated in JavaScript (scoring.js), not by the LLM. Score is deterministic given the three metric inputs (MD, MO, OR). TC is calculated separately by Stage TC and rendered alongside but not summed into Overall.

**Score tier labels (V31-style: Strong Opportunity / Viable but Competitive / etc.) — KILLED.** Decision in V4S26b: most ideas land 4.0-6.0, making fixed tier labels repetitive after multiple evaluations. Score Guide popup retained as the user-facing interpretation surface (triggered by ⓘ button next to Overall in the C-2 layout).

POSITIVE CONTROL TESTING (COMPLETE):
12+ ideas tested by Claude and ChatGPT attempting to score 7+. None achieved it. Both LLMs independently concluded: "Your evaluator is working." 95% of startup ideas should land between 4.5-6.2.

=== CORRELATION TRACKING ACROSS RUNS ===

V4S11 (OR content filter): MD-MO: 0.355, MD-OR: 0.403, MD-TC: 0.392, MO-OR: 0.077, MO-TC: 0.308, OR-TC: 0.499

CALIBRATION COMPLETE. Use 3-run or 5-run medians for future comparisons, not single-run snapshots.

PRE-SHIP BUILD ORDER RATIONALE (V33 — updated April 13, 2026):
The dependency chain: Rubric affects output quality → output quality determines what's worth showing in free vs pro → free/pro split determines what Paddle gates → Paddle determines what the landing page can promise. Nothing in this order forces looking back.

Rubric adjustment (step 15) is COMPLETE. Testing pass (step 16) is COMPLETE. Free vs Pro implementation is COMPLETE (V4S22-S25). Free preview philosophy shift deployed (V4S26a). Subscriber UI polish deployed (V4S26b). UI Polish (step 18) COMPLETE. Next: dark theme identity redesign (new session), then product content audit (step 19).

Steps 19-21 form a "product investigation block" — a full audit of the product section by section, then visually, then technically. This block sits between polish and payment because the landing page needs to screenshot and reference a finalized product. The investigation may surface small fixes, but should not introduce new features.

Step 22 (user feedback) sits after the investigation block and before Paddle because it's a trust-recovery feature that must exist before charging users.

V4 WORKFLOW UPGRADE (Items 8-13): These six features form one cohesive workflow upgrade designed and sequenced as a unit. They transform the product from an evaluator into a structured idea evolution environment. The full design rationale and detailed execution plan are in the separate V4_Workflow_Execution_Plan.md document. ALL 6 SESSIONS COMPLETE (V4S13-V4S18). Key conceptual shifts: "alternatives" become "branches" (strategic descendants), the re-evaluation screen becomes an idea evolution entry point with post-evaluation decision block, delta explanation uses explicit change metadata (not just two evals), Key Tradeoffs becomes a Sonnet synthesis call over structured comparison deltas, decision status labels on lineage nodes for idea triage.

BUILD ORDER RATIONALE: Workflow features (comparison, branching, lineage, delta, tradeoffs) are built BEFORE payment integration because they are the retention engine. If payment is added before the workflow exists, users pay for deeper evaluation only — a weaker value proposition. Building workflow first means when Paddle is integrated, the paid tier already includes the full workspace experience. Payment wraps around completed features, not incomplete ones.

PAYMENT PROVIDER: Paddle (merchant of record). NOT Stripe (not available in Turkey). Paddle handles checkout, sales tax/VAT, global payment methods (cards, PayPal, Apple Pay, Google Pay), chargebacks, and tax compliance. ~5% + $0.50 per transaction. Paddle products: 3 credit packs ($10/$20/$30) + 1 pro monthly subscription ($20/month).

=== V5 — LAUNCH ===
Product Hunt, content marketing, community distribution. First real users.
Free tier: 2 lifetime Standard Analysis previews with partial content gating. Deep Analysis is paid-only at launch. Free Deep deferred to post-launch conversion experiment if needed.

=== V6 — SCALE OR PIVOT ===
Based on V5 data: B2B teams, deeper individual product, platform play, or portfolio piece.
Validation-ready outreach pack / market test kit — PARKED (good strategic fit but not foundational; build after core workflow is stable).


5. Decisions Made (Locked In)

Architecture Decisions:
- Frontend split across page.js (hub, input, profile, reeval, delta + state management), EvaluationView.js (analysis + buildplan screens), components.js (8 shared UI primitives), ComparisonView.js, LineageView.js
- Server-side score calculation in JS, not LLM
- Inline styles over Tailwind
- Temperature 0 for consistent scoring
- Ethics filter blocks deception, illegal activity, and harm
- Evidence layer (real API data) free for ALL users
- Supabase for auth and database with Row Level Security
- Save button on Build Plan screen (user sees full evaluation before deciding)
- Soft-delete (archive) for ideas
- Progress tracking as mutable layer on immutable snapshots
- Evaluation limits: transitioning from weekly cap to credit system

V3.5 Scoring Decisions (Locked In):
- Demand rubric scores demand-after-friction with 6 anti-inflation categories
- Monetization rubric scores first-dollar realism, not theoretical revenue models
- Originality rubric scores structural defensibility, not narrative novelty
- Score-explanation cross-check enforced per metric and globally
- TC is the ONLY metric using user profile
- Confidence level per evaluation (HIGH/MEDIUM/LOW)
- Failure risks per evaluation (2-3 specific risks)

V4 Session 9 Decisions (Locked In):
- Stage 2 split into 2a (evidence extraction) + 2b (scoring) to physically prevent cross-metric contamination
- Stage 2a is a quarantine layer — sorter, not analyst
- Evidence packets use source tags: [competitor: Name], [domain_flag], [idea_description], [narrative_field]
- Narrative_field is LOWEST TRUST
- MD-MO tiebreaker: adoption-vs-payment test
- Anti-seriousness rule: domain seriousness is not a scoring input
- Evidence quality rule: sparse/weak evidence biases downward, not toward center

V4 Session 10 Decisions (Locked In):
- TC scored in its own isolated Sonnet call — never sees Stage 1 output, competition data, or domain flags
- Stage 2a extracts 3 packets only (MD, MO, OR) — no TC packet
- Stage 2b scores 3 metrics only (MD, MO, OR) — does not score TC
- Stage TC runs in parallel with Stage 2a via Promise.all — no added latency
- TC rubric preserved verbatim from battle-tested Stage 2 prompt
- MD-OR independence check in Stage 2b (Scoring Rule 7)
- Physical separation beats prompt rules — learned from entire V4S7-S11 calibration history
- Prompt-level OR-TC tightening has reached diminishing returns with collateral damage — do not attempt further prompt fixes for this pair
- When correlations at n=17 fluctuate in the 0.3-0.5 range across runs with zero prompt changes, that's noise not signal
- Pipeline calibration is COMPLETE — ship as product baseline, monitor with real users, use 3-run medians for any future comparisons

V4 Session 11 Decisions (Locked In — April 2, 2026):
- Comparison uses 6 screens navigated sequentially: Competitors → Scores → Key risks → Roadmap → Tools & Estimates → Key tradeoffs
- Desktop: two-column side-by-side. Mobile: tab toggle (Idea A / Idea B).
- Score arrows (green up / red down) on Scores screen ONLY — other screens are qualitative
- Scores screen uses grid-row alignment so metrics stay at same vertical position. Other screens use independent columns flowing naturally.
- Shared competitors highlighted with blue border + "Shared" badge
- Key Tradeoffs screen shows both winner AND loser per metric with first-sentence extractions. Label: "Key tradeoffs" (not "Summary").
- Entry: "Compare Ideas" button in My Ideas Hub → selection mode with checkboxes → tap 2 ideas → Compare
- ComparisonView is a separate component file. page.js has a thin comparison mode toggle.
- prepareComparisonData() computes everything once before rendering: shared competitors, score deltas, first-sentence extractions, overall summary
- failure_risks and confidence_level now persisted in scoring_json across all save paths (save route, re-evaluate route, GET route reconstruction)

V4 Session 12 Decisions (Locked In — April 2, 2026):
- (Unchanged from V23)

V4 Session 13 Decisions (Locked In — April 6, 2026):
- compareSelected stores {ideaId, evaluationId} objects, not plain IDs
- Re-eval screen renamed to "Evolve This Idea" with context snapshot, edit-toggle fields, post-eval decision block
- Post-eval decision block: Save as branch + Discard (Set as main deferred to V4S14)
- Change metadata (changed_fields array) stored in meta_json for delta explanation
- Backend unchanged in V4S13 — "Save as branch" temporarily used existing re-evaluate route

V4 Session 14 Decisions (Locked In — April 6, 2026):
- Branches are first-class idea objects: own idea row with parent_idea_id, own evaluations, own progress, own comparison eligibility
- Branch creation requires intentional friction: name (required), reason (required text), changed dimensions (at least one from 6 options: target_user, problem, wedge, monetization, gtm, core_concept)
- "Save as branch" now calls POST /api/ideas/[id]/branch (no longer uses re-evaluate route for branches)
- "Set as main version" uses PATCH /api/ideas/[id]/set-main — walks lineage to root, clears all is_main_version in tree, sets target to true
- Children count computed client-side from myIdeas array (no extra DB query)
- RLS automatic — every idea row has user_id, existing policies handle branches
- Existing alternatives in database untouched — alternatives popup still works for pre-V4S14 data

V4 Session 15 Decisions (Locked In — April 6, 2026):
- Lineage View is a separate component file (LineageView.js) imported by page.js — same pattern as ComparisonView.js
- Tree built entirely client-side from myIdeas array — no new API endpoint needed for v1
- Root finding: walks parent_idea_id chain up to NULL. Tree building: recursive nested structure from flat list.
- Org-chart layout uses CSS flex connectors (div-based, not pseudo-elements) — compatible with inline CSS convention
- Checkboxes hidden by default. "Compare" button at bottom enters compare mode → checkboxes appear → select 2 → "Compare Selected" → Cancel exits
- startComparison() accepts optional selectionsOverride parameter to avoid async state race from lineage comparison
- "View lineage" button appears on hub cards that have parent_idea_id or children (purple text, in delete row area)
- v1 is FUNCTIONAL ONLY — Emre has a specific mockup for the polished tree (centered layout, glowing blue dot connectors, glass cards, comparison-active state badges). Visual polish is a SEPARATE future pass after workflow features are validated. Do not attempt to upgrade the tree visual in workflow sessions.
- Lineage view v1 deferred items: collapsible nodes, drag-drop, branch merge, automatic branch suggestions, polished tree visualization

V4 Session 16 Decisions (Locked In — April 7, 2026):
- Hub filtering: only root ideas (parent_idea_id === null) and current main branches (is_main_version === true) display in My Ideas hub. All other branches are accessed exclusively through the lineage view.
- Save counter: only counts root ideas toward the save limit (branches don't count). Uses .is("parent_idea_id", null) filter on Supabase query.
- Compare button threshold: uses filtered hub count (roots + mains), not total myIdeas count.
- Delta explanation is a dedicated Sonnet call, fully isolated from the main evaluation pipeline. NOT the same as comparison tradeoffs — delta is directional change attribution (parent → child), comparison is symmetric tradeoff synthesis (A vs B).
- Delta prompt uses 4-block output: change_summary, improvements[], worsenings[], net_interpretation. Each improvement/worsening carries a causal sentence, metric, numerical delta, and attribution confidence (direct/indirect/ambiguous).
- Score direction is NOT quality direction — the prompt explicitly instructs Sonnet that a lower-scoring branch can be strategically superior. Net interpretation must evaluate strategic clarity, not just numbers.
- Delta results cached in meta_json.delta_result on the evaluation row. First view triggers Sonnet call, subsequent views return cached result.
- Delta is on-demand ("See what changed" button), not auto-generated on every branch save.
- Delta screen is Screen 5 (after Roadmap), only visible when viewing a branch. StepProgress shows "Delta" as step 5 for branches, "Evolve" as step 5 for non-branches.
- Branch ideas on Roadmap screen show three buttons: Evolve this idea → See what changed → ← Back to My Ideas. Delta screen also has its own Evolve button. Users can re-evaluate from either screen without being forced through the delta.
- Action buttons (Evolve, Set as main, Back to My Ideas) appear on both the Roadmap screen and the Delta screen for branches. This allows users who already know what changed to skip delta and go straight to evolving.
- fetchMyIdeas() now called after branch-save-with-set-main flow to ensure lineage view reflects main version changes immediately.

V4 Session 17 Decisions (Locked In — April 7, 2026):
- Key Tradeoffs is a dedicated Sonnet call, fully isolated from the main evaluation pipeline and from the delta explanation prompt. Tradeoffs = symmetric comparison synthesis (A vs B, "what am I choosing between?"). Delta = directional change attribution (parent → child, "what did my change do?"). These are DISTINCT features with different prompts and different cognitive jobs.
- Tradeoffs prompt asks for 3-5 decision-relevant tensions, not screen-by-screen recaps. Each tradeoff must name what you GAIN and what you SACRIFICE for each idea.
- Input is a preprocessed structured object built by buildTradeoffsPayload() in ComparisonView.js — NOT raw evaluation JSON or screen text. Includes: scores, deltas, failure risks, confidence, competitor counts/types, shared competitors, risk summaries, execution estimates (duration, difficulty, phase count).
- Dominance threshold is strict: dominant_idea is only set when one idea wins on 3+ dimensions AND losses are minor (delta < 0.5). Most comparisons should return dominant_idea: null.
- Background fetch: Sonnet tradeoffs call fires on ComparisonView mount so result is ready by the time user reaches screen 6. Cached in React state per session (client-side only, no server-side caching).
- Error fallback: if tradeoffs call fails, shows simplified score comparison instead of breaking the screen.
- Auth token passed from page.js to ComparisonView via compareData.authToken prop.
- Hub Compare button fix: onClick handler changed from onClick={startComparison} to onClick={() => startComparison()} to prevent click event being passed as selectionsOverride.

V4 Session 18 Decisions (Locked In — April 8, 2026):
- Decision status labels: Exploring (blue) / Lead (green) / Parked (gray) / Killed (red). Discussed and locked before implementation.
- Status badges appear on Lineage View nodes ONLY — not on hub cards. Status is a lineage-level navigation/triage tool, not a hub-level one.
- status_label column is separate from status column. status = system visibility (active/archived). status_label = user-facing decision state.
- Default status for all ideas (new and existing): 'exploring'.
- Each idea has its own independent status_label — no inheritance from parent.
- PATCH /api/ideas/[id] is a single route handling both status_label and title updates. Validates status against allowed list, validates title non-empty.
- Idea renaming: pen icon (✏️) next to title on both hub cards and lineage nodes. Inline input on click, save on Enter/blur, cancel on Escape.
- updateIdea() in page.js does optimistic local update via setMyIdeas, then PATCH call.
- TwoCol dead code cleaned from ComparisonView.js. No other dead code found.
- V4 workflow upgrade sequence declared COMPLETE with this session.

V23 Workflow Upgrade Decisions (Locked In — April 5, 2026):

Conceptual model:
- "Alternatives" as a concept is retired. Replaced by "branches" — strategic descendants of an idea.
- Every saved idea is a lineage root. Branches are child ideas linked by parent_idea_id.
- Re-evaluation stays as an action ("run a new evaluation pass") but is NOT a major storage category. After evaluation, user decides how the result enters the system.
- Two distinct idea-evolution operations: Re-evaluate (same node, new reading) and Create Branch (new strategic descendant node). These are different mental acts and must feel different in UI.
- A branch is justified when at least one of these changes materially: target user, core problem, value proposition/wedge, monetization logic, market entry path.
- Branches are first-class idea objects: own evaluation, own progress, own re-evaluations, own further branching, own comparison eligibility, visible parent link.

Re-evaluation screen redesign:
- Renamed from "Re-evaluate with changes" to "Evolve This Idea" or "Create New Version"
- Screen structure: (1) Context snapshot — scores, weakest metric, top risks, (2) Editable fields showing current values — target user, problem, core idea, (3) Evaluate button, (4) Post-evaluation decision block
- Post-evaluation decision block offers: Save as branch (keep alongside parent) / Set as main version (promote this as primary direction, preserve old in history) / Discard (don't save)

Branching data model:
- Add parent_idea_id (nullable FK to ideas), branch_reason (text), changed_dimensions (JSONB) to ideas table
- "Save as branch" creates a new idea row with parent_idea_id pointing to source idea — NOT a nested alternative
- Branch-of-branch supported in data model from day one
- "Set as main version" adds is_main_version flag on ideas table — a flag, not a separate object. Original root never disappears.

Hub display rules (V4S16):
- Hub shows root ideas + current main branches ONLY. Everything else: lineage view only.
- Each card shows its own score. Root card keeps "View lineage" button and branch count indicator.
- When main changes: old main loses is_main_version flag → disappears from hub → becomes regular branch in lineage tree. New main appears in hub.
- If old main is deleted: archived, gone from tree entirely.

Lineage view:
- V4S15 is "Lineage view v1" — functional, not polished visual payoff
- Must prove: lineage is readable, node relationships are correct, comparison can select from nodes, users understand root/branch/main
- Visual polish comes in a later pass

Delta explanation:
- Input MUST include: parent evaluation, child evaluation, explicit changed fields, branch reason, and changed_dimensions
- Without change metadata, Sonnet may infer wrong causal story. The changed fields are the causal spine.
- Delta is grounded attribution ("your narrowed target user improved monetization but reduced demand"), not correlation guessing
- Comparison (symmetric: A vs B, "what am I choosing between?") and Delta (directional: parent → child, "what did my change actually do?") are DISTINCT features with different prompts. Do not blur them.

Key Tradeoffs redesign:
- Rebuilt as a separate Sonnet call over structured comparison deltas — NOT screen-by-screen recaps
- Prompt asks for 3-5 decision-relevant tensions, not "what is notable on each screen"
- Input: preprocessed structured object (metric deltas, competitor asymmetry, risk asymmetry, roadmap asymmetry, execution burden, time/difficulty)
- Constraint: no external advice, no inferred market facts, nothing not present in comparison data, prioritize tensions/asymmetries/sacrifices
- Triggered from compare view, fed only normalized comparison JSON, fully separated from main eval pipeline

Decision status labels:
- Built as final workflow feature (V4S18) after all other workflow features exist.
- Labels: Exploring (blue) / Lead (green) / Parked (gray) / Killed (red)
- Displayed on Lineage View nodes only, not hub cards
- Tappable badge → dropdown to change status

V4 Session 1-5 Decisions: (Locked In, unchanged from V19)
V3.5 Session 2-3 Decisions: (Locked In, unchanged from V19)

- Quick Scan Mode. Deferred indefinitely.
- ChatGPT structural suggestions (Monte Carlo, founder psych modeling). Rejected.
- Guided input sub-question fields. Killed.
- Prompt-level OR-TC separation attempts. Killed — replaced by architectural TC isolation.
- Old "3 free per week" model. Killed — replaced by 2 lifetime free evaluations + credit system (V4S26a formalized).
- Old "$12/month flat subscription" model. Killed — replaced by credit + subscription hybrid.
- Idea branching as a SEPARATE standalone feature with idea_branches junction table. Killed — replaced by parent_idea_id on ideas table. Branches are ideas, not a separate entity type.
- "Alternatives" as a UI/conceptual category. Retired — replaced by branches in the lineage model. Existing alternative data remains in database under parent ideas.

8. Infrastructure

- GitHub: starmind-dev
- Vercel: idealoop-core (primary: idealoopcore.com, legacy: idea-validator-pink-zeta.vercel.app)
- Website: emreyildiz.dev (needs updating)
- Supabase: connected, PostgreSQL live

Environment Variables:
- ANTHROPIC_API_KEY, GITHUB_TOKEN, SERPER_API_KEY
- NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL, NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY, SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY
- Paddle keys: TBD (sandbox first, then live after verification)

API Limits:
- Serper: Limited free queries remaining. Must switch to paid plan before V5 launch.
- GitHub: 5,000 requests/hour with token. Effectively unlimited.
- Anthropic: Pay per token. Sonnet ~$3/MTok input, ~$15/MTok output. Pro pipeline = 5 Sonnet calls (Stage TC parallel with Stage 2a). Delta = 1 additional Sonnet call per branch (first view only, then cached). Tradeoffs = 1 additional Sonnet call per comparison (cached in React state per session).
- Vercel: Free tier 10s timeout. Pro needed for pipeline.
- Supabase: Free tier generous.

Database Schema (Built):
- profiles, ideas, evaluations, progress, eval_usage — all with Row Level Security
- ideas table: parent_idea_id (UUID FK nullable), branch_reason (TEXT), changed_dimensions (JSONB), is_main_version (BOOLEAN DEFAULT false) — added V4S14. status_label (TEXT DEFAULT 'exploring') — added V4S18.
- Index: idx_ideas_parent_idea_id on ideas(parent_idea_id) WHERE parent_idea_id IS NOT NULL
- evaluations table: meta_json stores changed_fields (V4S13), delta_result cache (V4S16)
- Credit/payment tables: TBD (designed during Paddle integration session)

API Routes (Built):
- ~~POST /api/analyze (light tier — current free pipeline)~~ **RETIRED V80:** the free `/api/analyze` route was DELETED; Deep (`/api/analyze-pro`) is now the default analysis endpoint.
- POST /api/analyze-pro (pro tier — Stage 1 → [Stage 2a + Stage TC parallel] → Stage 2b → Stage 3)
- POST /api/ideas/save (V4S11: now persists failure_risks and confidence_level in scoring_json)
- GET /api/ideas/list
- GET /api/ideas/[id] (supports ?evaluation_id=X) (V4S11: now extracts failure_risks and confidence_level from scoring_json)
- DELETE /api/ideas/[id]
- PATCH /api/ideas/[id] (V4S18: updates status_label and/or title on idea row)
- POST /api/ideas/[id]/re-evaluate (V4S11: now persists failure_risks and confidence_level in scoring_json)
- PATCH /api/progress
- GET /api/eval-usage, POST /api/eval-usage
- POST /api/profile
- POST /api/dev/reset-evals
- Payment/credit routes: TBD (Paddle webhooks + credit balance API)
- POST /api/ideas/[id]/branch (V4S14: creates new idea row with parent link + evaluation row)
- PATCH /api/ideas/[id]/set-main (V4S14: sets is_main_version on target, clears on rest of lineage)
- POST /api/ideas/[id]/delta (V4S16: loads parent + child evaluations, calls Sonnet with delta prompt, caches result in meta_json.delta_result)
- POST /api/compare/tradeoffs (V4S17: receives preprocessed comparison object, calls Sonnet with tradeoffs prompt, returns tradeoff synthesis — no DB interaction)

Prompt Files:
- src/lib/services/prompt-stage1.js — Stage 1 (competition discovery)
- src/lib/services/prompt-stage2a.js — Stage 2a (evidence extraction) — V4S20: sparse input rule, [user_claim] source tag, MD packet user-claim exclusion, cross-packet verification item 8
- src/lib/services/prompt-stage2b.js — Stage 2b (scoring from packets) — V4S20: OR actionability soft suggestion (CORRECTED V42: this was DROPPED somewhere between V4S20 and B1 — verified missing pre-B4 — V4S28 B4 reintroduced as enforced two-element required structure with anti-generic guardrail + honest exit). Summary tone calibration moved to Stage 2c by V4S28 B1 architectural split.
- src/lib/services/prompt-stage-tc.js — Stage TC (isolated TC scoring)
- src/lib/services/prompt-stage3.js — Stage 3 (roadmap, tools, estimates)
- ~~src/lib/services/prompt.js — Free tier single-call prompt (V4S20 sparse-input + scoring-rule-8 + summary-tone; V4S28 B4 evidence_strength + Option Z MEDIUM)~~ **RETIRED V80:** `prompt.js` / `SYSTEM_PROMPT_BASE` was DELETED with the free pipeline (free-exclusive, 3 refs all in the free route).
- src/app/api/prompts/prompt-delta.js — Delta explanation (V4S16: 4-block causal attribution)
- src/app/api/prompts/prompt-tradeoffs.js — Tradeoffs synthesis (V4S17: symmetric comparison, 3-5 decision-relevant tensions)

Frontend Files:
- src/app/page.js — main app with hub, input, profile, reeval, delta screens + all state management + entitlement system (V4S23). Delegates analysis/buildplan rendering to EvaluationView. ~3590 lines (V4S24a: reduced from ~5740 via extraction).
- src/app/EvaluationView.js — (V4S24a) — analysis screen (results1) + buildplan screen (results2) rendering. Receives ~65 props from page.js including state, setters, and 5 wrapper callbacks (onResetAndNewIdea, onBackToMyIdeasCleanup, onDiscardReEval, onSetAsMain, onNavigateToDelta). ~1860 lines.
- src/app/components.js — (V4S24a) — 8 shared UI primitives: StepProgress, StatusBadge, ScoreBar, SectionHeader, Card, PageContainer, AuthModal, DevModeBadge. Imported by both page.js and EvaluationView.js. ~480 lines.
- src/app/ComparisonView.js — (V4S11+V4S12+V4S17+V4S19) — comparison component with 6 screens, ~705 lines. Screens 1-5 use CSS Grid + flex. Screen 6 (Key Tradeoffs) is Sonnet-powered synthesis with background fetch on mount. Includes buildTradeoffsPayload() preprocessor. Estimates height-matched in V4S19.
- src/app/LineageView.js — (V4S15+V4S18+V4S19) — lineage tree component, ~580 lines, org-chart layout with CSS flex connectors, compare mode toggle, status badges with dropdown, inline rename, loading spinner on clicked nodes

10. Known Issues

RESOLVED — CALIBRATION COMPLETE (V4S10-TC, 3 independent runs):
- OR-TC correlation: 0.759 → 0.365 average across 3 runs. FIXED architecturally via TC isolation.
- MD-MO correlation: stabilized at ~0.5 average. The single-run 0.031 was an outlier, not steady state. Current level is natural conceptual overlap + small-sample noise.
- Double-counting: 0/34 across all three runs. ROCK SOLID.
- Health Companion OR: consistently 6.0-6.5 in PRO. Never returned to 7.5. STABLE.
- TC distribution: 6 unique values, 6.5-9.0 spread. No clustering at 7.5. HEALTHY.
- Stage 1 narrative contamination: 0-3/17 across all runs. STABLE.

UNCHANGED:
- PRO PIPELINE SPEED: ~120-160s with parallel Stage TC. Acceptable for paid tier.
- Serper limited free queries remaining. Must switch to paid before launch.
- emreyildiz.dev claims Product Hunt integration that doesn't exist.
- Score variance of ~0.5-0.7 points across runs is expected behavior.
- FREE tier MD-MO correlation consistently high (0.46-0.91 across runs). Property of single-call architecture — acceptable for light tier.

RESOLVED (V22 — Comparison Visual Polish):
- SCORE BAR OVERFLOW: Fixed.
- ROADMAP CARD OVERFLOW: Fixed.
- ROADMAP EXPAND INDEPENDENCE: Fixed.
- TOOLS CATEGORY MISALIGNMENT: Fixed.
- KEY RISKS DISPLAY: Fixed.
- CODEX GET ROUTE REVERT: Fixed.
- NOTE: Ideas saved before the failure_risks fix still need re-evaluation to populate risks.

RESOLVED (V26 — Hub Filtering):
- "6 of 5 ideas saved" counter: Fixed. Save counter now only counts root ideas (branches excluded). Hub only displays roots + current main branches.
- Lineage tree not updating after set-main: Fixed. fetchMyIdeas() now called after branch-save-with-set-main flow.

RESOLVED (V27 — Key Tradeoffs + Hub Compare Fix):
- Key Tradeoffs screen: rebuilt from static score restatement to Sonnet-powered tradeoff synthesis. Now produces decision-relevant tensions, not score recaps.
- Hub Compare button: was passing click event as selectionsOverride, causing function to bail. Fixed to arrow function. Pre-existing bug, not introduced in V4S17.

RESOLVED (V28 — Status Labels + Cleanup):
- TwoCol dead code: removed from ComparisonView.js. Was defined but unused since V4S12.

RESOLVED (V29 — Bug Fixes + Performance Polish):
- Status label not persisting: ideas/list route was not selecting status_label from database. Fixed by adding status_label to select query.
- Screen flash on lineage → idea navigation: lineage mode exited before async fetch completed, showing hub briefly. Fixed by making callbacks async — lineage stays visible until data loads.
- Screen flash on lineage → comparison: same pattern, same fix.
- Profile screen flash on page refresh: default currentScreen was "profile", visible during auth resolution. Fixed with auth loading gate that shows minimal screen until auth resolves.
- Comparison estimates unequal height: duration/difficulty cards in Tools & Estimates screen not stretching to match. Fixed with height:100% on estimates wrapper and display:flex on grid cells.
- Delta re-analyzing on every revisit: deltaData was cleared on navigation. Added client-side delta cache in evaluationCacheRef — repeat views are instant within session.
- Evaluation re-fetching on every click: added evaluationCacheRef (useRef) to cache loaded evaluations in memory — repeat visits to same idea within session are instant.
- Loading spinner added to lineage nodes: clicked node shows gold border glow + spinner during fetch, clicks disabled during load.

RESOLVED (V31 — Rubric Adjustment):
- Sparse input overconfidence: PRO pipeline gave MEDIUM confidence to 4-word idea "ai app for pets" and manufactured specific product to evaluate. Fixed with sparse input rule in Stage 2a — thin inputs now produce thin packets, confidence drops to LOW.
- Fake specificity reward: user-invented numbers (TAM, pricing, conversion rates) inflated scores. Fixed with [user_claim] source tag + MD packet exclusion. MO now explicitly flags "unverified assertions not corroborated by competitor data."
- Uniform cautious tone: every summary started with "this addresses a real pain point but..." regardless of score. Fixed with score-band-calibrated tone instruction. Summaries now differentiate between 5.4 (balanced) and 3.6 (direct about structural problems).
- OR lacks actionability: explanations diagnosed problems but didn't suggest what would improve defensibility. Fixed with one-sentence defensibility improvement suggestion after OR cross-check.

OPEN (V32 — Decision Chain Testing):
- Tradeoffs identity swap (intermittent): In Chain A PRO→PRO comparison, tradeoff tension cards described Idea A as Idea B and vice versa. Scores at bottom were correct. Did not reproduce in 5 other runs. Monitor — may be related to idea_a/idea_b ordering.
- Cross-pipeline delta contamination: When original and branch use different pipelines (e.g., FREE→PRO or PRO→FREE), delta attributes ALL score differences to the user's change. Some difference comes from pipeline depth mismatch, not the change itself. Fix: pipeline disclaimer on Evolve screen informing users that switching pipelines may affect delta and comparison accuracy. Not a system bug — an inherent limitation of comparing evaluations at different analysis depths.
- Pro toggle on Evolve screen: coded and deployed. Needs verification that it persists correctly across sessions. Users can now choose Light or Pro pipeline when re-evaluating/branching.

OPEN (V29):
- Existing "alternatives" saved under parent ideas remain in the database. They are NOT automatically converted to branches. The alternatives popup still works for ideas that already have alternatives. New evaluations from the upgraded re-eval screen will create branches instead.
- Lineage View v1 is deployed but is functional-only (simple indented org-chart). Emre has a mockup for the polished version (centered tree, glowing blue connectors, glass cards, comparison-active badges). Visual polish is a separate future pass after workflow validation.
- fetchMyIdeas sets savedIdeasCount from data.count (which may include branches) — slight inconsistency with the initial useEffect that filters by parent_idea_id null. Low priority since credit system will replace the limit concept.
- Existing ideas in database have no status_label value — column default 'exploring' handles this automatically for display, but existing rows won't have the value explicitly set until user changes it.
- Page refresh loses current screen state: app uses React state for navigation, not URL params. Refreshing always returns to input/profile screen. DEFERRED — would require URL-based routing or localStorage screen persistence. Low priority until after UI polish.
- Lineage tree vertical compactness: 4-level trees require scrolling. Connector heights (24px) and card padding could be reduced. DEFERRED to UI polish session.

V20 issues (unchanged):
- Payment integration: Paddle as merchant of record. Stripe not available in Turkey.
- Credit system database tables not yet designed.
- Landing page not yet redesigned for new positioning.
- User-type onboarding not yet built.
- Demo videos not yet created.

Deployed to Vercel same day.

April 2, 2026 -- V4 Session 11 (Side-by-Side Comparison): Built ComparisonView.js as separate component. 6-screen comparison flow. Fixed data pipeline bug: failure_risks and confidence_level were never being persisted/extracted. Codex session mid-build reverted some fixes.

April 2, 2026 -- V4 Session 12 (Comparison Visual Polish — COMPLETE): Fixed all visual alignment issues. CSS Grid for static screens, independent flex columns for Roadmap. Re-applied GET route fix that Codex had reverted.

April 6, 2026 -- V4 Session 13 (Evolve This Idea Screen): First of 6 workflow upgrade sessions. Re-eval screen redesigned with context snapshot, edit-toggle fields, post-eval decision block. Change metadata captured for delta explanation.

April 6, 2026 -- V4 Session 14 (Branching Data Model + Hub Integration): Database migration for branching fields. New routes: POST /branch, PATCH /set-main. Branch creation with intentional friction. Hub cards show branch origin, main badge, children count.
