April 7, 2026 -- V4 Session 16 (Delta Explanation + Hub Filtering): Fourth of 6 workflow upgrade sessions. Three major deliverables:
1. Hub filtering: My Ideas hub now shows only root ideas + current main branches. All other branches accessed exclusively through lineage view. Save counter only counts roots. Fixed the "7/5 ideas saved" counter bug.
2. Delta explanation: New API route POST /api/ideas/[id]/delta calls Sonnet with dedicated delta prompt (prompt-delta.js). 4-block output: change_summary, improvements[], worsenings[], net_interpretation. Each item carries causal sentence, metric, numerical delta, and attribution confidence (direct/indirect/ambiguous). Results cached in meta_json.delta_result — first view triggers Sonnet, subsequent views return cache. On-demand via "See what changed" button, not auto-generated.
3. Delta screen: New Screen 5 after Roadmap, only visible for branches. Shows change summary (purple), improvements (green cards with +delta badges), worsenings (red cards with -delta badges), net strategic assessment, score movement summary bar. Action buttons (Evolve, Set as main, Back) on both Roadmap and Delta screens for branches.
Bug fixes: fetchMyIdeas() added after branch-save-with-set-main flow so lineage tree reflects main changes immediately. Evolve button added to Roadmap screen for branches (was missing — users couldn't re-evaluate without going through delta first).
Key design decision: Delta (directional: parent → child, "what did my change do?") is architecturally and conceptually distinct from Comparison tradeoffs (symmetric: A vs B, "what am I choosing between?"). Different prompts, different cognitive jobs. ChatGPT analysis informed the prompt design.

April 7, 2026 -- V4 Session 17 (Key Tradeoffs Sonnet Synthesis): Fifth of 6 workflow upgrade sessions. Replaced static Key Tradeoffs screen with dedicated Sonnet call for symmetric tradeoff synthesis. New route POST /api/compare/tradeoffs, new prompt-tradeoffs.js. Frontend preprocessing via buildTradeoffsPayload() builds structured comparison object (scores, deltas, risk/competitor/execution asymmetries). Background-triggered on ComparisonView mount, cached in React state. Tradeoff cards show tensions with gain/sacrifice per idea, not screen recaps. Bug fix: hub Compare button onClick was passing click event as selectionsOverride (pre-existing bug). Deployed.

April 8, 2026 -- V4 Session 18 (Decision Status Labels + Cleanup): Sixth and final workflow upgrade session. Decision status labels (Exploring/Lead/Parked/Killed) on Lineage View nodes with tappable dropdown. Idea renaming via pen icon on both hub cards and lineage nodes. New PATCH /api/ideas/[id] route handles both status and title updates. Database: status_label TEXT DEFAULT 'exploring'. TwoCol dead code removed from ComparisonView.js. V4 WORKFLOW UPGRADE SEQUENCE COMPLETE. Deployed.

What V4 Session 16 Adds (DEPLOYED — April 7, 2026)

DELTA EXPLANATION + HUB FILTERING: Fourth session of 6-session workflow upgrade.

Hub filtering:
- My Ideas hub: myIdeas.filter(i => !i.parent_idea_id || i.is_main_version) — only roots and current main branches visible
- Save counter: .is("parent_idea_id", null) — branches don't count toward limit
- Compare button: uses filtered hub count
- When main changes: old main drops from hub into lineage view, new main appears in hub

Delta explanation:
- POST /api/ideas/[id]/delta — loads parent + child evaluations, preprocesses structured delta object (score deltas, competitor diffs, risk diffs, estimate diffs), extracts changed_fields from meta_json, calls Sonnet, caches in meta_json.delta_result
- prompt-delta.js — 4-block output: change_summary, improvements[], worsenings[], net_interpretation. Attribution confidence per item (direct/indirect/ambiguous). Explicit instruction that score direction ≠ quality direction.
- On-demand: "See what changed" button on Roadmap screen for branches triggers delta fetch + navigation to delta screen
- Delta screen (currentScreen === "delta"): 4 visual blocks + score movement summary bar + action buttons

StepProgress:
- Accepts branchMode prop. Branches: Profile → Idea → Analysis → Roadmap → Delta. Non-branches: Profile → Idea → Analysis → Roadmap → Evolve.

States added: deltaData, deltaLoading, deltaError, isBranchIdea helper.

Bug fixes:
- fetchMyIdeas() called after branch-save-with-set-main (was missing — lineage tree didn't update)
- Evolve button added to Roadmap screen for branches (was missing)

What V4 Session 17 Adds (DEPLOYED — April 7, 2026)

KEY TRADEOFFS SONNET SYNTHESIS: Fifth session of 6-session workflow upgrade. Replaces the static Key Tradeoffs screen (which just restated score differences) with a dedicated Sonnet call that produces decision-relevant tradeoff analysis.

Architecture:
- POST /api/compare/tradeoffs — new API route, fully isolated from main evaluation pipeline. Receives preprocessed structured comparison object, calls Sonnet with dedicated tradeoffs prompt, returns parsed JSON.
- prompt-tradeoffs.js — symmetric comparison synthesis prompt. Instructs Sonnet to identify 3-5 decision-relevant tensions (not screen recaps). Each tradeoff has: tension label, idea_a_advantage, idea_a_cost, idea_b_advantage, idea_b_cost. Dominance threshold is strict (3+ dimensions with minor losses). Explicitly forbids external advice, generic startup language, score-only recommendations.
- buildTradeoffsPayload() — frontend preprocessor in ComparisonView.js. Extracts scores, deltas, failure risks, confidence levels, competitor counts/types, shared competitors, risk summaries, execution estimates into a structured object. Sonnet receives this structured data, not raw evaluation JSON.

Frontend:
- ComparisonView.js now accepts authToken prop. Background useEffect fires tradeoffs API call on mount — result is ready by the time user navigates to screen 6.
- New TradeoffsScreen: decision summary card (blue), tradeoff tension cards (each with Idea A blue dot / Idea B purple dot, green up-arrow advantages, red down-arrow costs), dominant idea assessment (green, only if Sonnet found clear dominance), score reference bar at bottom.
- Error fallback: if Sonnet call fails, shows simplified score comparison (basic metric-by-metric winner display).
- Tradeoffs result cached in React state per session — navigating away and back doesn't re-fetch.
- page.js captures auth token in compareData during startComparison(), passes as prop to ComparisonView.

Bug fix:
- Hub Compare button: onClick={startComparison} was passing the click event as selectionsOverride, causing the function to bail out. Fixed to onClick={() => startComparison()}. This was a pre-existing bug (present before V4S17) — lineage comparison worked because it passes an explicit array.

What V4 Session 18 Adds (DEPLOYED — April 8, 2026)

DECISION STATUS LABELS + IDEA RENAMING + CLEANUP: Sixth and final session of 6-session workflow upgrade. Closes the V4 workflow upgrade sequence.

Decision Status Labels:
- Labels: Exploring (blue), Lead (green), Parked (gray), Killed (red). Default: exploring.
- Database: status_label TEXT DEFAULT 'exploring' on ideas table. Separate from system-level status column (active/archived).
- API: PATCH /api/ideas/[id] — accepts { status_label, title } in request body, validates, updates.
- Frontend: Status badges on Lineage View nodes ONLY (not hub cards). Tappable pill → dropdown with 4 options → PATCH call → optimistic local update.
- Each idea (root or branch) has its own independent status. No inheritance from parent.
- StatusDropdown component with outside-click-to-close and hover states.

Idea Renaming:
- Pen icon (✏️) next to idea title in both Lineage View nodes and My Ideas Hub cards.
- Click pen → title becomes inline input → Enter/blur saves via PATCH, Escape cancels.
- Same PATCH /api/ideas/[id] route handles both rename and status change.

Cleanup:
- TwoCol dead code removed from ComparisonView.js (was defined but unused since V4S12).
- No other dead code found from V4S13-V4S17 sessions.

States added: editingIdeaId, editingIdeaTitle (page.js). New function: updateIdea(ideaId, fields) — calls PATCH, does optimistic setMyIdeas update.
New prop: onUpdateIdea passed from page.js to LineageView.

V4 WORKFLOW UPGRADE SEQUENCE NOW COMPLETE. All 6 sessions (V4S13-V4S18) delivered. Product has evolved from evaluator to structured idea evolution environment with branching, lineage, delta explanation, tradeoff synthesis, status tracking, and inline editing.

April 10, 2026 -- V4 Session 19 (Bug Fixes + Performance Polish): Post-workflow polish session. Seven fixes deployed:
1. Status label persistence: ideas/list route was missing status_label in SELECT query — changes were saved to DB but never fetched back. One-line fix.
2. Screen flash (lineage → idea): lineage mode exited synchronously before async fetch completed, showing hub briefly. Fixed by making onViewIdea async — lineage stays visible until data loads.
3. Screen flash (lineage → comparison): same pattern, same fix for onStartComparison.
4. Profile screen flash on page refresh: added auth loading gate — shows minimal dark screen with "IdeaLoop Core" text until auth resolves.
5. Comparison estimates unequal height: duration/difficulty cards not stretching in CSS Grid. Fixed with height:100% on renderEstimates wrapper and display:flex on grid cells.
6. Evaluation cache: added evaluationCacheRef (useRef) — loaded evaluations cached in memory. Repeat visits to same idea within session are instant. Extracted applyLoadedIdea() helper.
7. Delta client-side cache: delta results cached in evaluationCacheRef alongside evaluations. Repeat views within session are instant.
8. Loading spinner on lineage nodes: loadingIdeaId state, gold border glow + spinning loader overlay during fetch, clicks disabled.
Build order decision: Rubric adjustment next, then UI polish, then Paddle integration.

April 11, 2026 -- V4 Session 20 (Rubric Adjustment): First rubric-only session. Designed and ran user-realistic test suite: 34 ideas across 7 input styles (one-liners, brain dumps, kitchen-sink, copycat, problem-first, technical builders, edge cases) plus 9 consistency variants (same idea × 3 formats) and 5 adversarial inputs. 68 total runs (34 × FREE + PRO). Key findings:
1. Writing quality does NOT bias scores — consistency test spread ≤0.7 across all 3 idea groups. Broken English customs tool scored within range of polished version. Critical fairness result.
2. Sparse input overconfidence — "ai app for pets" (4 words) got MEDIUM confidence and MD 5.5 on PRO. Fixed with sparse input rule in Stage 2a (thin inputs → thin packets).
3. Fake specificity vulnerability — user-invented numbers (TAM, pricing, conversion rates) inflated scores. Fixed with [user_claim] source tag in Stage 2a + MD packet exclusion rule.
4. Uniform cautious tone — every summary read like a rejection memo regardless of score. Fixed with score-band-calibrated tone instruction at end of Stage 2b.
5. OR lacks actionability — explanations diagnose but don't direct. Fixed with one-sentence defensibility improvement suggestion after OR cross-check.
All fixes verified with targeted tests. PRO pipeline: sparse input → LOW confidence (was MEDIUM), fake specificity → dropped from 5.1 to 5.0 with MO flagging user claims, tone → summaries now score-calibrated. Zero scoring regression on customs tool regression check (4.8 → 4.5, within tolerance). Deployed.

Found 5 bugs: tradeoffs identity swap (intermittent), evolve screen missing pro toggle (fixed), and 3 cross-pipeline contamination issues (root cause: delta has no pipeline awareness). Pro toggle coded and deployed.
- Chain B (generic document summarizer → legal discovery niche): 1 run (PRO→PRO). Zero bugs. Competitors correctly shifted from generic (Adobe, PDF-Summarizer) to legal-specific (CaseMark, LegalMation). Delta correctly attributed all improvements to the niche pivot. Tradeoffs captured generic-vs-niche tension perfectly.
- Chain C (influencer analytics for creators → B2B per-report pricing for brands): 1 run (PRO→PRO). Zero bugs. MO +2.0 / OR -2.0 swing correctly reflected across all features. Delta net assessment noted "slight overall score improvement masks a meaningful strategic improvement." Tradeoffs identified Market Size vs Defensibility and Monetization vs Competition tensions.
Key findings: Same-pipeline workflow is fully coherent — zero bugs across 3 PRO→PRO chains. Cross-pipeline branching is the only issue, mitigated by pipeline disclaimer (inform users, don't restrict). TC isolation confirmed working across all 6 runs. Testing pass COMPLETE.

What V4 Session 20 Adds (DEPLOYED — April 11, 2026)

RUBRIC ADJUSTMENT: Prompt-only changes to Stage 2a, Stage 2b, and free prompt. No architecture, route, frontend, or database changes.

Stage 2a changes (prompt-stage2a.js):
- Sparse input rule: ideas under 20 meaningful words produce thin packets — no product inference, no manufactured facts, unresolved_uncertainty names specific missing info. Stage 2b's existing "sparse evidence biases downward" rule handles scoring automatically.
- [user_claim] source tag: 5th source tag for unverified user statistics. Same trust level as [narrative_field] (lowest). Examples: TAM claims, pricing assumptions, conversion projections, "every person I talked to would pay."
- MD packet EXCLUDED: user-stated market statistics barred from MD packet unless corroborated by [competitor: Name] or [domain_flag] evidence. Concrete example in the instruction.
- Cross-packet verification item 8: strongest_positive cannot rely on [user_claim] as primary support.

Stage 2b changes (prompt-stage2b.js):
- Summary tone calibration: positioned AFTER all scoring instructions and JSON structure. Score-band-aware tone (6.0+ leads with strengths, 4.5-5.9 balanced, below 4.5 leads with core problem). Anti-pattern list blocks uniform cautious register. Specific anti-patterns named: "this addresses a real pain point but...", 3+ however clauses, generic niche advice.
- OR actionability: one sentence after OR cross-check identifying the single most realistic defensibility improvement for THIS idea. Must be specific ("build proprietary dataset of X from Y sources") not generic ("find ways to differentiate").

Free prompt changes (prompt.js):
- Sparse input rule: mirrored from Stage 2a adapted for single-call context. Confidence must be LOW, explanations must name missing info, conservative scores (cap 5.0 unless strong search evidence).
- Scoring rule 8: user-stated claims are not evidence. User numbers noted but do not drive scores upward.
- Summary tone calibration: mirrored from Stage 2b.

V4S20 test artifacts:
- run-tests-realistic.js: 34-idea automated test runner with 9 Excel sheets (All Results, Explanations, Consistency, Input Quality, Flags & Competition, Evidence Packets, Adversarial, TC Distribution, Timing)
- run-tests-targeted.js: 4-idea targeted verification script with inline pass/fail checks
- IdeaLoopCore_UserRealistic_TestSuite.md: full test design document with expected ranges, red flags, and decision triggers

What V4S28 Adds (DEPLOYED Through Bundle B4 — April 25-26, 2026)

PRE-LAUNCH PIPELINE FIX SEQUENCE: Audit-driven backend + UI improvements that change what users see in the live evaluation experience. Three bundles shipped (B1, B3, B4); five more in queue (B5-B9) plus B10 split (B10a behavioral regression + B10b narrative coherence) before launch.

Backend architecture changes (B1 + B3 + B4):

Stage 2c isolation (B1 — commit 8711364 + two patches):
- New `prompt-stage2c.js` synthesis stage for summary + failure_risks generation, decoupled from Stage 2b scoring rubric
- Sequential pipeline: Stage 2a (evidence packets) → Stage 2b + Stage TC parallel (scoring) → Stage 2c (synthesis) → Stage 3 (roadmap)
- Profile-aware Risk 3 archetype detection co-resides with profile-blind summary synthesis without observable cross-contamination
- `failure_risks` schema: array of `{slot, archetype, text}` objects with three slot enum (market_category, trust_adoption, founder_fit) and archetype enum (A-E for founder_fit, null for the others)
- STEP 1 PROFILE-DOMAIN MATCH: when founder profile matches required idea domain, founder_fit slot is dropped before archetype evaluation (Founder-fit case)
- Lead rotation rule: market_category Risk 1 must NOT begin with a proper noun
- LOW evidence_strength sparse-input handling: triggers specification-gap framing instead of fabricated evaluation

Main Bottleneck classification (B3 — commit f80330b + B1 schema regression patch):
- Stage 3 declares the SINGLE binding constraint that gates the idea
- 8-value enum: Technical build, Buyer access, Trust/credibility, Compliance, Distribution, Data acquisition, Category maturation, Specification
- Three relational cases per Section 4 lock: Alignment (founder gap matches MB enum), Layered (founder gap differs from MB enum, both compound), Founder-fit (Risk 3 null, MB stands alone as idea-intrinsic)
- Cross-references Stage 2c failure_risks archetype field for relational case detection
- Color taxonomy: Indigo / Purple / Teal / Slate / Pink / Cyan / Sage / Stone — selected to avoid collision with severity colors (red/amber/blue/green reserved for Difficulty pills, scores, TC, step indicators)

OR actionability hook + Evidence Strength rename (B4 — commit f8fb7f8):
- OR explanation now ENFORCED to end with two-element required structure: rubric-level justification + defensibility-improvement suggestion (or honest exit clause if no realistic defensibility path exists)
- OR hook firing rate: 100% (vs ~20% pre-B4 baseline)
- Anti-generic guardrail: forbids "consider building proprietary data" / "create network effects" / "deepen integrations" / "create competitive moat" without specific named targets
- Honest exit clause (verbatim): "No realistic defensibility path exists against incumbents with this approach."
- `confidence_level` field renamed to `evidence_strength` across all production surfaces (atomic 14-file rename)
- Evidence Strength semantically scoped to evidence quality (not idea outcomes): HIGH = strong evidence base, MEDIUM = specific concrete gap (Option Z rule), LOW = input too thin/contradictory
- Option Z MEDIUM rule: MEDIUM reasons MUST identify a specific concrete gap (forbids generic hedging like "clear market with some uncertainty")
- Cross-stage propagation: LOW evidence_strength → Specification main_bottleneck + "Cannot estimate..." duration + "N/A" difficulty (full Stage 2c → Stage 3 cascade)
- Dead-code deletion: `prompt-stage2.js` (unified Stage 2 prompt left over from B1 split, no remaining importers)

Frontend changes (B3 + B4 partial frontend):

Execution Reality (B3):
- Main Bottleneck colored chip rendered in Execution Reality row across EvaluationView + ComparisonView
- ComparisonView Execution Reality switched to 3-card vertical stack with chip integration

Evidence Strength (B4 partial):
- Label rename: "Evaluation Confidence" → "Evidence Strength" / "Confidence:" → "Evidence Strength:" across EvaluationView + ComparisonView + page.js Evolve screen
- HIGH evidence_strength produces NO card render (asymmetric display silent default — addresses the F/P inversion the audit identified)
- MEDIUM/LOW currently render with previous colored-card form; full asymmetric design (LOW prominent warning, MEDIUM subtle marker) deferred to B8 with UI mockup

Schema regression hardening (B3 + B4 hygiene):
- Pre-commit grep gate established as standing discipline for any field rename (B4 caught its own 14-file surface area this way)
- Schema-shape changes now require downstream consumer audit BEFORE shipping (B1 schema regression caught in B3 frontend rendering established the discipline)

Deferred to future bundles (B5-B10):
- Stage 2a sparse-input MO discipline + spec-quality trigger expansion (B5)
- Stage 1 profile strip + How-it-compares (B6)
- Specificity gate / Haiku layer (B7)
- Asymmetric MEDIUM/LOW Evidence Strength rendering + score tier label UI + specificity gate UI (B8)
- α formula + score tier labels numerical (B9)
- Behavioral regression launch gate (B10a) + narrative coherence verification (B10b)

V4S28 Methodology Locks (Carried Forward):
- Five Methodology Principles (Step 0 Fundamentals → Step 1 TC Isolation → Step 2 Contamination Check → Step 3 Roadmap Design → Step 4 Boring Wins) applied prospectively to every bundle's design discussion

V30 Pre-Ship Roadmap Decisions (Locked In — April 10, 2026):
- Full pre-ship build order locked: Rubric → Testing → Free/Pro UI → UI Polish → Product Content Audit → Edge Case Audit → Visual/Technical Audit → User Feedback → Paddle → Landing Page → Onboarding → Portfolio/README
- Rubric adjustment includes tradeoffs prompt "decision boundary" refinement (map tradeoffs to user priorities without recommending — "this tradeoff favors A when you prioritize X, favors B when you prioritize Y") — DEPRIORITIZED in V4S20, not blocking
- Testing pass is a NEW test regime focused on Decision Chain Tests (multi-step workflow consistency: evaluate → branch → delta → compare → tradeoffs checking nothing contradicts) plus targeted regression. Sparse-input scoring already validated in V4S20. Also includes cross-feature consistency verification: one idea through full loop checking outputs agree across features.
- Product content audit is section-by-section investigation: competitors list, scores, summary, key risks, roadmap, tools, time/difficulty. Each examined for output quality, free/pro differentiation, improvement opportunities, and new approaches.
- Edge case audit covers: zero saved ideas, deep branch trees, very short/long inputs, mid-stream timeouts, Supabase errors, pre-feature legacy data, mobile full-flow walkthrough, first-time empty states.
- User feedback on evaluations positioned before Paddle because it's a trust-recovery feature — users who disagree need a next move besides leaving.
- ChatGPT workflow/UI review (164-page conversation) confirmed all V4 workflow features were correctly designed and implemented.

V31 Rubric Assessment Findings (April 11, 2026):
- Rubric scoring is proportionate: median overall ~4.8, most ideas land 4.0-5.5. System catches platform inflation, LLM substitution, marketplace cold-start, shallow wrappers, and crowded commodities. No score inflation detected.
- Traceability is strong: explanations reference specific competitors by name, cite rubric levels, and ground in evidence packets.
- Writing quality does NOT bias scores: confirmed across 3 idea groups × 3 input qualities. Critical fairness result for global audience.
- Proportionality improved: summary tone is now score-band-calibrated. 5.4 ideas feel balanced, 4.4 ideas feel direct, 3.6 ideas feel honest about structural problems.
- OR is the metric most likely to trigger user disagreement — median OR ~4.5, most explanations end with "competitors could replicate with moderate effort." This is usually correct but feels dismissive on third read. OR actionability fix (one-sentence defensibility suggestion) partially addresses this.
- MO explanations have a formulaic tendency ("however, free substitute pressure") — accepted as accurate for AI ideas where LLM substitution IS the real threat. Not worth forcing artificial variety.
- Three text blocks in evaluation output (competition comparison, scoring summary, execution estimate explanation) serve distinct narrative roles and are complementary, not redundant.
- Score tier labels next to overall score and "Execution Reality" naming for Time & Difficulty explanation block are UI improvements deferred to Free vs Pro UI or UI Polish sessions.

V32 Decision Chain Testing Findings (April 11, 2026):
- Same-pipeline (PRO→PRO) workflow is fully coherent across all 3 chains and all test dimensions (evaluation scores, competitor shifts, delta attribution, tradeoff tensions, risk/roadmap/tool adaptation). Zero bugs.
- TC isolation confirmed rock-solid: TC stayed constant (7.5, 6.5, 7.5) across all chains when profile didn't change. No leakage from any feature.
- Delta causal attribution is accurate within same pipeline — correctly identifies improvements and worsenings, correctly attributes them to the user's change, correctly distinguishes score direction from strategic quality.
- Tradeoff synthesis produces genuinely decision-useful output — identifies real tensions (generic vs niche, monetization vs competition, market size vs defensibility) rather than restating score differences.
- Cross-pipeline branching is the only coherence failure — delta mixes pipeline-depth differences with user changes, producing contaminated attribution. This is inherent to comparing evaluations at different analysis depths. Fix: informational disclaimer, not restriction. Users shouldn't be punished financially for the system's limitation.
- Tradeoffs identity swap is intermittent (1/6 runs) — may be related to idea_a/idea_b ordering. Not blocking but worth monitoring.
- Confidence levels shift appropriately across pivots: crowded generic space → HIGH, specialized legal/B2B niche → MEDIUM. System correctly expresses more uncertainty when entering specialized markets.
- Summary tone calibration working correctly: OA 4.0 leads with structural problem, OA 4.6-4.9 gives balanced assessment. No uniform cautious register detected.

V4 Session 20 Decisions (Locked In — April 11, 2026):
- All rubric fixes are positioned UPSTREAM or DOWNSTREAM of scoring — zero changes to scoring bands, anti-inflation rules, packet boundaries, cross-checks, or any scoring logic in Stage 2b.
- Sparse input rule lives in Stage 2a (evidence extractor), not Stage 2b (scorer). Thin inputs produce thin packets → Stage 2b's existing "sparse evidence biases downward" rule handles scoring automatically. Threshold: 20 meaningful words.
- [user_claim] is a new source tag in Stage 2a with SAME trust level as [narrative_field] (lowest). Applies to user-stated statistics, TAM, pricing, conversion claims. Stage 2b's existing "prefer higher-trust sources" rule handles scoring automatically.
- MD packet EXCLUDED list explicitly bars user-stated market statistics unless corroborated by [competitor: Name] or [domain_flag] evidence.
- Cross-packet verification item 8: strongest_positive cannot rely on [user_claim] as primary support.
- Summary tone calibration lives at the VERY END of Stage 2b, after all scoring instructions and JSON structure. Cannot influence score selection — Sonnet has already committed numbers before reaching tone instructions.
- Tone is score-band-calibrated: 6.0+ leads with strengths, 4.5-5.9 balanced, below 4.5 leads with core problem. Anti-pattern list prevents uniform cautious register.
- OR actionability: each OR explanation ends with one sentence identifying the single most realistic change that would improve defensibility for THIS idea. Positioned after OR cross-check, before overall score section.
- Free prompt (prompt.js) mirrors: sparse input rule, user-claims scoring rule 8, and tone calibration block.
- Scoring rule 8 in free prompt: user-stated claims are not evidence. User numbers noted in explanation but do not drive scores upward.
- User-realistic test suite created: 34 ideas across 7 input styles (one-liners, brain dumps, kitchen-sink visionaries, copycat-with-twist, problem-first, technical builders, edge cases) + 9 consistency variants (same idea × 3 formats) + 5 adversarial inputs. Covers domains NOT in original V4S7 suite.
- Writing quality does NOT bias scores — confirmed by consistency tests. Broken English, messy paragraph, and polished brief versions of the same idea scored within 0.7 OA spread. This is a critical fairness result for a global product.
- PRO pipeline sparse input fix confirmed working: "ai app for pets" got LOW confidence, scores dropped from 4.6 to 3.6.
- PRO pipeline fake specificity fix confirmed working: dental idea with fake numbers dropped from 5.1 to 5.0, MO correctly flags user pricing claims as "unverified assertions."
- PRO pipeline tone fix confirmed working: summaries no longer start with "this addresses a real pain point but..." regardless of score level.
- FREE pipeline has structural limitations on sparse input and fake specificity enforcement — acceptable gap between tiers given single-call architecture.
- Three text blocks in evaluation output serve distinct narrative roles: (1) "How your idea compares" = factual landscape from Stage 1, (2) "Summary" = scoring verdict from Stage 2b, (3) Time & Difficulty explanation = execution reality from Stage 3. These are complementary, not redundant.
- Tradeoffs prompt "decision boundary" tweak (from V30 plan) was NOT implemented — deprioritized in favor of the three higher-impact fixes. Can be revisited if needed but is not blocking.

V4 Session 22 Decisions (Locked In — April 12, 2026):
- Three-state product model replaces "Free vs Pro": Free Preview (2 lifetime standard evals, light theme, partial content, no workflow), PAYG (credit packs, full content, light theme, no workflow, 5 saved ideas), Subscriber ($20/month, dark workspace, full content, full workflow, unlimited saves).
- 2 lifetime free Standard Analysis evaluations only. Zero free Deep Analysis at launch. Cost-driven decision: 2 Standard = ~$0.05/user vs 2 Standard + 1 Deep = ~$0.15/user (3x increase). Deep preview deferred to post-launch conversion experiment if needed.
- Theme follows subscription, NOT pipeline. PAYG stays light even when using Deep Analysis. Dark = subscriber identity.
- Content visibility follows payment, NOT subscription. Once credits spent, full report. Blur is free-preview-only.
- Workflow follows subscription only. Credits never unlock evolve/branch/compare/delta/tradeoffs/lineage.
- Naming: "Standard Analysis" (single-call free pipeline), "Deep Analysis" (chained pro pipeline). Do NOT call it "Pro evaluation" in user-facing UI. Account states: "Free Preview", "Credits" / "Pay as you go", "Workspace Subscription" / "IdeaLoop Pro Workspace".
- Internal code names (proMode, /api/analyze-pro) stay unchanged — users don't see them.
- Entitlement model uses separate axes (themeMode, canSeeFullContent, canUseWorkflow, saveCap, isPreviewEvaluation), NOT a single tier string.
- Dev testing override: ?mode=preview/payg/subscriber query param. Remove before ship.
- Theme system: Light "Report Teal" palette (bg #f4f2ef warm sand, surface #faf9f7 off-white, text #171919 dark ink, warm-tinted borders rgba(80,75,65,...), score ring #4d5258) for Preview+PAYG. Dark (current production, bg #0a0a0a, score ring gold with glow) for Subscriber. Functional colors (score bars, TC inverted colors, tool descriptions, phase numbers, risk numbers) shared across both themes. Gold accent bar REMOVED from dark theme (V4S25).
- Content gating (free preview only): REMOVED IN V4S26a. Originally: MD metric shown fully, other 3 metrics score+bar only, phases blurred, execution blurred. Replaced by quantity gate (2 lifetime evals). All gating infrastructure stays in codebase but inactive (isGated always false).
- Hub behavior: PAYG = simple cards with score/title/date/pipeline badge, rename, delete, save counter "X of 5", no compare/lineage/branch UI, upgrade prompt. Subscriber = current production hub with full workflow.
- Execution plan locked as V4S23-S25 sequence: entitlements → extract+theme → content gating.
- Cascade delete bug identified: deleting root doesn't cascade to branches, orphaned branches still counted. Fix deferred to separate session.
- Lineage node management gap identified: branches only manageable from lineage view which lacks delete. Fix deferred to separate session.

V4 Session 21 Decisions (Locked In — April 11, 2026):
- Decision Chain Testing uses live product (idealoopcore.com), not automated scripts. Tests the product AS A SYSTEM — full user workflow coherence, not individual evaluation scoring.
- Three chains tested: Chain A (customs document validator, target user pivot), Chain B (generic document summarizer → legal discovery niche), Chain C (influencer analytics → B2B per-report monetization pivot).
- Same-pipeline (PRO→PRO) workflow is fully coherent — evaluation scores, delta attributions, comparison displays, and tradeoff tensions all tell consistent stories across all three chains. Zero bugs in same-pipeline runs.
- Cross-pipeline branching (FREE↔PRO) produces contaminated delta attribution — delta has no awareness of which pipeline produced each evaluation, so it attributes pipeline-depth differences to the user's change. This is a known limitation, not a system bug.
- Fix for cross-pipeline contamination: pipeline disclaimer on Evolve screen near the pipeline toggle, informing users that switching pipelines may affect delta and comparison accuracy. Users are informed, not restricted — forcing same pipeline would be punishing users financially (4-5 credits per PRO re-eval).
- ~~Pro toggle on Evolve screen: toggle UI before the evaluate button, handleReEvaluate routes by proMode (V4S21 Chain A).~~ **RETIRED V80:** the `proMode` toggle (both the input + Evolve UIs) was excised; Evolve re-eval now always runs Deep.
- Tradeoffs identity swap (Chain A Run 1): A/B qualitative content was reversed while scores at bottom were correct. Did not reproduce in other 5 runs. Logged as intermittent — may be related to idea_a/idea_b ordering when both are PRO. Monitor but do not fix unless it reproduces.
- TC isolation confirmed working across all 6 runs — TC stayed constant when profile didn't change (7.5 in Chain A, 6.5 in Chain B, 7.5 in Chain C). No leakage.
- DEFERRED TO UI POLISH: (1) Delta/tradeoffs screens need distinct headers to make cognitive job difference clear — "What Your Change Did" (delta) vs "What You're Choosing Between" (tradeoffs). Without this, users who made one clear change may feel the two screens are redundant. (2) Comparison screens (Competitors, Risks, Roadmap, Tools — not Scores) should each get a one-line difference-focused summary sentence at the top (e.g., "Competitors shifted from consumer document tools to legal tech incumbents"). Must be strictly descriptive, not interpretive — interpretation is Tradeoffs' job. Max ~15 words, no judgment, difference-focused not version-focused. (3) Lineage tree visual polish from functional org-chart to Emre's mockup (glowing connectors, glass cards).

Key concerns raised:
- **P6-S1** (HIGH, architectural regression): MAT2 MO score varies ~1.5pt across profiles on identical idea — violates V4S20 anti-contamination architecture
- **P8-S2** (HIGH): MAT1 confidence flips MEDIUM→HIGH→MEDIUM across profiles — possible Stage 2b profile contamination
- **P12-S1** (MEDIUM): Competitor lists drift across profiles — possible Stage 1 profile leakage
- Cross-Cut #3 (Profile leakage): cascade hypothesis proposed — all three findings might share a Stage 1 root cause. Strip profile from Stage 1 as potential unified fix.

April 24, 2026 -- V4 Session 28 (Phase 0 Variance Testing + Phase 0.5 Stage 1 Pro — COMPLETE, LOCAL ONLY NOT COMMITTED): First V4S28 implementation work. Two workstreams completed same day:

**PHASE 0 — Variance testing (19 runs + P8-S2 resolution + extended diagnostic):**
- 19 re-runs: MAT1/MAT2/MAT3 × 2 additional passes per profile + SP1 × 1, plus R1 from audit baseline. Backend retrieval-capture patch shipped pre-runs (github_done/serper_done now emit full results arrays, not just counts).
- Cascade hypothesis REJECTED: MO drift (P6-S1) and confidence flip (P8-S2) are anti-correlated (phi = -0.63), appear in different cells, never co-occur. Three separate mechanisms.
- P8-S2 extended diagnostic (n=7 post-R1 per profile, 21 total MAT1 observations): confidence labels flip HIGH/MEDIUM at pooled 38% HIGH rate regardless of profile. Beginner 29%, intermediate 43%, senior 43% — spread 14pt, within sampling noise. 2/3 profiles BIMODAL_UNSTABLE. Byte-identical reasoning pairs in 2/3 profiles. Same two attractor templates fire across all three profiles. **Not profile contamination — Stage 2b synthesis is bimodal at temp=0 on idea-sufficiency judgments.** P8-S2 REFRAMED from contamination-prevention to Stage 2b bimodality-stabilization.
- NEW Finding 1 (MAJOR): Stage 1 non-deterministic at temp=0. Three cells had byte-identical Stage 1 inputs (Jaccard 1.0 keywords + Jaccard 1.0 Serper URLs) yet produced competitor lists with Jaccard 0.25-0.62. 100% of cells showed competitor drift independent of profile.
- Outputs: variance-raw.json, variance-analysis.md, p8s2-resolution-raw.json/.md, p8s2-extended-raw.json/.md.
- Execution-plan + execution-order updated: Section 8 P8-S2 reframed, Phase 0 Findings section added, Phase 0.5 workstream opened.

**PHASE 0.5 STAGE 1 Pro pipeline (cheap-first fix sequence + validation):**

Test harness: run-stage1-stability.js — 3 cells × 2 reruns, measures byte Jaccard + fuzzy Jaccard (semantic match tolerating label variation) + Serper URL Jaccard. Phase 0 baseline: MAT1=0.62, MAT2=0.25, MAT3=0.50, mean 0.46.

Fix #1 — Sort retrieved items by URL before Stage 1 injection (both routes). No meaningful improvement on its own (MAT2=0.38, MAT3=0.38). Ordering wasn't the mechanism. Kept as defensive; ~4 lines per route.

Fix #3 — Sampler-level hardening on Pro Stage 1 Sonnet call: top_k: 1 + top_p: 0.1 alongside temperature: 0. (Sonnet 4 accepts both params alongside temperature; the either/or restriction only applies to Sonnet 4.5+. Anthropic does NOT support seed param on Sonnet.) Result: MAT2 byte Jaccard jumped 0.38 → 1.00 on stable input. MAT3 byte 0.00 / fuzzy 0.43 — MAT3's Serper URL J dropped to 0.75 this run, retrieval drift cascaded. **Major identity-level stability gain, exposed label drift as separate residual problem.**

Fix #2 — Fixed competitor count — NOT TESTED, NOT NEEDED. Counts already stable within each cell pair.

Fix #4 — Canonical naming conventions added to prompt-stage1.js (+~200 words between IMPORTANT RULES and JSON STRUCTURE). Rules: real companies = shortest brand name, no parentheticals; manual workflows = "Manual [noun] workflow" pattern; professional services = profession/role name only; internal_build = always exactly "Internal build". Descriptive details move to description field.

Final validated result (three-fix bundle, canonical-names test):
- MAT1-beginner: byte 1.00, fuzzy 1.00 (Serper J 1.00) — PASS
- MAT2-intermediate: byte 0.50, fuzzy 0.50 (Serper J 0.75) — retrieval-drift-capped, not synthesis drift
- MAT3-insider: byte 1.00, fuzzy 1.00 (Serper J 1.00) — PASS

Declared Stage 1 synthesis stability PASS for Pro pipeline. 2/3 cells at byte J=1.00 on stable input is the strongest possible evidence. MAT2's 0.50 decomposes as ~70% retrieval cascade (Counterforce Health URL appeared r2 only) + ~30% minor residual label drift in one substitute entry ("Insurance brokers" canonical vs "Benefits brokers and consultants" non-canonical). Retrieval-layer drift is outside Stage 1 responsibility.

Five methodology principles validation (run retroactively at user prompt — carried forward as process fix: run the gate BEFORE shipping, not after):
- Fundamentals gate: PASS (content-rule fix on structurally-correct name field)
- TC isolation: PASS (no scoring impact)
- Contamination check: PASS (no pathway to other Stage 1 outputs; name-to-description info relocation preserves data for Stage 2a)
- Roadmap design principle: PASS (content obligations, not prose choreography)
- Boring wins: PASS (pure structural fix, not narrative guidance)

Files shipped locally (UNCOMMITTED at end of session):
- src/app/api/analyze-pro/route.js — Fix #1 + Fix #3
- ~~src/app/api/analyze/route.js — Fix #1 only (Standard route Fix #3 pending)~~ **CORRECTED V42:** src/app/api/analyze/route.js — Fix #1 only. Fix #3 + Fix #4 were later TESTED + REVERTED on Standard (commit 17f09be) — TC drift exceeded ship-blocker gate on Standard's merged-call architecture. Standard remains at Fix #1 only, no further sampler work pending.
- src/lib/services/prompt-stage1.js — Fix #4
- run-stage1-stability.js — test harness

Key learnings carried forward:
1. **Three-layer decomposition of synthesis stability**: retrieval layer (Serper/Google — outside scope), identity layer (sampler variance — solved by top_k=1), label layer (naming inconsistency — solved by canonical-naming prompt). Byte Jaccard conflates all three; fuzzy Jaccard isolates identity.
2. **Anthropic acknowledges temp=0 is not fully deterministic.** MoE routing + floating-point aggregation + batch effects contribute. Maximum sampler-level determinism is temp=0 + top_k=1 + top_p=0.1. Beyond that requires prompt-level constraints.
3. ~~**Same fix pattern transfers to Stage 2b.** Stage 2b bimodality is same phenomenon class. Expect param hardening + tightened confidence rubric to close it.~~ **CORRECTED V42 — this prediction was falsified.** Stage 2b sampler hardening was tested + reverted at Step 3a parameter level (within-profile bimodality dissolved but cross-profile spread regressed 14pt → 42.9pt). The lesson updates to: same phenomenon class does NOT guarantee same fix transfers cleanly across architecturally different stages. Stage 1's clean isolated synthesis call accepted top_k=1 + top_p=0.1 without scoring side-effects; Stage 2b's classification-with-rubric call did not. P8-S2 was instead resolved at the UX layer (Section 8 locked design — HIGH hidden, MEDIUM only when actionable, LOW prominent) shipped in B4 as Option Z MEDIUM rule + asymmetric display. Sampler fix obviated.
4. **Run Five Methodology Principles gate BEFORE shipping prompt changes.** Retroactive validation works but isn't the right process.
5. **Measure at both byte and fuzzy layers.** Byte alone nearly misclassified Fix #3 as ineffective when it had solved the identity layer completely.

V4 Session 27+28 Decisions (Locked In — April 20-24, 2026):
- Cascade hypothesis rejected (confirmed by data, not by argument)
- Stage 1 synthesis non-determinism resolved for Pro pipeline via three-fix bundle
- P8-S2 reframed from contamination-prevention to Stage 2b bimodality-stabilization
- Stage 1 Fix #3 (top_k=1, top_p=0.1) applies to Sonnet 4 model specifically (claude-sonnet-4-20250514); would need restructuring for Sonnet 4.5+ which doesn't allow both top_p and temperature
- Retrieval-layer drift (Serper/Google ranking fluctuation) is out of Stage 1's scope; not a V4S28 target
- Five Methodology Principles gate must be run BEFORE shipping prompt-level changes (process correction)
- Anthropic seed parameter not supported on Sonnet API; stability ceiling is temp=0 + top_k=1 + top_p=0.1 at sampler level

=== V4S28 BUNDLE EXECUTION MODEL (adopted Bundle B1 session, April 25-26) ===

V4S28 was originally framed as a "section-by-section ship" — design and ship each audit section as its own deploy. Mid-session this was replaced with a **bundled execution model** that groups sections by the code surface they modify, ships each bundle as a single deploy, and runs targeted verification per bundle.

Bundle map (post-B8 closure, May 1, 2026):

| Bundle | Sections | Status | What it does |
|---|---|---|---|
| B1 | S1 + S2 + S3 | **CLOSED** (Apr 26) | Stage 2c creation — summary + failure_risks isolated from scoring |
| B2 | S5 | **REOPENED for pre-B10a** | TC adjustment-math anchor-fixing fix (B6-surfaced; absorbed into redefined B9) |
| B3 | S4 | **CLOSED** (Apr 26) | Main Bottleneck — Stage 3 prompt edit + early frontend chip rendering |
| B4 | S6 P6-S3 + S8 semantic | **CLOSED** (Apr 26) | Stage 2b prompt — OR actionability hook + Evidence Strength rename + Option Z MEDIUM rule + frontend HIGH-hidden + dead-code deletion of prompt-stage2.js |
| B5 | S6 P6-S5 + S8 P8-S5 | **CLOSED** (Apr 27) | Stage 2a sparse-input — packet quality under thin input + three-trigger expansion + counter-example clause |
| B6 | S11 + S12 | **CLOSED** (Apr 28) | Stage 1 prompt — profile strip + How-it-compares + atomic three-strip route-level profile cleanup |
| B7 | S13 | **CLOSED** (Apr 28) | Specificity gate at Haiku layer + minimal frontend (5 files: keywords.js + analyze-pro/route.js + analyze/route.js + components.js + page.js) |
| B8 | S8 frontend (asymmetric MEDIUM/LOW rendering) + S9 α formula | **CLOSED** (May 1) | C-2 layout (summary card + prose card with EXECUTION CONTEXT divider for TC); MEDIUM/LOW callouts (blue-tinted, partnered framing); Mix B color palette + locked boundaries (MD/MO/OR red<3 amber 3-4.5 blue >4.5-<6.5 green ≥6.5; TC inverted green 1-<4 blue 4-<6.5 amber 6.5-<8 red ≥8); thin_dimensions UI metadata field for LOW bullet rendering; α formula change (TC removed from Overall, weights re-normalized to 37.5%/31.25%/31.25%); Stage 3 max_tokens 4096→8192 hotfix. Score tier labels: KILLED. |

**B9 scope redefinition (May 1, 2026):** Original B9 was "S9 — α formula + score tier labels (numerical only, no LLM)." α formula bundled into B8. Score tier labels killed in V4S26b (most ideas land 4.0-6.0; fixed tier labels would feel repetitive). B9 now redefined as the dedicated pre-B10a polish session — addresses the items deferred from B7+B8 plus the B2-reopened TC adjustment-math fix. Treat B9 as the last fix-window before B10a/B10b verification gates run. After B9 closes, the codebase is frozen for verification.

Each bundle has its own targeted verification runner (~15-25 cases, 30-40 min wall time). Full 34-run regression runs ONLY at B10. If a bundle's verification reveals issues, patch and run a smoke test (~4-6 cases targeting only the patched cases) instead of re-running the full bundle.

**Why bundles, not section-by-section ship:** Sections that touch the same prompt or route file would otherwise produce overlapping deploys with high merge-conflict risk and weak attribution if regressions appear. Bundles cleanly attribute "this deploy did these things" and produce one combined commit per surface.

**Bundle B1 closure record:**
Three rounds of verification across two days. Round 1 (initial 22-run B1): PARTIAL — schema clean, LOW handling clean, archetype A+B fired correctly, but P1-S1 profile inference failed, null Risk 3 failed (0/3 cases — coding gap overrode domain fit), templating ~89% (worse than baseline). Round 2 (post-three-fix patch): MIXED PASS — P1-S1 fixed via verbatim-quote rule + 3 inference patterns + worked example; null Risk 3 fixed via STEP 1 PROFILE-DOMAIN MATCH precondition (3/3); lead rotation hard-rule ate templating to 0%. New issues surfaced: Stage 2c parse failure (max_tokens 2500 truncation on 1 case), invalid `monetization` slot (model invented slot name in 2/21). Round 3 (4-case smoke test on follow-up patch): PASS 4/4 — max_tokens 4096 fixed parse failure, slot-name forbid line eliminated invented slots, P1-S1 stem-match detector cleared 5 false-positive flags from Round 2.

**B1 lessons that carry forward:**
- The two-strike rule held: B1 patch was strike two; if it had failed verification, architectural split (Stage 2c-summary + Stage 2c-risks) was prepared as the strike-three fallback. Don't keep tightening prompts when contamination is structural.
- Auto-detectors can have false positives (substring vs token match, regex too narrow). Don't trust detector flags blindly — read actual outputs, then fix detector or fix prompt as appropriate.
- Verification thresholds must be set BEFORE running, not adjusted post-hoc. Round 2 was honestly scored as MIXED PASS, not relabeled as PASS to ship.
- Worked examples in prompts work — the MAT3-tech-no-access summary opens almost verbatim from the prompt's worked correction example. Concrete > abstract for prompt instructions.

**Bundle B3 closure record:**
Two rounds of verification: 25-run v1 + 42-run v2 comprehensive (67 total runs). Round 1 (v1 runner, 25 cases): runner reported 19/25 PASS but the 6 "fails" were ALL test-design errors, not model errors — runner expected one Main Bottleneck enum value per case based on intuition, but the design's three relational cases (Alignment / Layered / Founder-fit per Section 4 lock execution-plan-v4-2.md lines 627-631) legitimately allow different MB values depending on Stage 2c's founder_fit firing. Round 2 (v2 runner, 42 cases comprehensive): runner reported 37/42 PASS but the 5 "fails" were again `validOutcomes` under-specification — model produced design-faithful Layered case outputs that the test's validOutcomes list didn't include. After mental correction of the validOutcomes coverage, actual model behavior was 42/42 design-faithful. Final state: schema clean (42/42), prose hygiene clean (42/42 no section-name leaks), opening variety holds (TC-first opening only fires when MB is Technical build), sparse handling clean (5/5 across Pro and Free pipelines), all 8 enum values fire, all 3 relational cases fire correctly, F2 closure achieved (2/3 distinct chips across MAT3 trio — substantial progress over audit baseline of 0/3 distinct headlines), MAT1 duration ordering preserved (senior < beginner upper bound). Strike count: 0 (no prompt patches needed).

Mid-bundle bug: B1 schema regression. After B3's frontend deploy (commit f80330b), live UI crashed with React error #31 — `<div> with keys {slot, archetype, text}`. Root cause: B1 had restructured failure_risks entries from plain strings to `{slot, archetype, text}` objects but three frontend consumers (EvaluationView Key Risks render, ComparisonView prepareComparisonData extractRisks, ComparisonView buildTradeoffsPayload extractRisks) had never been updated to extract `.text`. EvaluationView crashed; ComparisonView silently rendered empty risk strings AND fed empty risk strings to the tradeoffs Sonnet call. Fix: render `risk.text` in EvaluationView with backwards-compat for old string-form risks, add `.text` to the key fallback chain in both ComparisonView extractRisks functions. Patched and deployed within session. B1 verification missed this because B1 was verified entirely against runner JSON output — the runner doesn't render React.

**B3 lessons that carry forward:**
- **Apply Fundamentals Gate (Step 0 of Five Methodology Principles) BEFORE diagnosing test failures, not after.** Initial reading of the v1 25-case results misdiagnosed "Trust/credibility over-firing" as a prompt bug. Re-reading Section 4 lock revealed all 6 "failures" were design-faithful Founder-fit-case behavior. Cost: one near-prompt-patch that would have violated the TC Isolation Principle. The B1 lesson "don't trust detector flags blindly" applies recursively — the runner is itself a detector, and when its expected values don't match the locked design, the runner is wrong, not the prompt.
- **Test-design errors masquerade as model failures.** Multiple rounds of `validOutcomes` under-specification in the v2 runner because validOutcomes were derived from intuition-driven case predictions rather than systematically enumerated (Founder-fit + Alignment + Layered) for each idea+profile pair. Future test-runner design rule: for any case-aware verifier, declare ALL THREE relational cases as plausible validOutcomes unless the design explicitly forbids a case for that scenario.
- **Schema changes that cross frontend boundaries need downstream consumer audit.** B1 changed failure_risks from string array to object array. Three frontend consumers were missed because B1 was verified entirely against runner JSON (which doesn't render React). Future schema-shape changes: audit ALL consumers (frontend rendering, downstream Sonnet call inputs, data export) before shipping the schema change, not after a crash surfaces it.
- **Visual UI verification catches what runner verification can't.** B3's Path 3 decision (ship S4 frontend with B3 instead of waiting for B8) was the right call — the live UI exposed the B1 schema regression that runner-only verification had missed for over a day. Frontend rendering should ship with backend changes that produce user-visible output, not wait for a separate frontend bundle.
- **Comprehensive variance characterization beats single-sample inference.** v1's 2-sample ANTI-TC test couldn't distinguish "1/2 variance" from "systematic 50/50 split." v2's 5-sample ANTI-TC test revealed the actual distribution: 2 Layered-B + 2 Founder-fit + 1 Alignment-C, all converging on Trust/credibility as MB. Stage 2c's borderline domain-match call jitters across three readings, but Stage 3 produces design-faithful output regardless. The variance is upstream, not in B3.
- **Two-AI workflow paid off.** ChatGPT's review of the v2 runner design caught a real edge case (archetype E softening — empty mapping routes E to Layered, validOutcomes per test handle specifics). Without that review, archetype E firings would have miscategorized as Alignment with arbitrary enum picks. ChatGPT for criticism + diagnosis + strategic pushback; Claude for implementation. Neither alone produces the v2 we shipped.
- **Color taxonomy decisions deserve discussion before code.** Original Sage shade for Category maturation was emerald-green which collided with severity-coded color conditioning (green = good/easy in Difficulty pills). Iteration through fuchsia → forest → sage produced the locked muted gray-green that signals "categorical, not severity." Same for Stone (warm gray for Specification edge case). Pre-code color taxonomy locks save mid-implementation re-rendering.

Single round of verification, 17 runs / ~38 minutes wall time. One commit on main: f8fb7f8 (atomic 14-file modification + 2 deletions). Files modified: prompt-stage2b.js (Pro), prompt.js (Free), prompt-stage2c.js, prompt-stage3.js, prompt-tradeoffs.js, analyze-pro/route.js, save/route.js, [id]/route.js, re-evaluate/route.js, branch/route.js, delta/route.js, EvaluationView.js, ComparisonView.js, page.js. Files deleted: prompt-stage2.js (dead code from B1 architectural split — unified Stage 2 prompt retired with no remaining importers, verified via grep), run-stage1-stability.js (Phase 0.5 stability harness relocated to separate test-runners folder, not deleted from system). Final state: OR hook firing rate 100% (vs ~20% pre-B4 baseline), schema rename complete (zero confidence_level references in src/), Option Z MEDIUM compliance (zero forbidden generic-hedging patterns), zero confidence-about-idea reasoning, sparse cross-stage propagation 1/1 clean (LOW evidence_strength → Specification + N/A in Stage 2c + Stage 3), variance stability 6/6. Strike count: 0. MAT2-senior single soft-warning was a runner detector under-specification (B3 meta-lesson — gap-marker enumeration list missed `is unknown` construction), NOT a model issue; actual behavior 17/17 design-faithful. Manual UI verification confirmed HIGH evidence_strength produces no card render (asymmetric display rule working). **B4 lessons that carry forward:**
- **Atomic-bundle discipline on schema renames is non-negotiable.** ChatGPT's review during design ("if you're going to rename, do the full rename — half-rename is worse than the old naming") locked the all-or-nothing decision. Pre-commit grep gate caught the surface comprehensively (14 files vs the 4-file expectation in handoff doc). A partial rename would have been a B3-class regression.
- **Comprehensive surface audit BEFORE writing edits.** Each file containing the field name was cataloged + classified (field-reference vs natural-language use) before any code change. The catalog became the modification checklist; the grep gate verified completion.
- **Methodology gate applied prospectively, not retroactively.** All Five Principles cleared during design discussion before any prompt text was written. Step 2 (Contamination) was the most-debated — the locked design's explicit scoping language ("the field reports how well-grounded the evaluation can be, not an authority claim about outcomes") was the architectural protection against the rename creating new contamination paths.
- **Detector under-specification is the runner's own B3 meta-lesson.** MAT2-senior soft warning was the runner missing `is\s+unknown` from its gap-marker enumeration. Model produced a design-faithful concrete-gap reason. The B3 meta-lesson "the runner is itself a detector, and detectors can encode wrong expectations" applied to B4 immediately. Runner-side fix: add the missing pattern to SPECIFIC_GAP_MARKERS; no model patch needed.
- **Doc-drift is real and accumulates between sessions.** Master Reference V41 still described Stage 2b sampler hardening as pending B4 work after Phase 0.5 had closed it. V42 update propagated the corrections. Future bundles should expect doc-drift and audit it explicitly before treating handoff doc claims as ground truth.
- **Narrative Contract document was created post-B4 ship as the source-of-truth for cross-surface non-overlap.** V1 locks contracts for TC + Risk 1/2/3 + Summary + Main Bottleneck + Execution Reality. V2 adds OR explanation + Evidence Strength contracts. The contract document operationalizes the Step 0 Fundamentals Gate prospectively. B10b consumes the contract as ground truth for narrative coherence verification.

Streaming logs preserved every API response cleanly; rescore-b5.js replayed against existing streaming.json with corrected extractor + strengthened detector regexes (added "too non-specific" / "lacks [specific thing]" / "leaves [X] ambiguous" / "no defined [thing]" patterns surfaced from inspecting actual model outputs). T7 variance stability: 12/12 stable across reruns (3 sources × 4 runs each: MD1 LOW×4, BN1 LOW×4, NC4 MEDIUM×4) — no expanded-trigger bimodality. T8 Free pipeline parity: 2/2 (FREE-SP-DENTAL=LOW, FREE-NC4=HIGH).

Manual UI smoke test confirmed visible production behavior matches verified backend on both MD1 (LOW + Specification cascade + spec-gap-anchored summary + spec-gap-anchored failure_risks; no fabricated dental-SaaS-style content) and NC4 (MEDIUM + Buyer access + real duration/difficulty + substantive gym-owner SMB evaluation; counter-example for Trigger 3 holds in production).

Pre-commit grep gate (carried discipline from B3 + B4): five greps run before single combined commit, all expected hit counts matched — `FEWER THAN 20\|fewer than 20` (2 hits), `SPARSE INPUT RULE` (2 hits), `MO PACKET SPARSE-INPUT RULE` (1 hit, Pro only), `TRIGGER 2\|TRIGGER 3` (4 hits, 2 in each prompt), `Independent gym owners` (2 hits, counter-example anchor in both prompts).

Three honest extras flagged at design time and approved before code: (a) Trigger 3 counter-example clause is methodology-derived hardening beyond the locked plan's letter (consistent with B1's worked-example lesson); (b) cross-packet verification item 9 is approved Option A addition (ChatGPT pressure-test); (c) authored test case text where the locked plan named only case types. All three transparently logged in the methodology gate output rather than blurred into "strict plan compliance."

**B5 lessons that carry forward:**
- **Pre-flight runner check before full-suite spend.** When a runner makes shape assumptions about an API it can't introspect, validate against ONE real response before kicking off long runs. Cost of validation: one Sonnet call. Cost of getting it wrong: 50 minutes wall time + full API spend. The first SSE event from one warm-up case must be inspected against the runner's extractEvaluation() shape assumption before launching the full case bank. B5's runner had documented the shape assumption inline as a known risk — that wasn't enough. Validation must be active, not declared. New standing discipline alongside the pre-commit grep gate.
- **Test-case authoring needs design audit (B3 meta-lesson at the case-design layer).** MD-MULTI miss recurs the B3 + B4 meta-lesson at a new level: the case I authored had "also A also B also C" surface structure but a coherent connecting mechanism (freelancer tooling + AI personalization across features), so it didn't actually fit Trigger 2's contradictory-scope criterion. Future bundle test cases must be audited case-by-case against locked trigger criteria before adding to the bank, same way validOutcomes are now audited per B3. Concrete rule: for any new case added to a B-N runner, write one sentence stating which locked trigger condition the case is supposed to fire, and confirm the case's structural features match those criteria (not just surface phrasing).
- **Detector under-enumeration is a recurring discipline.** B5 rerun strengthened LOW_REASON_MARKERS and SPECIFIC_GAP_MARKERS regexes (added "too non-specific" / "lacks [specific thing]" / "leaves [X] ambiguous" / "remains ambiguous" / "no defined [thing]" / "input lacks [specific thing]"). Future detectors should enumerate from the Narrative Contract V[current] anchor predicates list, not intuition. Detector coverage is part of the Narrative Contract maintenance loop — when verification surfaces a design-faithful phrasing the detector missed, the regex is updated AND the contract's anchor predicates list expanded. Both directions: detectors derive from contract; contract expands from verification surfacings. B4's `is\s+unknown` miss + B5's "leaves [X] ambiguous" miss + B5's "too non-specific" miss are the same lesson firing three times.
- **Methodology gate's three-honest-extras pattern.** B5's design discussion explicitly flagged three methodology-derived additions beyond the strict plan letter (Trigger 3 counter-example, cross-packet item 9, authored test case text). Each was approved before code. This level of transparency about design extrapolations is now part of the Methodology gate output — future bundles should explicitly state design extrapolations vs. strict plan compliance, not blur the line.
- **Doc-drift audit happens turn 1 of every session.** Going into B5, the handoff doc said "first work item is V1→V2 NarrativeContract update." V2 already existed in the project. Drift was caught immediately and V2 was treated as canonical for B5 design discussion. Pattern carries forward: doc-drift audit happens turn 1, not later.
- **Narrative Contract V4 created (April 28, 2026, post-B6 ship):** Section 3.11 added — How-It-Compares user-facing landscape contract documenting B6's judgment-language enforcement check (P11-S1; verbatim 9-term forbidden list including inverted/softened/comparative forms after post-fix tightening) + sparse-input retrieval-quality rule (P11-S2; three triggers verbatim from B5 §3.10 + counter-example clause + Stage-1-specific provisional-framing template + Trigger 1 worked example with MANDATORY directive) + temporal anchoring (S9 carryover; relevance-gated factual date inclusion). Section 3.12 added — Stage 1 Profile-Blindness architectural discipline contract documenting the locked profile injection map (TC + Stage 2c + Stage 3 only; Stage 1 + Stage 2a + Stage 2b profile-blind by V4S28 B6 atomic three-strip route-level enforcement) + Free competitor-selection guidance partial-fix pattern as locked acceptable state for single-call architecture. Section 3.1 (TC) amended with B6-surfaced TC adjustment-math anchor-fixing observation + monitoring directive for B7–B9 + deferred-fix pointer to pre-B10a B2 session. Section 4 matrix expanded with How-It-Compares column + 3 new content-type rows (factual landscape mapping, market-accessibility judgment, timing-judgment phrasing). Pending sections in subsequent contract versions: V5 (Specificity gate / Haiku layer — B7), V6 (Score tier labels — B9; B8 is UI rendering, not a new contract), V7+ (post-V4S28).

Round 2 thresholds: T1 MAT1 trio Jaccard 0.88 (Phase 0 baseline 0.38; profile-strip working), T2 grep gate PASS (4 userProfile hits in expected locations only, 0 stale "and their profile" references), T3 sparse provisional framing 7/7 cases behave correctly, T4 judgment-language leak rate 1/25 = 4% (under locked <5% gate; pre-B6 audit baseline 8.8%), T5 zero timing-judgment leaks (positive-case dates unverified due to Serper retrieval), T6 internal_build buyer-anchored stability PASS (MAT1 trio 0/0/0 — pre-B6 audit had Beginner=0, Intermediate=1, Senior=1 founder-skill flip eliminated; IB-SMB clear-negative 0), T7 B5 regression PASS (MD1 LOW+cascade, NC4 NOT LOW, SP-DENTAL no MO_INFERRED_PRICING). **B6 lessons that carry forward:**
- **Path A scope expansion is the right move when contract-vs-code inconsistency surfaces during pre-implementation reads.** B6's plan was prompt-only; codereads found that route.js was injecting profile into Stage 2a in contradiction to NarrativeContract V3 §3.10. The fix expanded to atomic three-strip route-level cleanup as part of B6's commit. Discipline: doc-drift / contract-vs-code drift caught at pre-implementation read time gets folded into the bundle, not deferred — provided the discipline is contract-enforcement (not new design decisions).
- **Worked examples beat abstract directives for prompt-rule reliability.** B6's enforcement check went through three rounds of tightening. The version that finally held was the one with explicit GOOD/BAD side-by-side examples, not the one with the most precise abstract rules. Future prompt edits default to worked examples.
- **TC adjustment-math anchor-fixing surfaced.** MAT1 trio test produced final TC = 7/7/7 despite stated adjustments 0.0/-0.5/-1.0. Two failure modes possible: (a) stated adjustment not applied to score; (b) silent base inflation. Both are anchor-fixing patterns. Deferred to pre-B10a B2 session per Section 5 protect-from-spillover directive. Monitoring directive activated for B7–B9 (B8 verification surfaced no new TC observations).

**B7 lessons that carry forward:**
- **Locked design fired correctly first run — strike count 0.** When the design phase locks both the example matrix AND the calibration qualifier ("imaginability ≠ specificity") AND the boundary cases, the implementation has nothing to debate. B7's design phase was unusually thorough and the implementation needed no patches. Pattern: invest in design lock thoroughness for high-leverage gates.
- **Discriminating missing_elements emerged as a property of the locked enum, not an explicit instruction.** Haiku returns only genuinely absent slots per case (not always all three) because the locked example matrix demonstrates this implicitly. Future enum-based gates should rely on example matrix to teach behavior rather than adding explicit instructions about per-case selection.
- **Frontend cards UI sized to actual missing dimensions** (cardsToShow.length renders 2 vs 3 cards). Discipline: render only what the gate's payload demands, not always all slots.

**B8 lessons that carry forward:**
- **str_replace discipline on multi-block replacements.** When replacing a "logical section" that visually reads as one thing but is mechanically composed of multiple distinct code blocks (Overall card + Evidence Strength card + Metrics Card = visually one "evaluation block"), the old_str needs to cover ALL the blocks being deprecated, not just the first one. The duplicate-render bug came from treating "replace the Overall card" as the same operation as "replace the evaluation section" — they're not. Future bundles touching multi-block UI sections should write one large str_replace covering the full deprecated region, OR explicitly verify post-edit that no orphaned blocks remain via grep.
- **Pre-existing token limits surface under elaborate inputs.** Stage 3 at 4096 tokens worked fine for the 17-idea test suite (typical 500-1500 char inputs) and never hit the ceiling. The 4799-char IdeaLoop Core test idea exposed it. Latent caps in any LLM call need to be reviewed periodically as the input distribution evolves — and especially before any user testing with elaborate inputs.
- **MEDIUM trigger calibration is a real follow-up.** Live observation: Stage 2b fired MEDIUM on the IdeaLoop Core test idea (extremely well-specified — named buyer, trigger, friction, three monetization paths with dollar amounts, full tech stack, distribution strategy) with reason "buyer urgency is under-evidenced." That's a category error: confusing "input lacks specificity" (the actual MEDIUM trigger per Option Z rule) with "input is specified but external validation not yet proven" (different epistemic gap that should map to HIGH). NOT a B8 bug — B8 only changed how callouts render, not when they fire. But worth flagging to the rubric calibration session (post-V4S28 content audit).
- **Persistence pass-through is structurally clean post-Codex.** Worry about field-extraction regressions on schema additions is now obsolete given the single-developer model. The four-route audit confirmed evidence_strength flows through scoring_json as whole object on all paths. Future schema additions inside existing nested fields will work without persistence-route edits.
- **Haiku gate UX issues surfaced.** Live test surfaced gate UI disappearing mid-keystroke (suggestion vanishes when user starts typing in response to it), fire-up timing feeling off, and general reliability concerns. Bundle owner: "we need to make it near perfect because it can be very annoying and cost us many users." Treat the gate as a UX surface needing careful polish, not just functional correctness. Deferred to redefined B9 (pre-B10a polish) as highest-priority item.

=== IMPORTANT RULES (carried from V4S28 process learnings) ===
- Discuss approach before writing any code
- Run Five Methodology Principles gate (execution-plan.md line ~128) BEFORE shipping any prompt-level changes, not retroactively
- Two-strike rule on prompts: one fix attempt acceptable, second only if scope is tight, third = escalate to architectural separation
- Set verification thresholds explicitly BEFORE running tests
- Targeted verification per bundle, full 34-run regression only at B10
- Measure synthesis stability at both byte AND fuzzy Jaccard layers — byte alone undersells identity-level wins (carried from Phase 0.5)
- Canonical naming rule applies to Stage 1 competitor names (carried from Phase 0.5)
- Complete copy-paste-ready files only, not partial diffs
- "Go" or "go buddy" are the proceed signals
- Pre-flight runner check (B5 standing discipline): validate runner extraction shape against ONE warm-up case BEFORE launching full bank — declared assumptions are not enough, validation must be active
- Doc-vs-code drift audit during pre-implementation reads (B6 standing discipline): when codereads surface contract-vs-code inconsistencies (e.g., NarrativeContract says profile-blind but route injects profile), Path A fold-in is acceptable scope expansion when the discipline is contract-enforcement, not new design decisions
- Worked examples beat abstract directives for prompt-rule reliability (B6 standing discipline): default to GOOD/BAD side-by-side examples + concrete worked input/output before reaching for tighter abstract phrasing
- TC observation logging during B9 (active monitoring directive): any TC misbehavior surfaced during B9 polish work logged under the absorbed B2 surface in B9 itself. Pre-B10a session lands the structural fix.

=== NEXT SESSION (Bundle B9 continuation — TC adjustment-math fix focused session) ===

**B9 prompt-side closed (May 1, 2026).** Evidence Strength contract rewrite + Haiku gate UX overhaul both deployed, verified, and locked. Remaining B9 surfaces carry forward across subsequent focused sessions, in priority order:

**Next session (focused): TC adjustment-math fix (B2 absorbed into B9).**

The B6-surfaced bug: MAT1 trio test (same legal document automation idea × Beginner / Intermediate / Senior profiles) produced final TC = 7/7/7 despite stated adjustments 0.0 / -0.5 / -1.0. Two failure modes possible: (a) stated adjustment not applied to score; (b) silent base inflation. Both are anchor-fixing patterns where the model decides the final TC score independently and reverse-engineers base + adjustment to match.

**Likely structural fix (Q1 from prior session — needs design discussion before any prompt edit):** enforce explicit `base_score` + `adjustment_value` numeric JSON fields in the Stage TC output schema with `score = base_score + adjustment_value` arithmetic consistency check at parse time. This requires modifying `prompt-stage-tc.js` (locked-from-spillover during V4S28; the focused next session is the authorized window for this single edit).

**Pre-implementation methodology gate (Methodology Five Principles, mandatory before any prompt edit):**
- Locked verification thresholds before running any test runner (Principle 6)
- Worked GOOD/BAD examples beat abstract directives (B6 standing discipline)
- Two-strike rule on prompts: one fix attempt acceptable, second only if scope tight, third = escalate to architectural separation
- Pre-flight runner check (B5 standing discipline) before launching full bank
- Doc-vs-code drift audit during pre-implementation reads (B6 standing discipline)

**Verification scope for TC fix:** targeted runner with MAT1/MAT2/MAT3 trios verifying base_score + adjustment_value arithmetic consistency. Lock thresholds before running. Active monitoring directive that ran during B7-B9 surfaced no additional TC observations beyond the B6 finding — fix targets the single observed pattern.

**Open design questions to lock in next-session design phase before implementation:**
- Q1 (carried forward): TC adjustment-math fix shape — locked at `base_score + adjustment_value` arithmetic consistency or open to alternative architectures (e.g., remove the additive structure entirely and require single final score with rationale; or: keep base + adjustment but require model to commit to base BEFORE seeing adjustment context via two-step prompt structure)?
- Q2 (new, post-B9): Does TC fix change the Narrative Contract surface? §3.x covers TC scoring discipline — if the fix introduces base_score / adjustment_value as new locked predicates, V6 → V7 increment required. If purely structural arithmetic enforcement without changing TC's MUST-OWN/MUST-NOT-DRIFT-INTO predicates, V6 stays active.
- Q3 (new, post-B9): How aggressive should Free parity be? Free pipeline does TC inside the unified prompt. If fix requires base_score + adjustment_value JSON fields, Free's single-call architecture needs the same schema discipline — but Free's prompt is already dense and adding numeric arithmetic verification may strain attention budget.

**Subsequent B9 surfaces (queued, not next-session scope):**

1. **Free tier `prompt.js` thin_dimensions parity (B8 follow-up).** B8 added thin_dimensions to Pro Stage 2b. Free tier still doesn't emit it. Free LOW evaluations currently fall back to the EvaluationView's all-3-prompts default (workable, but not idea-specific). Mirror the Stage 2b instructions block in Free's unified prompt. Small surface — schema slot and instruction language already exist; just add to Free prompt and verify with 2-case smoke test.

2. **Tradeoffs/Delta input sanitation (B8 follow-up).** Locked design says "thin_dimensions is UI-only metadata, never seen by any LLM." analyze-pro/route.js enforces that for Stage 2c/Stage 3 via the assembly filter. But Tradeoffs and Delta are separate post-pipeline LLM calls that read the *persisted* evaluation, which (after restoration) does have thin_dimensions. The LLMs ignore the unrecognized field, so it's harmless in practice — but it's a soft violation of the invariant. Conservative fix: strip thin_dimensions at the Tradeoffs/Delta call sites before passing the evaluation object to those prompts. Grep gate verification.

3. **Manual UI smoke testing (mandatory pre-B10a discipline).** Paste 3-5 cases per evidence_strength state (HIGH well-formed, MEDIUM Option-Z gap, LOW sparse) and verify: C-2 layout renders correctly across all three states, MEDIUM/LOW callouts use correct copy and bullet rendering, color boundaries render correctly at edge cases (4.5 / 6.5 thresholds for MD/MO/OR; 4 / 6.5 / 8 thresholds for TC inverted), Score Guide popup triggers from ⓘ button. Test re-eval flow (when gate fires, when gate doesn't fire). Test compare flow with TC color logic. Test lineage view with new color boundaries.

4. **Archetype coverage test cases (test-case authoring, B10a prerequisite).** Across 177+ runs in B1-B7 verification, archetypes D and E never fired and C only fired twice. Three new idea+profile pairs needed before B10a's 34-run regression so the gate has full archetype coverage:
   - Archetype C: founder profile clearly missing domain credibility for high-trust idea (e.g., "AI for clinical decision support" + non-medical founder).
   - Archetype D: capital/runway gap (e.g., medical device hardware + bootstrap solo founder).
   - Archetype E: sales/conversion gap (e.g., enterprise B2B SaaS requiring outbound sales motion + technical-only founder).

**G1-LONG silent-failure diagnosis (HIGHER-PRIORITY follow-up, may interleave with TC session or be its own session):**

Stage 2b returns `level: null` on dense 1500+ word inputs even after max_tokens 4096 → 8192 bump applied during B9 v2. Root cause not yet diagnosed. Affects high-effort users — the segment whose trust matters most.

Diagnosis path:
- Log raw Stage 2b response text on long-input evaluations
- Verify whether evidence_strength is omitted in the model's JSON output OR lost during parse / route assembly
- Check whether JSON parser fallback silently returns partial evaluation
- Confirm whether the final UI handles missing evidence_strength safely (probably renders nothing)
- Add schema validation: if Stage 2b omits required evidence_strength, surface a controlled fallback (default to HIGH-silent + log incident), not null

This is not necessarily launch-blocking if rare, but it is a real quality issue and may surface during B10a regression suite if any 34-run cases have similar density.

**What B9 prompt-side closure does NOT change:**
- Stage 1 / 2a / 2c / 3 prompts beyond what shipped in prior bundles (locked).
- Score tier labels — KILLED. Don't reintroduce.
- α formula or scoring boundaries — locked in B8.
- C-2 layout structure — locked in B8.
- evidence_strength rendering callouts — locked in B8 (blue partnered framing for MEDIUM/LOW).
- NarrativeContract V6 — section-naming addition is optional/lightly-required prompt guidance, not a contract surface change. V6 stays active until TC fix or other surface triggers V7 increment.
