=== POST-B9 OPEN ITEMS (carry forward) ===

**B9 prompt-side closure findings (May 1, 2026, NEW — added with V47):**

- **Pricing dominance in MEDIUM callouts (UX watch item, not blocking).** B9 v2 verification surfaced pricing as 80% of MEDIUM callouts (12/15) on the test bank. Audit confirmed all 12/12 pricing-MEDIUMs fire on inputs with genuinely no pricing context — every individual fire is correctly identifying real absence (1 borderline case correctly distinguished product-pricing-feature from product-own-pricing). Dominance is structurally driven by the natural shape of casual input descriptions ("AI [thing] for [audience] that [does X]" — names buyer + workflow + feature but rarely monetization), not by model defect or templating. MEDIUM reasons are domain-aware in ~80% of cases (per-document/subscription/integration for legal; per-message/per-practice for dental; per-upload for creator tools, etc.) rather than templated.

  **Watch repeated-evaluation sessions specifically.** The fatigue pattern would emerge from a power user running 5+ ideas consecutively, not from one-off user tests. If aggregate fatigue surfaces post-launch, address at the UX layer (compact repeat callouts / inline pricing education / session-level dismissal) rather than suppressing valid prompt behavior. Prompt-layer pricing suppression would weaken Monetization Potential scoring honesty.

- **G1-LONG-1500W silent failure (HIGHER PRIORITY technical follow-up).** Stage 2b returns `level: null` on dense 1500+ word inputs even after max_tokens 4096 → 8192 bump applied during B9 v2. Root cause not yet diagnosed. Affects high-effort users — the segment whose trust matters most.

  Diagnosis path: log raw Stage 2b response on long inputs, verify whether evidence_strength is omitted in model output or lost during parse / route assembly, check whether JSON parser fallback silently returns partial evaluation, confirm whether final UI handles missing evidence_strength safely, add schema validation surfacing controlled fallback (default to HIGH-silent + log incident) instead of null.

  Tracked as separate technical follow-up — may be its own session or interleave with TC fix session. Not necessarily launch-blocking if rare, but real quality issue.

B9 v2 prompt rewrite locked input-actionable richness gaps as the only valid MEDIUM trigger; verified across 38 cases with 0% evidence-side leakage rate (T4 gate).

With α formula change, TC is no longer in Overall — but the comparison Scores screen still presents it as a peer of MD/MO/OR with the Overall computed below. Cleanest fix mirrors EvaluationView: small "EXECUTION CONTEXT · NOT IN OVERALL" divider before TC row.

With α change, TC doesn't affect Overall anymore — so highlighting "weakest: TC" suggests fixing something that won't move the score. Worth excluding TC from this calculation, or clarifying the framing.

**CLOSED — V8.1 Haiku gate calibration revisit (May 4, 2026, single session, three iterations):** Originally surfaced during B9 thin_dimensions hygiene smoke testing (May 4, 2026). The 100+ word restaurant manager input + multiple other rich-but-multi-product cases were getting gated despite naming target_user + workflows + features. Calibration revisit closed via three iterations:

- **v1 (commit b52afc0):** System-wide enum rename (workflow → use_case, core_feature → mechanism, target_user retained) + 14-row PASS-first matrix + Option A pass criterion (slot presence dominates, multi-product not a fail condition) + word-count thresholds dropped + generic-benefit-language guardrail. Seven files modified atomically. Verification (86-call regression bank): 50/61 = 82% pass rate, Block A bug-trigger 5/5 ✓, Block B floor 8/8 ✓, Block D collapse 1/6 ✗ (recalibration miss). Iteration discipline: paused, re-discussed design lock per B7 method.

- **v2 (commit f80b500, REVERTED):** Prompt-level fix attempt — added COLLAPSE PRINCIPLE block + BUYER-CATEGORY PRINCIPLE block + 5 new matrix rows + the line "When in doubt, prefer PASS." Verification: catastrophic floor collapse, Block B 8/8 → 0/8. Inputs like "an app that helps people", "tool to make work easier", "I want to disrupt the legaltech industry with AI" all PASSed. Reverted via `git revert f80b500` within minutes of verification. **Lesson captured**: meta-instructions about decision posture ("prefer PASS") far more powerful than instructions about specific cases — any future calibration nudge should isolate posture-level prompt directives carefully.

- **v3 (current production):** v1 prompt unchanged + code-layer rescue layer in `keywords.js`. Three helper functions added (`hasConcreteForToVerbObject` / `isGenericBenefitPhrase` / `shouldOverrideCollapseFalseReject`) plus `buildRescueKeywords` for synthesizing keywords on rescue. Five conditions ALL required for override: (1) Haiku returned `specificity_insufficient: true` / (2) `missing_elements` contains `use_case` OR `mechanism` / (3) `missing_elements` does NOT contain `target_user` (HARD condition) / (4) input matches `for [target_user] to [verb] [object]` regex with concrete noun-object / (5) action phrase NOT in 15-entry generic-benefit blocklist. Pattern coverage scoped narrow: `for X to verb-object` only — NOT `for X that/which verb-object`. Verification: 58/61 = 95% pass rate, Block A 5/5 ✓, Block B floor 8/8 ✓ (zero regression), Block D collapse 6/6 ✓ (fully closed). Three documented residual false-rejects (G2/G11/K1 — `for X that` patterns or multi-buyer cases the conservative-scope rescue intentionally does not match) tracked for B10b observation.

**Architectural lessons captured (V8.1):** (1) Calibration vs exception handling are different layers — pattern-level model bugs get code-layer deterministic fixes, NOT prompt-layer broad teaching. (2) Cost asymmetry principle locked — false-rejects (recoverable UX friction) strictly preferable to false-passes (trust-destroying nonsense + token burn). (3) Methodology Principle 6 held throughout — locked thresholds before runner ran each iteration; no goalpost-moving. NarrativeContract §3.13 V8.1 subsection documents the rescue layer architecture + slot rename + verification baseline. NarrativeContract V7-LOCKED → V8-LOCKED at session close.

**LOW PRIORITY — V8.1 Haiku gate latency optimization (candidate prompt-slim follow-up):** v3 verification showed median ~960ms / p95 ~2400ms (vs B7 baseline 1138ms / 952ms median). Same prompt as v1 — rescue layer adds zero latency. Accepted under V8.1 Lock-F (richer prompt semantics worth the cost; gate runs once per Analyze click; below user-perceptual "stuck" threshold). Per B7 design this is intentionally a generic calibration anchor. If jarring, two design questions surface: should the example rotate (small array of examples randomly chosen on render) or should it match the user's input domain (harder — would require Haiku to suggest a domain-matched example, adding latency/complexity).
